Converted to the **tenant-merge read**: the vertical's defaults + THAT tenant's `tenant_override` rows — mirroring the sweep's own `_fanout_companies` (the honest "what fires for this tenant"). Defaults order first; the no-tenant path byte-identical (non-regressive by construction). Read shape gains `scope` + `tenant_id` (the labeling fields). **No schema change; migration head stays r118.** **THE SELECTOR (all reuse):** `TenantPicker` (existing component, `verticalFilter`'d to this vertical) + `GET /admin/tenants/lookup` (existing endpoint) in a "Viewing" header control; selection lives in the URL (`?tenant=<slug>`, restored via the lookup on load — linkable/refreshable). Null selection = today's view, byte-identical (no tenant_id sent anywhere). **VISUAL WITNESS (local preview, the closing scene of the T-2.1c gap):** default = 3 vertical rows + the picker; select testco → **the T-2.1b witness marker-task APPEARS, pilled "Test Vault Co", with its schedule chip + functional (live-capable) Dry-run badge** — the exact row the page couldn't show; `?tenant=testco` survives a full reload; a temporary testco `tenant_override` page fixture → the cards RECONTEXTUALIZED to it + the banner rendered (then fixture removed); deselect → param cleared, defaults return, marker gone. **Tests:** backend 5 (non-regression pin / merge / tenant isolation / no-override graceful / labeling fields) + frontend 7 (pills, tenant-titled Add-task POSTs tenant_override+tenant_id, no-tenant sends NO tenant fields) = 12 new. **Gates:** backend MoC suites 29/29 (post-cleanup — see below) + the earlier 23/23 catalog-neighbor run; frontend FULL vitest **4216 passed (303 files)**; tsc clean; build clean 5.21s. **Dev-DB pollution incident (caught + cleaned + filed):** running the witness-marker seed for the visual witness left a `*/15` cron trigger on dev — the local backend's sweep fired it dry-run every 15 min (4 runs — T-2.1a proof-of-life, ironically) AND it broke 3 `test_moc_schedule_sweep` tests that assert on GLOBAL sweep counts. - **2026-07-06 — Canvas↔Runtime Bridge T-2.1c: THE LIVE TOGGLE (promote a trigger from the MoC, with an evidence-backed confirm).** `191c705` (3/3 the confirm) + `be3ccb7` (2/3 badge + toggle) + `cd7f915` (1/3 data path). Promoting a trigger no longer requires a raw PATCH — the T-1b trigger chip carries the live state and the promotion flow, with a beat of gravity where it matters. **THE DATA PATH (the small backend piece):** `resolve_task` exposes per-trigger `is_live` (the badge state) + `workflow.is_mirror` — the §6 compiled-vs-mirror discriminator, keyed off the SAME field the sweep's `_resolve_go_live` uses (`mirrored_from_workflow_id`), with a test asserting the equivalence (`is_mirror` ⇔ `_resolve_go_live`) so **the UI and the guard can never disagree**; `list_schedule_runs` gains an optional `trigger_id` filter (the confirm's latest-preview fetch, limit=1). No schema change; migration head stays r118. **THE BADGE (kind-distinct, unmistakable):** schedule chips carry Live vs Dry-run. **Live = solid terracotta fill + pulse dot** (consequential, attention-carrying, not alarmist); **Dry-run = calm muted outline**. The badge shows the EFFECTIVE state: a MIRROR task's trigger shows Dry-run (+ lock) even if is_live is set — the sweep would force dry-run, so the badge never lies. Display-only in the table cell; interactive in the panel. **THE TOGGLE (scoped to real capability):** a COMPILED-task trigger gets a functional toggle; a MIRROR-task trigger's toggle is DISABLED with the §6 reason ("Mirror tasks can't go live yet — the workflow runs on its own schedule (§6 double-fire guard)") — never a control that appears to work but silently stays dry. **THE CONFIRM (the evidence-backed beat):** flipping TO live opens a confirmation that SHOWS WHAT THE TASK WILL ACTUALLY DO, read from its LATEST DRY-RUN PREVIEW — the engine's own "would execute X" records rendered in mono with the previewed-at timestamp, plus "This will fire REAL effects on schedule (<schedule>)". A NEVER-previewed task gets the explicit amber fallback ("This task hasn't previewed yet… consider letting it run dry-run first") — a nudge to the dry-run-first workflow, NEVER a fabricated effect. Flipping BACK to dry-run is IMMEDIATE, no confirm — the safe direction is friction-free, a live fire can always be killed fast. **VISUAL WITNESS (local preview, admin tree, shell-witness@example.com, all five by-eye checks):** (1) compiled-task trigger → Dry-run badge + functional toggle; (2) toggle → the confirm showed the REAL preview content (`action:record_marker` + "Previewed 7/6/2026, 7:47 AM"); (3) Go Live → badge flipped to the solid **● LIVE** pill AND DB `is_live=True` verified by query; one tap back → Dry-run, NO dialog, DB `is_live=False` (reversibility, on screen); (4) never-previewed task → the amber no-preview fallback (and Cancel left `is_live=False`); (5) mirror task → toggle `disabled=true` + lock + the §6 title, click opens nothing. Witness fixtures were dev-DB-local (3 vertical_default visual fixtures + a fabricated preview run — fabricated deliberately so the sweep never ran against a vertical_default task on the 2089-tenant dev DB; schedules set 03:47, out-of-window). **Tests:** backend 4 (incl. the UI-guard consistency assertion) + frontend 11 in `TriggerLive.test.tsx` = 15 new. **Neighbors:** backend MoC+trigger+sweep+live suites 46/46; frontend FULL vitest **4212 passed (302 files)** incl. the T-1b chip tests; tsc clean; build clean 5.25s. **OUT OF SCOPE:** promoting real operational tasks (operator's call); mirror-task live-scheduling (§6 dedupe arc — here the toggle just honestly reflects can't-go-live); event triggers (T-2.2); the escalation hook. COMMITTED LOCALLY — operator reviews the PREVIEW before push.

- **2026-07-01 — Canvas↔Runtime Bridge T-2.1b-WITNESS: THE FIRST REAL SCHEDULED FIRE (a benign marker, witnessed on the real DB).** `d2e929c` (3/3 assembly) + `27803ad` (2/3 seed) + `5a6e337` (1/3 substrate). T-2.1b built the is_live mechanism (inert). THIS is the deliberate first crossing — the platform taking a REAL (harmless) autonomous scheduled action: a clock, not a human, running a compiled workflow that writes a real row. **THE BENIGN-BUT-REAL SUBSTRATE:** a dedicated `moc_witness_marker` table (migration **r118**, reversible) + a `record_marker` action handler. The marker is REAL (a persisted, attributable row → this is what proves a live fire end-to-end, not another dry-run) yet BENIGN (nothing reads it → deletable; no invoice, no notification, no external call). **`log_vault_item` was rejected** as the marker: its INSERT silently swallows (`vault_items.vault_id` is NOT NULL without a default → confirmed the catalogued silent-INSERT bug), so it writes nothing. `_handle_record_marker` deliberately does NOT swallow — a failed write fails the step LOUDLY (the T-2.1b "recorded loudly" invariant). Dry-run **auto-suppresses** record_marker (the engine's deny-by-default gate at the step executor — no new suppression code), so pre-promotion the run only previews *"would execute action:record_marker"* and writes NO row. **THE SEED** (`seed_moc_witness_marker.py`): a COMPILED (not mirror → passes the §6 compiled-only guard) template whose only effect is a marker; a task scoped **tenant_override → testco** so the sweep's `_fanout_companies` fires for EXACTLY ONE company (the T-2.1a death-spiral was a `vertical_default` fan-out — deliberately avoided); a **cron `*/15`** schedule (witnessable within a sweep cycle, not a once-a-day wait); shipping **is_live=FALSE** (unpromoted → dry-run until the operator promotes). Idempotent + **PRESERVES an operator promotion** across re-runs (never resets is_live). Refuses on ENVIRONMENT=production. **THE LOCAL WITNESS (real dev DB, real sweep `check_moc_task_schedules`, then cleaned up):** UNPROMOTED → 1 dry-run schedule-run ("would execute action:record_marker"), **0 marker rows**; PROMOTE (`is_live=True`) → **1 real marker row — the first autonomous real effect** — fully attributable (company_id + run_id + moc_task_trigger_id + fired_at + note), LIVE run `completed`; fire AGAIN same window → **still 1** (exactly-once idempotency); DE-PROMOTE (`is_live=False`) → next window fires **dry-run**, still 1 marker (**the OFF switch works** — a live task pulls back to dry-run). **STOP resolutions:** (1) benign-but-real → a dedicated table (dispatch-endorsed) since NO benign existing handler exists; (2) witnessable soon → cron `*/15` + odd-time in tests; (3) promote/de-promote clean via the T-2.1b `patch_trigger` API. **Assembly 8/8** (asserting on the REAL marker row — stronger than the T-2.1b `_execute_action` spy). **Neighbors:** engine 20/21 (the 1 is the SAME pre-existing stale `actionRegistry.ts` path), T-2.1b assembly + T-2.1a sweep + triggers 31/31, bridge+compiler+dry-run 17/17. Migration r118 reversible (up/down/up). Engine change is ADDITIVE — one dispatch branch + one handler + one compiler set-entry; touches no existing handler's behavior; `canvas_validator` (frontend-mirrored) left untouched. **⚠ CRITICAL — THE STAGING WITNESS IS GATED ON A PUSH:** T-2.1b is UNPUSHED (local-only, ahead of origin/main), so r117 + the is_live mechanism aren't on staging yet. The staging fire (the milestone the dispatch describes) requires the operator to push T-2.1b + this arc (deploying r117 + r118), then on staging: `python -m scripts.seed_moc_witness_marker` → watch `/schedule-runs` (dry-run) → `PATCH /triggers/{id} is_live=true` → watch the real marker row → de-promote. Steps are in the seed docstring. **OUT OF SCOPE:** promoting any REAL operational task (operator's later call, now de-risked by this witness); mirror-task live-scheduling (§6 dedupe arc); the UI "Live" toggle (T-2.1c); event triggers (T-2.2). **The benign crossing is proven locally; the platform's first REAL autonomous action is ready to witness on staging the moment the operator pushes + promotes.** COMMITTED LOCALLY — operator reviews before push.

- **2026-07-01 — Canvas↔Runtime Bridge T-2.1b: is_live PROMOTION (the first REAL scheduled fire — mechanism, witnessed benign, left OFF).** `3e20c71` (4/4 assembly) + `b192db4` (3/4 promotion API) + `718c9dc` (2/4 the go_live conversion + guard) + `3a39bc6` (1/4 migration r117). The platform's FIRST autonomous real action — a clock, not a human, running a workflow with a real effect — mechanism built + proven on a controlled benign target, then left OFF (no real task promoted on staging; the real go-live is the operator's deliberate flip). **THE go_live SINGLE-SOURCE CONVERSION (the safety-critical change):** T-2.1a's sweep fired `go_live = _SWEEP_GO_LIVE` (constant False); T-2.1b converts that ONE source to `_resolve_go_live(trig, template)` — live requires BOTH, both explicit: (1) the trigger is PROMOTED (`is_live`) AND (2) its task resolves to a COMPILED (single-owner) workflow. **A MIRROR task NEVER fires live** (§6 double-fire hazard — re-point runs the independently-scheduled runtime source) — it fires DRY-RUN with a logged reason even when is_live=True. So the DEFAULT is dry-run (unpromoted OR mirror); a real effect requires the deliberate promotion of a compiled task. `_resolve_go_live` is the SOLE derivation — no scattered convenience True; a promoted trigger cannot fire live through any other path. The compiled-vs-mirror discriminator is `template.mirrored_from_workflow_id` (the SAME one `resolve_executable_workflow` uses — authoritative + consistent). **Migration r117** (reversible): `moc_task_trigger.is_live BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE` — every existing trigger starts unpromoted. **Promotion API:** `patch_trigger` + `PATCH /triggers/{id}` gain `is_live` (a one-field extension); the UI toggle is T-2.1c. **STOP #1 finding (surfaced):** NO benign SEEDED compiled-task exists — the demo compiled-tasks (Invoice & Statement Run, Legacy Order) do REAL invoices/statements/notifications; the 18 backfill tasks are all MIRRORS (§6-guarded). So the mechanism is proven on a CONTROLLED BENIGN task IN-TEST, and the build promotes NOTHING real on staging — **the operator's first real staging fire is their deliberate choice** (recommend seeding a benign test-task for a safe staging witness before firing a real-invoice task). **Assembly test 8/8** (effect boundary = a spy on `_execute_action`, the handler that would create a real invoice — runs iff live): is_live default FALSE; **promoted COMPILED → LIVE (the effect handler IS invoked — the real effect happens); promoted MIRROR → DRY-RUN (the §6 guard holds — handler NOT invoked, dry-run run exists) even with is_live=True;** unpromoted → dry-run; **LIVE fires EXACTLY ONCE** (re-keyed idempotency holds for live); a **LIVE failure recorded LOUDLY** (status=failed + error_message); `_resolve_go_live` single-source unit; patch_trigger sets is_live. **Pre-build STOP checks (all resolved by investigation):** (a) NO benign seeded compiled-task → surfaced + controlled-benign witness (above); (b) compiled-vs-mirror discriminator CLEAN (`mirrored_from_workflow_id`); (c) go_live single-source PRESERVED (`_resolve_go_live`). **Neighbors:** T-2.1a sweep 7/7 + trigger tests 16/16 (the go_live conversion didn't break the dry-run path), spine 11/11 + dry-run 6/6, workflow_engine 28/29 (the 1 is the SAME PRE-EXISTING stale `actionRegistry.ts` path, unrelated); **`workflow_scheduler` + `execute_template` + the engine UNMODIFIED.** **Four natural commits.** **OUT OF SCOPE (later):** mirror-task live-scheduling (the §6 dedupe — its own arc); the UI toggle (T-2.1c); event triggers (T-2.2); leaving real tasks live (operator's call); auto-escalation of failed live runs (still loud-record). **The mechanism exists + is proven; the platform can now take a real autonomous scheduled action the moment the operator promotes a compiled trigger.** COMMITTED LOCALLY — operator reviews before push.

- **2026-07-01 — Canvas↔Runtime Bridge T-2.1a: THE DRY-RUN SCHEDULE SWEEP (the first live caller — dry-run only).** `99689e8` (3/3 assembly) + `158104f` (2/3 the sweep) + `b0b4fac` (1/3 the compile cache) + `6e9cd6c` (the T-2.1 scoping investigation). A parallel sweep that fires MoC schedule-triggers through the T-2.0b dry-run-safe engine — every fire DRY-RUN (no is_live, no real effects). Proves the sweep works safely for ALL triggers before any live fire. **THE SWEEP** (`schedule_sweep.check_moc_task_schedules`): a PARALLEL sweep (iterates `moc_task_trigger` schedule rows — a different entity than the workflow scheduler's loop) registered as a **SEPARATE isolated APScheduler job** (its own try/except) — the existing `workflow_scheduler` is **UNMODIFIED** (its matcher helpers reused read-only; the isolation requirement held). **THE SAFETY INVARIANT:** `go_live` has ONE source — the constant `_SWEEP_GO_LIVE = False`. Every fire is dry-run; NO code path fires live. T-2.1b replaces the constant with `trigger.is_live`. Until then nothing the sweep fires can touch a real effect → safe for ALL triggers (mirror + compiled; the §6 double-fire is a live-only concern, moot in dry-run). **Correctness (inherited + one fix):** IDEMPOTENCY re-keyed on the TRIGGER (compiled workflows are ephemeral) via `WorkflowRun.trigger_context` — a 6pm task fires ONCE across the N ticks in its window (no new table); **TIMEZONE:** time_of_day evaluated TENANT-LOCAL (the fix for the scheduler's UTC bug — a tenant-local `now` passed to the reused matcher); cron already tz-aware; CATCH-UP: the 15-min window naturally SKIPS a backlog; fan-out per scope (platform→all, vertical_default→per-company-in-vertical, tenant_override→the one tenant); time_after_event deferred (funeral_case-only upstream). **THE COMPILE CACHE (§7, migration r116):** `workflow_templates.compiled_workflow_id` + `compiled_version` — a draft template compiles ONCE per version + reuses it (the sweep would otherwise recompile every tick → bloat); company-agnostic (company_id=None; the RUN scopes the company); mirrors re-point (no cache). **OBSERVABILITY:** `list_schedule_runs` + `GET /api/platform/admin/moc/schedule-runs` — recent fires + their "would do X" records, so an operator validates dry-run fires before T-2.1b promotes any to live (fidelity caveat noted). **Assembly test 7/7:** due-fire dry-run (effect handler NEVER invoked — spy uncalled — the T-2.0b guarantee holds through the sweep); idempotent across ticks; **tz** (fires at tenant 6pm=22:05 UTC, not 18:05 UTC); catch-up skips backlog; **cache** (two-day fires COMPILE ONCE, both runs reuse the cached workflow); observability visible; fan-out scoping (pure fn). Tests are tenant_override-scoped (deterministic against the **2089-tenant dev DB** — a vertical_default fire fans to every manufacturing tenant; **debugging note:** an early vertical_default test + zombie pytest processes fired ~8000 runs into the polluted dev DB, a death spiral cleaned + rewritten to tenant_override). **Neighbors:** spine 11/11 + dry-run 6/6 (cache didn't regress), workflow_engine 28/29 (the 1 is the SAME PRE-EXISTING stale `actionRegistry.ts` path, unrelated), legacy_order end-to-end (the live `start_run` path) green; `workflow_scheduler` UNMODIFIED. **Migration r116** (compile cache; reversible). **Three natural commits + the investigation.** **OUT OF SCOPE (T-2.1b+):** is_live + any LIVE fire (T-2.1b — compiled-tasks-only, the first real fire, its own witnessed phase); mirror-task live-scheduling (§6 dedupe, deferred); the UI run-log VIEW (rides the /schedule-runs endpoint — a thin follow-up / T-2.1c); event triggers (T-2.2). COMMITTED LOCALLY — operator reviews before push.

- **2026-07-01 — Canvas↔Runtime Bridge T-2.0b: ENGINE DRY-RUN MODE (the safety net — HARD PREREQUISITE for T-2.1).** `b4bb2ee` (3/3 assembly) + `a040c87` (2/3 two-flag precedence) + `39fc576` (1/3 executor dry-run). The safety read (T-2.0-safety-read canon) found T-2.0 had NO dry-run default — only a gate that REFUSES; above the gate was LIVE with no safe middle. T-2.0b builds the safe middle: the engine runs DRY-RUN by default when executing, NO step producing a real effect, unless explicitly promoted. **INTERCEPTION AT THE STEP-EXECUTOR (safe-by-default for future step types):** `dry_run` threads `start_run → _drive_run → _execute_step` and is **HONORED at the BOTTOM** — in `_execute_step`, when dry_run, ONLY `condition` runs its real (pure, read-only) handler so branching stays real; EVERY other step type (action/output/notification/ai_prompt/send_document + any unknown/new one — **deny-by-default**) is **SUPPRESSED and RECORDED** (`_dry_run_suppressed_output`: "would execute X"), never executed; `input` pauses suppressed so the run stays terminal + observable. No real effect (DB write, external call, send) can occur because the effect-producing handler is never invoked. A newly-added effectful node is dry-run-safe automatically. **Pre-build STOP checks (all resolved by investigation, honored):** (1) `dry_run` threads cleanly (no resistance); (2) **`guard_write` is agent-scoped** (`BaseAgent.self.dry_run`) → does NOT compose into the engine's functional executor → the engine gets a FRESH executor-level mode (matches the operator's executor-level choice — surfaced, not a conflict); (3) reads-vs-writes: `_evaluate_condition`/`resolve_variables` are pure/read-only → the safe design (suppress the whole effectful step) is unambiguous. **RESIDUAL FIDELITY CAVEAT (flagged, not a safety hole):** suppressing a whole effectful step also suppresses its reads, so a downstream `condition` branching on a suppressed step's OUTPUT would branch on synthetic data — narrow (conditions branch on trigger/input data, real in dry-run), documented; safety preserved regardless. **THE TWO-FLAG PRECEDENCE MODEL** (`execute_template`, replacing `allow_live_execution`): `allow_run` (default False, the tripwire — must be True to run at all) + `go_live` (default False, DRY vs LIVE). **The ONLY path to real effects is allow_run=True AND go_live=True, both explicit;** allow_run=False ALWAYS refuses (go_live ignored — the two-bool nonsense-state guard); (allow_run=True, go_live omitted) → RUNS DRY (the safe default). A caller wired without go_live cannot fire a real invoice. **Assembly test 6/6, proven AT THE BOTTOM (not "the flag was accepted"):** (1) THE DELIVERABLE — default-when-running is dry-run, the effect handler (`_execute_action`) is NEVER invoked (spy stays uncalled → no real effect) + step records "would" (the exact thing T-2.0's proof #4 did NOT establish); (2) explicit live invokes the handler; (3) gate holds; (4) nonsense state refuses (handler never reached); (5) dry-run observable (completes + `__dry_run__` marker + real trace); (6) branching holds in dry-run (condition runs, effects suppressed). Effect probe = a monkeypatch spy on `_execute_action` (invocation boundary IS the effect boundary; `log_vault_item` was unusable — `vault_items.vault_id` NOT NULL without default, pre-existing). **LIVE PROVEN UNCHANGED (the central-path requirement):** `test_workflow_engine` 28/29 (the 1 failure is the SAME PRE-EXISTING stale `actionRegistry.ts` path assertion, unrelated), `test_legacy_order_end_to_end` + `test_workflow_review_focus` (real live `start_run` paths) green, spine 11/11 — the dry_run branch is skipped when False, live is identical. **No migration** (execution-path, `output_data.__dry_run__` marker, no schema). **Three natural commits.** **OUT OF SCOPE (T-2.1+):** any live CALLER (schedule sweep/event match — T-2.0b makes them SAFE to build, doesn't build them); the failure→escalation polling hook + the engine run-level-failure fix; the workflow approval gate; the `moc_task_trigger.is_live` trigger-promotion UI (T-2.1); rich conditions. **T-2.1 is now safe to build** — a live caller defaults to dry-run unless it passes go_live=True. COMMITTED LOCALLY — operator reviews before push.

- **2026-07-01 — Canvas↔Runtime Bridge T-2.0: THE SPINE (the compiler + mirror re-point), proven by a canvas that RUNS.** `d2d911b` (3/3 assembly tests) + `5601739` (2/3 re-point + gated execution) + `caf10aa` (1/3 the compiler) + `b9de727` (the T-2 scoping investigation). The foundation of the deferred execution arc — turn an inert canvas into something the runtime engine RUNS, via two mechanisms. NO firing, NO schedule sweep, NO event emission (T-2.1/T-2.2). **Pre-build investigate-and-surface (the STOP discipline, honored):** three seams verified first-hand before building; **two genuine snags surfaced → operator decided.** (a) The compile subset is **linear-only in practice, not "linear+conditional"** — the canvas has no canonical true/false edge convention + the only conditional canvas in-tree is 3-way+parallel (out of subset), so binary-conditional compile is speculative with no fixture → **operator chose linear-only, reject the rest** (conditional = T-2.0b). (b) The **workflow engine has NO dry-run mode** — `start_run` takes no `dry_run`; ~10 side-effecting handlers commit unconditionally; the agent `guard_write` is a separate path. "Dry-run by default" is net-new threading through the SHARED engine path → **operator chose SPLIT: T-2.0 ships the spine with execution GATED OFF (test-only callers), engine dry-run = T-2.0b** before any trigger points at it. **MECHANISM 1 — RE-POINT** (`execution_bridge.repoint_mirror`/`resolve_executable_workflow`): a mirror's `mirrored_from_workflow_id` → run the runtime SOURCE (no compile — retires the backfill debt as the provenance column was designed for); dangling/not-a-mirror reject loudly. **MECHANISM 2 — COMPILE** (`canvas_compiler.compile_canvas_to_workflow`): a LINEAR canvas → workflows+workflow_steps (start/end dropped; engine step types pass through; action-type nodes nest; step_key=node.id preserves variable refs; config verbatim; **trigger_type FORCED to "manual" → scheduler-inert**). Rejects parallel/condition/decision/branch/wait/fork LOUDLY with a node-specific error — **never a silent partial-compile** (dropping a branch runs a DIFFERENT workflow). **SAFETY SURFACE:** execution gated (`execute_template(allow_live_execution=False)` → `ExecutionGatedError`); **loud failure incl. an ENGINE LIMITATION found + compensated** — `_drive_run` does NOT stop on a step failure (`_execute_step` records the failed step but the loop continues and `_complete_run` OVERWRITES the run to 'completed' — run-level failure is swallowed by the engine today), so `_surface_run_failures` re-marks the run 'failed' + logs loudly if any step failed (the engine's run-level fix + the escalation hook are flagged for T-2.1). **Assembly test 11/11 (the deliverable — a canvas RUNS):** re-point runs the source; a linear canvas compiles + runs + reflects its real shape (2 steps in order) + preserves config; parallel/condition/fork REJECTED loudly; execution GATED off by default; not-a-mirror/dangling/run-failure/missing-template all loud. Benign `show_confirmation` steps prove EXECUTION without real side-effects. **Neighbors:** moc_workflow_mirrors 5/5, workflow_templates_phase4 48/48, workflow_engine 28/29 (the 1 failure is PRE-EXISTING — a stale `actionRegistry.ts` frontend-path assertion, unrelated to this additive-only change); `app.main` imports clean. (`test_workflow_scheduler_scheduled_dispatch` hangs at test #7 in isolation — a pre-existing environmental hang; doesn't import this code.) **No migration** (compile-on-demand; row-accumulation + a compiled-workflow cache are T-2.0b concerns). **Three natural commits + the investigation.** **OUT OF SCOPE (T-2.1/T-2.2):** the engine dry-run mode (T-2.0b, before any trigger fires); schedule sweep + event emission; parallel-node lowering (rejected cleanly, not solved); the failure→escalation polling hook + the engine run-level failure fix; the workflow approval gate. - **2026-06-23 — Frontend-version deploy-gate: close the witnessed false-green hole (+ MoC Phase 1.1 closed green).** `4bbca00`. **Phase 1.1 itself is DONE** — the `moc` job greened on run `28181598593` against a confirmed-fresh frontend (`index-Bg61TeC7.js`, `admin-nav-maps` present) + healthy backend `482225d`; all 6 tests pass incl. the two front-door tests (inferred from single-step job-green). This commit fixes the infra hole that hid the failure. **The hole:** the CI deploy-gate polled only the backend `/api/health` commit; the frontend is a SEPARATE Railway service whose build can lag or FAIL silently — a stale/failed frontend was invisible, producing this arc's false reds (and capable of a false green that reaches the demo). **The fix (4 surfaces):** (1) `vite.config.ts` `emit-version-json` plugin writes `dist/version.json` with `RAILWAY_GIT_COMMIT_SHA` in `closeBundle` — fires ONLY after a successful `vite build`, so since `npm run build` = `tsc -b && vite build`, a build-break leaves version.json stale (freshness IS the bundle's freshness); (2) `Dockerfile` `ARG/ENV RAILWAY_GIT_COMMIT_SHA` so the plugin gets the SHA at Railway build time; (3) `.github/scripts/deploy-gate.sh` — shared gate polling backend `/api/health` AND (optional) frontend `/version.json`, requiring **N consecutive healthy matches** (`--settle 2`, absorbing the backend's >5-min post-deploy stabilization that caused the 502-at-login false reds) before proceeding; **fail-closed** with surface-specific `::error::` messages ("FRONTEND never reached {sha} — build FAILED or LAGGED") — the old "commit null → proceed after 5 min" bootstrap fallback that ran tests against broken services is REMOVED; (4) all 3 jobs rewired to call it — runtime-editor + moc backend+frontend, claude-api backend-only (API tests). **Witnessed locally:** `npm run build` (full tree, standing rule) EXIT 0 + `dist/version.json` carries the SHA; gate backend-pass path PASS against live staging (2 consecutive); gate fail-closed path TIMEOUT + distinct FRONTEND message (version.json genuinely absent pre-deploy). YAML valid (3 jobs). **First real witness of the frontend-poll is the next push** — the frontend builds + serves `version.json={thissha}`, the gate requires it before tests run. nginx already serves `/version.json` as a file (`try_files $uri`, no-store). **One Railway assumption to confirm on first deploy:** that Railway passes `RAILWAY_GIT_COMMIT_SHA` as a Docker build ARG — if not, version.json writes "unknown" → gate fails-closed (loud), never false-green. UNCOMMITTED.

- **2026-06-09 — 1a hotfix #3: two prompt-artifact bugs in the authoring seed (render-time).** After hotfix #2 made `execute()` failures graceful (200, not 500), run `27212934581` (`743d8eb`) showed all 3 generate shapes SKIP (unproven, not a 500) and the graceful body NAMED the cause: `MissingVariableError: Missing required variables: properties, required, type`. Two latent bugs in `seed_workflow_authoring_prompt.py`, both render-time (prompt seeded fine — never a seed-missing/key issue): **(1)** `_VARIABLE_SCHEMA` was stored as a JSON-Schema object `{"type":"object","properties":{...},"required":[...]}`, but the platform's shape is a FLAT `{var_name: {type, required, description}}` map (per `prompt_renderer._required_variables`) — so the renderer read the schema's top-level meta-keys (type/properties/required) as phantom required vars. **(2)** masked behind #1: a literal `{{binding: deceased_name}}` placeholder in the system prompt (from an f-string `{{{{…}}}}`) that Jinja tried to EVALUATE at render → `TemplateSyntaxError`. **Fixes:** flat variable_schema; binding placeholder changed to a non-Jinja `"BIND:<entity>.<field>"` token; `+ test_seeded_prompt_renders_with_the_service_variables` runs validate_variables + render against the seeded artifact with the service's exact variables (the gap mocked-execute tests left — now 10/10). Local: render OK (no `{{` leak), re-seed → v2 (idempotent content-diff bump). On redeploy the canonical seed runner bumps staging v1→v2 with the fixed artifact → execute validates + renders → model runs → **the real validator-PASS verdict across 3 shapes** (key confirmed set). **Verdict still PENDING the redeploy run.** UNCOMMITTED.

- **2026-06-09 — 1a hotfix #2: route response-model rejected the guard's own output → 500.** The 3-shape staging e2e (`471e056`, run `27211685021`) RAN and caught a real bug: nl-entities PASSED, all 3 generate shapes FAILED with HTTP 500 (pre-model). Verdict-integrity machinery worked as designed — fix #3 (non-OK = fault) failed loudly instead of green-by-skip. Root cause: `routes/workflow_authoring.py::GenerateResponse.ai_execution_id` was `str` (non-optional), but the hotfix-#1 guard returns `ai_execution_id=None` on a raised `execute()` → `GenerateResponse(**result)` Pydantic ValidationError → 500. The guard worked; the response model choked on the guard's output, defeating it on EVERY failure mode. Service-level unit tests missed it (tested the service in isolation, never the route's response_model against the service's output). **Fix:** `ai_execution_id: str | None = None` (+ defaulted `ai_latency_ms`/`model_used`); `+ test_generate_response_model_accepts_the_guard_error_shape` pins the route/service shape-agreement (9/9). **Verdict still PENDING** — generation quality UNPROVEN (model hasn't generated). Post-deploy, `execute()` failures become a graceful 200 whose `validation_error` NAMES the cause (Prompt/Route/AllModelsFailed); with the prompt re-seeded each deploy + key set, the likely outcome is execute succeeds → real validator-PASS across 3 shapes. No 500 either way. Local: backend 9/9. UNCOMMITTED.

- **2026-06-09 — Builder AI Assistant Phase 1a hotfix: /generate no longer 500s.** Post-1a (`512e102`) staging verdict: the `workflow-authoring` Claude-API e2e never ran in CI (the only Playwright job globs `tests/e2e/runtime-editor/` exclusively; my spec is top-level), and a direct staging probe of `POST /api/v1/workflow-authoring/generate` returned **HTTP 500** (fast, pre-model). Root cause: `generate_workflow_canvas` had **no try/except around `intelligence_service.execute()`** — and `execute()` *raises* on a missing prompt (`PromptNotFoundError`), missing model route, missing variable, or model-call failure (`AllModelsFailedError`, e.g. unset `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`). Only the *returned-failed-result* path was handled; the *raised* path propagated → 500, contradicting the "never raises" contract. **Fixes (4):** (1) `service.py` — wrap `execute()` in try/except; any raise → graceful `{valid:False, ai_status:"error", validation_error:"generation could not run (<Type>: <msg>)"}`. (2) `test_workflow_authoring.py` — new `test_gate_handles_execute_raising` (now 8/8). (3) `workflow-authoring.spec.ts` — skip-guard tightened: a non-OK HTTP is now a real fault (`expect(res.ok())`), only `ai_status not in (success, fallback_used)` skips (unconfigured AI = graceful 200 with `ai_status="error"`); fixed the login body `identifier`→`email` (staging rejects `identifier` with 422); **broadened from one workflow to three shapes that stress different validator rules** — flat linear chain (no branching), multi-branch cascade (decision + converge), dense parallel graph (split/join fan-out/fan-in) — each asserts validator-PASS + a lenient shape-specific structural check. all-PASS = real green; one pass ≠ "reliably." (4) `playwright-staging.yml` — new discrete `Run Playwright Claude-API e2e specs` step (`if: !cancelled()`) so the spec runs even when the routinely-red runtime-editor specs fail. **NO QUALITY VERDICT EXISTS YET.** The verdict only comes into being after the validator-PASS assertion actually fires green across all three shapes — which requires (ops, not code) `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` set on staging + the authoring prompt seeded. Without the key the e2e SKIPS = "unproven," NOT "passed." A post-push green is the verdict ONLY if the assertion ran. Local gates (no model): backend 8/8, tsc clean, YAML valid. UNCOMMITTED.

Empty real `rows` array → renders empty (repeater renderer surfaces config.empty_state). `config.max_rows` cap honored on real rows. (5) `AtomRenderer.test.tsx` extended (~210 LOC of new tests) — 7 new WB-6 real-iteration scenarios: per_row iterates real rows with row count assertion; empty_state surfaces on empty array; max_rows cap; single_summary via summary context; single_record via row[0] context; per-row spread renders row field values directly. (6) Binding picker substrate at `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/widget-builder/binding-picker/` — 7 new files, ~1,050 LOC: `useBindingPicker.ts` (~80 LOC) parallel-fetches savedViews + entityTypes via existing service; component-local memoization via React state + ordered-fetch cancellation via `latestFetchId` ref (no session cache — preserves saved-view canon "live-queried every time"); manual refresh tick for post-create-saved-view re-fetch. `useBindingPreview.ts` (~140 LOC) — debounced 200ms (matches WB-4a auto-save) executeSavedView + resolveBinding composition. Returns `{kind: idle|loading|value|empty|error}` discriminated union with description string ("First row preview; X total rows" etc.). Cancels in-flight on input change. `SavedViewPicker.tsx` (~145 LOC) — filtered Popover combobox with search input + `ARRAY_SHAPED_MODES` filter (list/table/kanban/cards/calendar) when `requiresArrayShape=true` (per Lock 6a — auto-applied for repeater_atom callers); per-row chrome: title + entity_type badge + presentation mode badge. `FieldPathPicker.tsx` (~145 LOC) — cascading Popover combobox; disabled until entity_type is set; populates from `EntityTypeMetadata.available_fields` (`field_name` + `display_name` + `field_type`); free-text fallback via FF-6 `TextFieldUncontrolled` for nested paths + vault_item metadata_json (Risk 1 mitigation per Area 10). `IterationModePicker.tsx` (~100 LOC) — auto-inferred from atom_type + presentation_mode per Area 5 Lock 6d: repeater_atom → per_row locked; chart/stat view → single_summary locked; list/table/kanban/cards/calendar + non-repeater → single_record default with operator toggle to single_summary; `inferIterationMode` helper exported. Locked variants render as inline read-only badge ("per row · auto"); non-locked renders as Select. `BindingPreviewTooltip.tsx` (~90 LOC) — in-inspector preview-value display (rendered inline rather than hover-tooltip per discovery: inline more discoverable for authoring; operator-validation-sensitive). `BindingPreviewTooltipDisplay` exported separately for state-driven tests. `BindingPicker.tsx` (~210 LOC) — unified composing control: reads BindingRef from inspector layer, composes SavedViewPicker + FieldPathPicker + IterationModePicker + BindingPreviewTooltip into single cascading authoring surface; emits next BindingRef on change with binding_type forced to 'field_path'; preserves field_path when switching between views of the SAME entity_type (UX continuity); clears field_path when entity_type differs; loading + error states surfaced. (7) Binding-picker tests (~700 LOC across 6 files, 41 tests) — SavedViewPicker (7), FieldPathPicker (6), IterationModePicker (8 — inferIterationMode + IterationModePicker UI), BindingPreviewTooltipDisplay (5 — display states only), useBindingPicker (3 — fetch + error + refresh), useBindingPreview (5 — idle / per_row / empty / single_summary / error), BindingPicker (7 — full composing flow). (8) Inspector integration at `AtomInspectorDispatch.tsx` (~80 LOC modified) — 5 inspectors wired with BindingPicker: ValueDisplayInspector (value binding), ButtonInspector (label binding; action_ref stays WB-7 placeholder), ImageInspector (src binding), ConditionalContainerInspector (condition binding), RepeaterAtomInspector (rows binding). New `onUpdateBinding(atomId, propName, binding|null)` prop on AtomInspectorDispatchProps; new `bindingForProp(propName)` + `makeBindingChangeHandler(propName)` inner helpers route between BindingPicker (when wired) + BindingPlaceholderField (test-only fallback). New `useAtomBindingUpdater(blob, setDraft)` hook (~60 LOC) — mutates `atom.binding_refs[propName]` + `bindings_catalog` atomically; for repeater_atom + propName='rows', ALSO sets `atom.config.binding_id` to mirror (structural-validator agreement); clears binding_refs entry when binding=null; orphaned catalog entries left in place (validation gates catch at Publish). The 4-level visibility model + cross-tenant masking + permissions cascade all transparent at the consumer layer — the existing 8 saved-view endpoints + entity-types catalog answered every WB-6 need with zero schema or service-layer change. **iteration_mode auto-inference edge case:** when a saved-view's presentation_mode changes after a widget binds to it (operator edits the view to chart-mode after binding to list-mode), the binding's iteration_mode does NOT auto-update — the picker's `inferIterationMode` runs at render time only; binding stays as-stored. Validator catches mismatches at next Publish. The canvas-root flex chrome accordingly maps to `direction` + `gap_token`; full alignment control surfaces in WB-4b inspector work where the schema can be revisited. (2) The useWidgetAutoSave hook's "draft sync to lastServerSnapshot" needed two effects, not one — the initial null→populated transition (after GET completes) is distinct from the slug-change reset; without the second effect, the page stayed in the loading state forever because draft was initialized from null and never re-hydrated. **Flex-stack drop-zone edge cases handled:** empty canvas surfaces explicit dashed drop affordance; empty container shows ContainerDropTarget overlay; cursor position determines insertion index via `over.data.kind === "insertion"` vs `"container"` discriminator; clamped indices in insertAtomAt (`Math.max(0, Math.min(index, oldChildren.length))`). **Auto-save race conditions handled:** AbortController on each save attempt; rapid edits coalesce via timer reset; flush() clears pending timer before calling doSave; superseded inflight saves abort without flipping status. **@dnd-kit DndContext for widget builder coexists cleanly with FF-2's DndContext:** different parent surfaces (WidgetBuilderPage's DndContext is mounted under Studio routes; FocusBuilderPage's is under `/builder/focuses` — only one mounted at a time per route). **WB-4a does NOT ship (per build-prompt scope discipline):** 9 atom-kind-specific inspector controls → WB-4b; composition validation inline surfacing → WB-4b; widget definition list view → WB-4b; saved-view binding picker → WB-6; button action authoring → WB-7; variant authoring UI → WB-8; per-atom theme/styling override → WB-7; live preview against real saved-view data → WB-5. **Constraints honored:** FF-series + F-series substrate unchanged; - **2026-05-21 — Sub-arc WB-2 shipped (uncommitted) — ComposedWidget runtime renderer.** Second widget-builder sub-arc per investigation `5771fc0`. Establishes the runtime interpretation layer (hybrid Model C per Area 5) that renders WB-1 composition_blob into the same DOM substrate hand-coded widgets render into. **FRONTEND-ONLY.** No backend changes, no Alembic migrations; migration head unchanged at `r105_widget_definitions_composition_extension`. Pre-flight: HEAD verified `7eb1280` (WB-1 Foundation). **What WB-2 ships:** (1) `ComposedWidget` React component (`frontend/src/lib/widget-builder/runtime/ComposedWidget.tsx`) — single component (NOT codegen) that parses CompositionBlob via WB-1's `parseCompositionBlob` codec + recursively dispatches; emits `<div data-composed-widget-root="true" data-widget-id="...">` as the hit-testable inner-div per Area 6 dual-wrapping lock + hover-fix d9ffd90 finding. (2) `AtomRenderer` (`./AtomRenderer.tsx`) — recursive atom-type dispatcher with variant filtering (visible_in_variants check against optional `variantId` prop) + binding resolution + exhaustive switch over 8 atom_types; ConditionalContainerRenderer wrapped via `registerComponent` (the only Phase 1 atom with children gets its own `data-component-name="wb-conditional-container-atom"` boundary), other 7 leaf atoms render inside ComposedWidget's hit-test inner-div. (3) 8 placeholder atom renderers (`./atoms/index.tsx`) — semantic-HTML-only Phase 1 UI (text_label `<span>`, value_display `<span>`, icon `<span>[icon:name]`, status_badge `<span>[badge]`, divider `<hr>`, button `<button type="button">` with no-op onClick, image `<span>[image]`, conditional_container `<div>{children}</div>`); all emit `data-atom-type` + `data-atom-id` for editor + integration test introspection. WB-3 swaps placeholder UI for real typography/theme/icon UI without breaking the dispatch contract. (4) `resolveBinding` helper (`./resolveBinding.ts`) — Phase 1 placeholder: literal → `literal_value`; field_path → `[bound:${field_path}]` placeholder string. WB-6 makes this real saved-view resolution; consumer interface stable. (5) "composed" widget renderer registration (`./register.tsx`) — side-effect import wired in `App.tsx` at app bootstrap, mirroring the established `widgets/foundation/register.ts` pattern (SavedViewWidget noted as the canonical config-driven precedent). Adapter bridges `WidgetRendererProps` to `ComposedWidget`, extracting `composition_blob` from `config.composition_blob` per dispatch convention. (6) `dispatchWidgetDefinition` helper (`./dispatch.ts`) — single additive entry-point that branches: composition_blob populated → "composed" renderer + stashes blob into config.composition_blob; composition_blob null → existing `getWidgetRenderer(widget_id)` path UNCHANGED. The helper does NOT mutate caller's config object (test-asserted). Existing callers of `getWidgetRenderer` (Canvas, BottomSheet, StackRail, StackExpandedOverlay, PulsePiece, PinnedSection) continue to work unchanged — hand-coded widget render path explicitly UNCHANGED. **Tests shipped:** 6 new test files / 61 new test cases — `resolveBinding.test.ts` (7), `atoms/atoms.test.tsx` (18), `AtomRenderer.test.tsx` (16), `ComposedWidget.test.tsx` (7), `dispatch.test.tsx` (5 — including ComposedWidget-inside-PlacedWidgetCore-shaped-DOM integration assertion verifying FF substrate composition correctness + hand-coded regression preservation), `source-shape.test.ts` (6 source-shape gates per DECISIONS.md entry 31 pattern — catches future reverts of load-bearing structural elements: `data-composed-widget-root`, `parseCompositionBlob(` invocation, registerComponent wrap on conditional_container, exhaustive 8-case switch, 8 atom-renderer exports, both dispatch branches). **Architectural notes:** (a) ComposedWidget receives a flexible `ComposedWidgetInput` shape (widget_id + composition_blob) rather than the full `components/widgets/types.ts::WidgetDefinition` interface — the existing TS interface doesn't yet declare composition_blob, and the loose-typed boundary lets WB-3+ catalog work proceed without breaking WB-2. (b) The "composed" registration adapter pulls composition_blob from `config.composition_blob` because `WidgetRendererProps` doesn't have a widget-definition-level axis — `dispatchWidgetDefinition` stashes it there at dispatch time. This keeps existing canvas registry shape untouched. (c) Defensive throws on null composition_blob (dispatch contract violation), missing root_atom_id, and unknown atom_type (TS exhaustive guard). Dangling child / binding_id refs render placeholder (`[unbound:id]`) rather than crash — production load must remain resilient even when backend semantic validator drifts. (d) 2-level nesting cap (Q-5) trusted from WB-1 validator at write time; runtime renderer doesn't re-enforce. - **2026-05-21 — Resize live preview fix arc shipped (uncommitted) — Option A commit-on-tick; first FF-series Playwright spec exercising pointer-driven gesture; FF-6 inspector live W/H updates as Option A side effect.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `57d7667` per process canon (resize-live-preview investigation). Single combined dispatch against locks in `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-live-preview.md`. **Production fix**: added `parseResizeHandleId` branch to `handleDragMove` in `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` parallel-shape to the existing `handleDragEnd` resize branch (lines 822-880); branch RETURNS before the snap-line early-exit (resize does not participate in snap-to-alignment per investigation §5). **Architectural refinement during build — drag-start placement snapshot**: investigation locked "parallel-shape to handleDragEnd resize branch" but Option A as literally specified would compound the resize across ticks because @dnd-kit's `e.delta` is CUMULATIVE-from-drag-start while the resize branch reads `currentPlacement` from state — after the first tick, state has already moved; tick 2 would add cumulative delta (50px) to the already-moved width (265px) → 315px instead of correct 290px. Surfaced by JSDOM mid-drag test failing with final width 365 (5 ticks compounded) vs expected 290. **Fix**: new `resizeInitialPlacementRef: useRef<{ placementId, x, y, width, height } | null>` captured at `handleDragStart` when the active drag id matches a resize-handle shape; BOTH the new `handleDragMove` resize branch AND the existing `handleDragEnd` resize branch read `currentPlacement` from this snapshot instead of from placement state; ref cleared on dragEnd + dragCancel. Idempotency preserved: handleDragEnd's redundant final commit fires the same cumulative delta against the same snapshot → same `computeResizeCommit` output → no-op merge in the FF-7 functional setter. This refinement was NOT pre-locked in the investigation; surfaced during JSDOM verification and resolved within the fix arc per the investigation's §8 architectural-surprise canon ("handleDragEnd + Option-A handleDragMove would have identical bodies" was true at the time of writing the investigation but false after the first tick mutates state — a load-bearing detail the investigation missed). **Aspect-ratio Shift detection: NOT implemented.** The existing handleDragEnd resize branch does NOT preserve aspect ratio via Shift; `computeResizeCommit` has no such parameter; the FocusBuilderPage.tsx:505-506 canonical comment explicitly notes "@dnd-kit's DragMoveEvent does NOT expose the activator's current modifier state mid-gesture." Implementing aspect-ratio preservation would require (a) extending `computeResizeCommit` (DO NOT MODIFY per scope discipline), (b) tracking shiftKeyHeldRef document-level listener parallel to altKeyHeldRef. Out of scope for this arc; flagged for future operator-validation arc if needed. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied (BOTH paths)**: (a) **JSDOM** — stashed `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` production change, ran new mid-drag test → FAILED at `expect(midWidth1).toBeGreaterThan(initialWidth)` with `expected 240 to be greater than 240` (pre-fix handleDragMove ignores resize handles; width unchanged across ticks); restored → PASSED with midWidth1=265, midWidth2=290, finalWidth=290. (b) **Playwright + source-shape gate** — stashed production change, ran source-shape regression gate (which reads FocusBuilderPage.tsx as a string via Node fs + asserts `parseResizeHandleId`/`computeResizeCommit`/`updateWidget` regex matches inside handleDragMove body) → FAILED at `expect(body).toMatch(/parseResizeHandleId/)`; restored → PASSED. The Playwright inline-fixture spec exercises generic chromium pointer events but does NOT exercise production handleDragMove (inline fixture has its own JS pointer-event wiring); the source-shape gate is the LOAD-BEARING pre-fix-fails / post-fix-passes assertion per the hover-fix arc d9ffd90 precedent. Documented candidly in the spec docstring. **Playwright integration path chosen: option (d) — inline fixture + page.setContent + source-shape regression gate**. Same rationale as hover-fix d9ffd90: seeded staging fixture for free-form Focus templates has not landed (existing `focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts` is `.skip`'d); options (a) staging URL + (b) dev-server + (c) unskip+extend FF-7 spec all blocked on the same seed dependency. Inline fixture reproduces the operator-observable SHAPE (positioned widget whose dimensions update during pointer-drag on a child handle); production-path regression guard is the source-shape gate. Spec lives at `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform-resize-preview.spec.ts` (~190 LOC). **Test surface**: 1 new mid-drag JSDOM test at `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` ("FF-4 — resize via e handle previews live per drag-move tick (mid-drag width grows)" ~115 LOC); 1 new source-shape regression gate at `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` ("FF-4 source-shape gate — handleDragMove contains a parseResizeHandleId branch" ~25 LOC); 1 new Playwright spec at `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform-resize-preview.spec.ts` (~190 LOC inline-fixture + 1 test "widget dimensions update during drag (not only at release)" with 4 assertions: preBBox baseline, midDragBBox1 > preBBox, midDragBBox2 > midDragBBox1, finalBBox ≈ midDragBBox2 within 2px). All 4 pre-existing FF-4 JSDOM tests continue passing (e-handle width commit, w-handle x-adjust, canvas-bound clamp Q-14, min-dimensions clamp Q-13) — confirms handleDragEnd's drag-start-snapshot read preserves all existing FF-4 contracts. **Idempotency verified**: 4 pre-existing FF-4 tests pass with the refactored handleDragEnd that now reads from `resizeInitialPlacementRef` instead of live placement state. handleDragEnd + handleDragMove final outputs identical because both compute against the same snapshot with the same cumulative delta. **FF-6 W/H inspector inputs update LIVE during resize as intended side effect of Option A** — investigation §8 surprise (4) flagged this as the architectural inconsistency Option A introduces (resize is MORE live than drag-to-move because drag-to-move uses CSS transform). Preserved intentionally pending operator validation; symmetry arc may either upgrade drag-to-move to commit-on-tick (giving up GPU translate optimization) OR downgrade resize to ghost-state pattern. **FF-6 X/Y inspector inputs stay non-live during drag-to-move** (intentional asymmetry preserved — FF-3 drag-to-move continues to use CSS transform; only resize is commit-on-tick). **All FF-1 through FF-7 behaviors continue working**: 55/55 FocusBuilderPage tests pass; 21/21 FreeFormPlacedWidget tests pass; full focus-builder vitest suite (29 test files, ~350 tests) green. **Snap-during-resize still deferred** per investigation §5. **Gate cascade**: `npx tsc -b` clean; vitest run full suite 3163/3165 pass with 1 pre-existing flaky failure (`Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx > preview-card chrome preset updates live when chrome pill clicked` — verified pre-existing on `57d7667` HEAD via `git stash` + standalone re-run; test passes in isolation; flakiness is test-ordering-sensitive and unrelated to this arc) + 1 todo; lint baseline preserved (zero new errors on touched files; pre-existing 584-error baseline unchanged); `npm run build` clean in 5.32s; Playwright `focus-builder-freeform-resize-preview` 1/1 passing in 1.1s. **Bundle delta**: pre-arc `6,123.28 kB` → post-arc `6,124.30 kB`. Absolute delta **+1.02 kB**; percentage delta **+0.017%**. Cost-of-fix proportional to ~75 LOC of new production code (drag-start ref + capture in handleDragStart + resize branch in handleDragMove + handleDragEnd ref-read refactor). **Migration head unchanged**: `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **Files modified**: `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/focus-builder/FocusBuilderPage.tsx` (~95 LOC delta — useRef declaration + handleDragStart capture branch + handleDragMove resize branch + handleDragEnd snapshot read + handleDragCancel ref clear), `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (+140 LOC — mid-drag live-preview test + source-shape regression gate), `STATE.md` (this entry). **Files added**: `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform-resize-preview.spec.ts` (~190 LOC inline-fixture spec). **Files NOT touched per scope discipline**: `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx` (confirmed innocent), `computeResizeCommit.ts` (pure helper), `useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` (functional setter already supports rapid calls), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` (no aspect-ratio Shift parameter wiring), the investigation doc (read-only reference), CLAUDE.md / PLATFORM_ARCHITECTURE.md / DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md / DECISIONS.md / BRIDGEABLE_MASTER.md / FUNERAL_HOME_VERTICAL.md / VISION.md (canon docs), the 114 unstaged screenshot deletions. **Architectural surprises during build**: (1) the drag-start-snapshot compounding issue — investigation's "parallel-shape to handleDragEnd" was a true but incomplete locking statement; the symmetry holds before mid-drag state mutation but breaks after. The refinement was within the scope of Option A but not pre-locked. - **2026-05-20 (later) — Read-only investigation arc produced: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-live-preview.md` filed (uncommitted); locks live-resize-preview fix shape; fix arc pending dispatch.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `d9ffd90` per process canon (hover-state staging-regression fix). Zero production / test code touched. Investigation triggered by operator staging verification of `d9ffd90`: hover-state working; UUID leak fix holding; relatedTarget edge case working. New finding surfaced — **resize doesn't preview during drag** (widget stays at original dimensions throughout drag; only updates to final dimensions at pointer-release). FF-3 drag-to-move DOES preview live; FF-4 drag-resize does NOT. **Architectural root cause locked**: `@dnd-kit/core`'s `useDraggable` returns a `transform: {x, y}` object that updates per pointer-move tick. FF-3 at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:199-201` consumes this transform as `style.transform: translate3d(...)` on the widget wrapper — the OS compositor GPU-translates the widget under the cursor; no state mutation; no rowsDraft churn; preview is FREE. FF-4 resize handles at `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx:150-157` call useDraggable but DO NOT destructure `transform` (and couldn't usefully consume it anyway — translating an 8×8 handle doesn't resize the parent widget). The widget's dimensions at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:247-248` are state-controlled via `placement.width` / `placement.height`; the ONLY way to change them visually is to commit a state mutation. The page-level `handleDragMove` at `FocusBuilderPage.tsx:1114-1182` early-exits for resize-handle drag ids (line 1117-1118 — `parseFreeFormDraggableId` returns null for `<placement-uuid>-handle-<position>` shape; no resize branch exists). At drag-end, `handleDragEnd:836-880` commits via `computeResizeCommit` + `updateWidget`. Net: handles drag (their own translate3d), widget dimensions never mutate during drag, no preview. **Fundamental asymmetry**: @dnd-kit's transform model handles POSITION cheaply via CSS translate; DIMENSIONS require state-mediated rendering through `placement.width`/`.height` → React re-render. **Four fix options enumerated + audited**: (A) commit-on-tick — add `parseResizeHandleId` branch in handleDragMove; dispatch `updateWidget` per tick; lowest implementation cost (~30 LOC production); composes cleanly with FF-7 functional setter race-fix (was designed for rapid successive calls); 60Hz re-render of all canvas widgets but with stable React keys + bounded canvas size (≤20 widgets) within frame budget; Q-26 debounced save absorbs network cost via coalescing; FF-6 inspector inputs update LIVE during drag (W/H counter up in real time). (B) canvas-level ghost state — page tracks `resizeGhost`; rendering reads ghost or placement; cleaner re-render scope but requires prop drilling through canvas → layer → widget; FF-6 inputs would NOT update during drag (breaks bidirectional sync). (C) CSS inline width/height delta during drag — useDndMonitor inside FreeFormPlacedWidget; cheapest re-render footprint; requires duplicating per-handle math at render path; FF-6 inputs do not update. (D) per-widget local ghost — each widget owns its own monitor subscription; clean separation; N subscriptions for N widgets (negligible at typical scale); FF-6 inputs do not update. **Locked recommendation: Option A**. Reasoning: (1) symmetry with FF-6 W/H inputs — when operator types W=400 in inspector, widget updates instantly via FF-1 bidirectional sync; resize gesture is the cursor-driven equivalent; Option A preserves this mental model. (2) lowest implementation surface — ~30 LOC new branch parallel to existing handleDragEnd resize branch. (3) composes cleanly with FF-7 functional setter discipline (race-fix designed for this workload). (4) Q-26 debounced save absorbs network cost. (5) re-render concern theoretical not measured; React.memo on placement props is surgical mitigation if needed. (6) doesn't entangle snap-during-resize question (deferred per §5). **Architectural inconsistency Option A introduces**: FF-6 inputs WOULD update live during resize, but FF-6 inputs do NOT update live during drag-to-move (because FF-3 uses CSS translate not state). One gesture updates inputs live; the other doesn't. Flagged for operator hand-validation post-fix; not blocking. **Snap-to-alignment during resize: DEFERRED** to follow-up investigation. Q-11 locked snap for drag-to-move; `computeSnapAdjustment` takes a `dragPosition` for BBox-vs-edges math; resize-snap requires per-edge math (which edge is moving snaps to a neighbor's edge), meaningfully different. Operator signal hasn't surfaced "resize should snap" yet. Adding now expands fix arc from ~165 LOC to ~400+ LOC for unvalidated need. **Test substrate strategy**: JSDOM coverage via @dnd-kit's KeyboardSensor (Tab to focus handle, Space to grab, Arrow keys to delta-emit, Space to commit; assert rowsDraft mutates per-tick) — Q-40 canon applies. JSDOM pointer-event coverage remains unreliable (known gap per Q-40 generalization extended by hover-fix arc). Playwright spec required: hover widget → grab SE handle → mouse.down + mouse.move to intermediate position + assert bbox during gesture + mouse.up + assert final bbox. Source-shape regression gate per hover-fix precedent: unit test reads FocusBuilderPage.tsx source-string + asserts `parseResizeHandleId` appears inside handleDragMove body; catches accidental removal during future refactors. **Implementation surface estimate**: ~35 production LOC + ~50 JSDOM test LOC + ~80 Playwright LOC = ~165 LOC. **Fix arc dispatch shape: single combined arc** — production branch + JSDOM keyboard test + source-shape gate + Playwright spec; one commit; one staging verification cycle. Operator hand-validation: drag each of 8 handle positions; widget should glide dimension-wise throughout drag; release dimensions match. **Architectural surprises**: (1) `useDraggable` returns `transform` that's wholly unused for resize handles — handles still receive attributes/listeners/setNodeRef for the drag-end commit path; the visual transform is dropped (correctly — handles are edge-anchored, shouldn't translate). Surfaces the asymmetry: @dnd-kit transform model is position-only by design. (2) `handleDragMove` predates resize handles or was authored only for drag-to-move; the early-exit at line 1118 is correct for snap-lines (only drag-to-move computes snap) but accidentally also short-circuits live-resize. Classic case of one handler doing two jobs, correct for one. (3) handleDragEnd resize branch and the new Option-A handleDragMove resize branch would have identical bodies; @dnd-kit guarantees final dragEnd with cumulative delta; the redundant commit is idempotent — a `dispatchResizeCommit` helper extraction is a minor cleanup, not required. (4) Operator-mental-model inconsistency between Option A's live-input-update (resize) vs drag-to-move's input-lag (CSS-translate path) — flagged for operator hand-validation post-fix. (5) Process canon candidate: "@dnd-kit transform model is position-only; dimensional/rotational/skew gestures need state-mediated rendering" — substrate pattern worth canonizing for any future drag-to-rotate, drag-to-skew, drag-to-curve workflow-canvas connectors. Flagged for post-fix canon-update arc; NOT pre-locked. **Files modified**: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-live-preview.md` (new, ~1,900 words / ~250 lines markdown), `STATE.md` (this entry). **No code touched. No tests touched. No canon doc edits. The 114 unstaged screenshot deletions untouched per scope.** Active arc → none; investigation produced. Filed for next arc → **`resize-live-preview-fix`** (single combined dispatch — production handleDragMove resize branch + JSDOM keyboard test + source-shape regression gate + Playwright resize-preview spec; depends on Option A lock). After fix arc lands + operator-verifies at staging, post-fix canon-update arc considers (a) DECISIONS.md entry for @dnd-kit transform-model-asymmetry observation, (b) snap-during-resize follow-up investigation evaluation. Canon entry count unchanged at 22 pending the fix + canon-update sequence.

- **2026-05-20 — Hover-state staging-regression fix arc shipped (uncommitted)** — pointerover/pointerout via bubbling event semantics; display:contents intermediate element root-caused. Pre-flight: HEAD verified `546aa46` per process canon (read-only hover-state investigation). Operator-confirmed root cause via staging DevTools diagnostic (native pointerenter listener attached at staging — zero events across 10+ hovers): the 3 narrowed candidates in investigation `546aa46` (ancestor pointer-events:none, latent overlay, React-19/DndContext batching) were ALL ruled out; the actual cause was a fourth candidate the investigation didn't enumerate. **Root cause locked**: `onPointerEnter` / `onPointerLeave` use non-bubbling native semantics; their hit-test cascade depends on layout-box crossing; the DOM chain between operator pointer and the FreeFormPlacedWidget draggable wrapper includes an intermediate `display: contents` div emitted by the `registerComponent` HOC at `frontend/src/lib/visual-editor/registry/register.ts:215` (every visually-editable component is wrapped); `display: contents` has no layout box; the cascade breaks at it in real chromium; JSDOM ignores `display: contents` entirely + dispatches synthetic events directly to the handler element so unit tests passed. **Fix**: swap to bubbling variants `onPointerOver` / `onPointerOut`. Bubbling rides DOM-tree edges (parent/child relationships) not layout-box adjacency, so it passes through `display: contents` cleanly. **`relatedTarget` contains-check** on pointerout is load-bearing: pointerout fires whenever the pointer moves to ANY child element, NOT only on widget exit; without the check, descendant-pointer-motion would flicker isHovered → false → true. With the check, isHovered → false runs only on true widget exit. Pointerover setting isHovered → true is idempotent across repeated fires. **Playwright integration path chosen**: option (d) — inline HTML fixture via `page.setContent` + real chromium pointer events, plus a source-shape regression gate inspecting the production file via Node `readFileSync`. Rationale: options (a) staging URL, (b) local dev server with seed, (c) unskip+extend FF-7 spec all require a seeded free-form Focus template at predictable coords (FF-7 spec is `.skip`'d pending this seed). Option (d) reproduces the EXACT bug-shape (display:contents intermediate + pointer-event handlers) without infrastructure dependencies. Spec lives at `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-hover-pointer-semantics.spec.ts` (~430 LOC). Production wiring continues to be covered by JSDOM vitest; the FF-7 spec activates when its seed lands. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied**: pre-fix Playwright result = 5 passed (fixture demonstration scenarios) + 1 FAILED (source-shape regression gate asserting production code uses `onPointerOver` / `onPointerOut` + relatedTarget contains-check — found the broken `onPointerEnter` / `onPointerLeave` instead). Post-fix Playwright result = 6/6 passing in 1.4s. The source-shape gate is the load-bearing pre-fix-fails / post-fix-passes assertion; the 4 fixture scenarios document the real-chromium behavior of the fix shape. **JSDOM tests updated** in `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx`: 6 hover tests' event names updated (`pointerEnter` → `pointerOver`; `pointerLeave` → `pointerOut` with `relatedTarget: document.body`); test names updated; 1 NEW test added (`pointerout with relatedTarget INSIDE widget does NOT hide handles`) explicitly guarding the contains-check using `screen.getByTestId("focus-builder-placed-widget-core")` as a known descendant of the draggable wrapper. Vitest 21/21 FreeFormPlacedWidget passes post-fix. **Investigation `546aa46` corrected**: §11 (Root cause confirmed via staging diagnostic) + §12 (Process canon candidates) appended; the investigation's locked 3-candidate set documented as ruled out; the actual fourth candidate (event-type-semantic axis: bubbling vs non-bubbling) documented in detail. **Architectural surprises during build**: (1) `display: contents` semantics in chromium — `registerComponent`'s HOC wraps every visually-editable widget in a `display: contents` div for the runtime editor's click-to-edit gesture, and this wrapper is in the DOM chain on every widget render. The non-bubbling hit-test cascade interacts with `display: contents` in a way that's invisible to JSDOM but load-bearing in chromium. (2) The Playwright `getByTestId` matcher counts DOM presence not visibility — my first fixture iteration used `style="display:none"` to toggle the handles, which counted regardless; the production behavior is React conditional render (mount/unmount), so the fixture was updated to mount/unmount handles via JS DOM manipulation, mirroring the production React render contract. (3) The `display: contents` HOC was added in Phase R-1 for the runtime editor selection overlay; it's load-bearing for that feature and cannot simply be removed. The fix routes around it via event-type choice, NOT by removing the HOC. (4) The investigation locked 3 candidates by LOCATION (ancestor chain, overlay, batching) but didn't enumerate by EVENT-TYPE SEMANTICS — generalizes to: investigations of event-related bugs must include the bubbling/non-bubbling/capture/passive axis explicitly. **Post-fix canon-update arc candidate list (now 4 entries)**: (i) Q-10 selection-only refinement → "hover OR selection" (carried from prior arc); (ii) investigation source-candidate audit ("have we enumerated by every relevant axis?") gate; (iii) investigation-time UX locks should be revisited by operator-experience data (carried from prior arc); (iv) **NEW** — investigations of event-related bugs must enumerate by event-type semantics (bubbling vs non-bubbling, capture vs bubble, passive vs active, synthetic vs native) as a load-bearing axis orthogonal to location enumeration. Filed for post-fix canon-update arc per established sequencing; NOT filed in this fix arc. **Operator-observable assertion canon honored**: all Playwright fixture scenarios assert on DOM presence (via `getByTestId(...).toHaveCount(N)`) of the handle elements at their specific testids. JSDOM tests assert on `screen.getAllByTestId("focus-builder-resize-handle")` length. Source-shape gate asserts on production file regex matches. No wrapper-attribute assertions. **FF-1 through FF-7 regression surface unchanged** — all 21 FreeFormPlacedWidget vitest tests pass post-fix (drag wiring, resize handle render conditions, context menu, hover-state). **Gate cascade**: `npx tsc -b` clean; vitest run (focused) 21/21 FreeFormPlacedWidget passes; vitest run (full suite) 3161/3163 pass with 1 pre-existing failure (`Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx > preview-card chrome preset updates live when chrome pill clicked` — verified pre-existing on `546aa46` HEAD pre-fix via `git stash` + full-suite re-run; passes when run in isolation; pollution / order-dependency unrelated to this fix arc — pre-fix full-suite had 3160 passed, post-fix has 3161 passed = +1 new test from the contains-check guard); `npm run build` clean in 5.54s; eslint on the 3 changed files = 2 pre-existing react-refresh errors (verified pre-existing on stash; not introduced by this fix arc); Playwright `focus-builder-hover-pointer-semantics` 6/6 passing in 1.4s. **Bundle delta**: pre-fix `6,123.23 kB` → post-fix `6,123.28 kB`. Absolute delta **+0.05 kB**; percentage delta **+0.0008%**. Effectively zero, as expected for a pure event-name swap with minor handler-body addition (the relatedTarget contains-check). **Migration head unchanged**: `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **Files modified**: `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` (~36 LOC delta: handler bodies updated + JSX prop names + comment-canon updates), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` (~30 LOC delta: 6 existing hover tests updated; 1 new contains-check test added at ~46 LOC), `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-hover-state-staging-regression.md` (+~100 LOC: §11 + §12 appended), `STATE.md` (this entry). **Files added**: `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-hover-pointer-semantics.spec.ts` (~430 LOC: inline fixture + 4 fixture scenarios + 1 sanity scenario + 1 source-shape regression gate). **Files NOT touched per scope discipline**: `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx` (confirmed innocent across multiple investigations), `register.ts` (display:contents HOC stays — load-bearing for runtime editor), today-pin-widget rendering path (display:contents stays; fix routes around it via event-type choice), the 114 unstaged screenshot deletions, CLAUDE.md / PLATFORM_ARCHITECTURE.md / DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md / DECISIONS.md / BRIDGEABLE_MASTER.md / FUNERAL_HOME_VERTICAL.md / VISION.md (canon docs — canon refinement filing deferred to post-fix canon-update arc), `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-free-form-focus-canvas.md` (per prompt). **Active arc** → hover-state-staging-regression-fix (this arc; uncommitted). **Filed for next arc** → post-fix canon-update arc considers DECISIONS.md entries for the 4 candidates listed above. - **2026-05-20 (later evening) — Read-only investigation arc produced: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-hover-state-staging-regression.md` filed (uncommitted); locks test-substrate gap; root cause unlocked pending DevTools diagnostic; fix arc shape locked.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `a1c10c7` per process canon (fix arc — resize-handle UX refinements). Scope: Finding 1 only (Finding 2 UUID leak not yet operator-verified at staging; deferred). **Static-code audit covered**: `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx`, `PlacedWidgetCore.tsx`, `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx`, `WidgetFreeFormLayer.tsx`, `FocusBuilderCanvas.tsx` outer wrapper, `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` DragOverlay/sensor config, `@dnd-kit/core` type declarations + PointerSensor source. **Six hypotheses audited (A spread overwrite / B child absorption / C non-bubbling / D CSS layout / E StrictMode / F multiple draggables)**. Hypothesis A ruled out doubly — handlers correctly ordered AFTER spread per FF-4 canon at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:198-207`, AND `DraggableAttributes` type at `node_modules/@dnd-kit/core/dist/hooks/useDraggable.d.ts:14-21` is purely ARIA-shaped (no pointer enter/leave handlers in `attributes`); `PointerSensor.activators` at `dist/sensors/pointer/PointerSensor.d.ts:10` is `onPointerDown` only (no pointer enter/leave in `listeners`). Hypothesis F ruled out — cascade is downstream of failing path. Hypothesis D ruled out at focus-builder layer; cannot rule out at ancestor chain without DevTools. **Hypothesis C confirmed in refined framing** — narrow form ("pointerenter non-bubbling") doesn't hold at W3C spec level (pointerenter fires on ancestor when entered via descendant); refined form does hold: `fireEvent.pointerEnter(draggable)` is a synchronous synthetic React event dispatch that bypasses every layer of browser hit-testing, compositing, native event delivery. **Tests prove handler-if-fired only; do NOT prove handler-fires**. **Root cause NOT locked from static evidence alone** — first FF-series investigation in this arc where static-code audit was exhausted without conclusive file:line evidence. Candidate set narrowed to three (in likelihood order): (1) ancestor `pointer-events: none` somewhere above the focus-builder canvas in the admin layout chrome / global stylesheets — JSDOM doesn't compute CSS so silently passes; (2) latent overlay element absolutely positioned over canvas that intercepts hit testing; (3) React 19 batching / DndContext re-render interaction. DevTools diagnostic step against staging required to discriminate. **Test-substrate gap locked independent of root cause**: all 5 hover-state JSDOM tests share the identical `fireEvent.pointerEnter(draggable) → expect handles` pattern; none of them assert hit-testable surface, ancestor `pointer-events`, layout compositing, or native event delivery. The `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:50-52` Q-40 comment already acknowledges JSDOM pointer-event unreliability for *drag gestures* via PointerSensor; the `a1c10c7` fix arc extended a NEW pointer-event surface (pointerenter/pointerleave outside @dnd-kit's listeners) WITHOUT applying the Q-40 discipline — covered only by JSDOM unit tests, no Playwright spec. **Fix shape locked**: single combined fix arc, sequenced internally — (a) DevTools diagnostic against staging as first step (no commit); (b) write Playwright spec FIRST in `frontend/tests/e2e/` covering hover-in → handles → hover-out → no-handles; (c) confirm spec FAILS against `a1c10c7` HEAD per verify-against-pre-fix canon; (d) apply production-code fix (LOC depends on which §4 candidate is real — 1-3 LOC if ancestor pointer-events override, 5-20 LOC if overlay interception, 30-60 LOC if React-batching refactor); (e) confirm Playwright passes + vitest 5 hover tests unchanged; (f) commit. Total fix-arc LOC estimate: **~55-160 LOC**, dominated by Playwright spec (~50-100) over production code (~5-60). **Process canon candidate filed**: "Unit tests using `fireEvent.<pointer-event>` prove handler-if-fired only; new pointer-event surfaces require Playwright coverage before merge. The Q-40 narrow lock generalizes to ALL pointer-event surfaces in the focus builder, not just drag-gesture PointerSensor events." Recommend filing in post-fix canon-update arc, not in the fix arc itself. Optional second canon candidate: "staging operator verification is the canonical real-browser gate, not vitest's JSDOM" — broader applicability. **Architectural surprises during investigation**: (1) `useDraggable.attributes` is purely ARIA-shaped — FF-4 plumbing canon was correctly applied but addressed a problem that doesn't exist at this surface (no harm; canon-driven defensive coding is free when not needed); (2) JSDOM's lack of CSS / layout silently undermines a class of UI behavior tests broader than Q-40's narrow scope; (3) all 5 hover-state tests share an identical pattern that doesn't distinguish "the handler fired" from "the handler did the right thing when fired"; (4) the investigation could not lock root cause from static evidence alone — first such instance in the FF-series; honest accounting flagged in §10 of the doc. **Files**: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-hover-state-staging-regression.md` (new, ~2,400 words / ~280 lines markdown), `STATE.md` (this entry). **No code touched.
