- **2026-05-20 — Resize handle UX refinements fix arc shipped (uncommitted) — Finding 1 (hover-state) + Finding 2 (DragOverlay UUID leak class-fix).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `224cc06` per process canon (read-only investigation commit). Single combined dispatch against locks in `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-handle-ux-refinements.md`. **Finding 1 — hover-state addition**: `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` gained local `isHovered` state + `onPointerEnter` / `onPointerLeave` handlers (declared AFTER `{...attributes}` spread per FF-4 plumbing canon so @dnd-kit's attributes can't overwrite). Resize handle render condition changed from `selected ? <ResizeHandleOverlay/> : null` → `(isHovered || selected || isDragging) ? <ResizeHandleOverlay/> : null`. The `isDragging` defensive third branch was added pre-emptively (not via runtime verification) because @dnd-kit pointer-capture behavior during keyboard-sensor active drag is environment-sensitive; the cost is zero (one boolean read) and the risk removed is handles-vanishing-mid-resize. Touch / pointer-coarse degrades naturally via selection branch (no special-case code). **Finding 2 — UUID leak class-fix via `resolveDragLabel` pure helper**: new `resolveDragLabel.ts` (~54 LOC) + `resolveDragLabel.test.ts` (9 tests covering all four drag-id shapes). Helper encapsulates palette-prefix check directly (Option B per dispatch — no cross-file dependency on `FocusBuilderPalette.tsx::paletteItemIdToSlug`; both files own a copy of the canonical `palette-widget:` prefix string). FocusBuilderPage.tsx's `handleDragStart` callsite at line 792 changed from `setActiveDragLabel(slug ?? id)` → `setActiveDragLabel(resolveDragLabel(id))`. Returns palette slug for `palette-widget:<slug>` ids (preserves existing operator-visible label for palette drags); returns null for all other shapes (DragOverlay child guard at line 1303 short-circuits cleanly — no refinement needed). The class-of-bug fix extended to whole-widget drag (FF-3) automatically — the `free-form-placed-widget:<uuid>` shape was leaking too but operators hadn't reported it because the prefix made it read as a label, not a UUID. **Architectural surprise during build — load-bearing dual purpose of `activeDragLabel`**: pre-fix, `activeDragLabel !== null` at FocusBuilderPage.tsx:721 was acting as a **drag-in-progress sentinel** for the page-level arrow-key nudge guard. With my null-for-resize change, the sentinel evaporated → page-level keydown handler raced @dnd-kit's KeyboardSensor → 3 FF-4 resize integration tests failed with deterministic position drift (x=102 vs expected 100, x=194 vs expected 200, etc — the page-level nudge handler was applying its `stepDelta=1` shift on top of @dnd-kit's keyboard step). **Fix**: separated concerns with a new `isDragInProgress: boolean` state, set true in `handleDragStart`, cleared in `handleDragEnd` + `handleDragCancel`. The nudge guard now reads `isDragInProgress` instead of `activeDragLabel !== null`. Two independent signals for two independent concerns: label content (rendering decision) + drag lifecycle (event-conflict guard). The investigation flagged the DragOverlay rendering as Finding 2's source but did NOT surface this secondary usage of `activeDragLabel`; it was discovered during build via FF-4 regression test triage. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied**: reverting the callsite to `setActiveDragLabel(paletteItemIdToSlug(id) ?? id)` made Test B (resize-handle drag) + Test C (whole-widget drag) fail with visible UUID text in the DragOverlay; Test A (palette drag) continued passing (palette slug is the one shape both pre/post-fix render correctly). Restored → all three pass. **Test surface**: `resolveDragLabel.test.ts` (9 new tests: palette slug return, multi-segment slug, resize handle null × 2, free-form whole-widget null, bare UUID null, empty string null, palette-prefix-only edge case, unrecognized shape null); `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` (5 new tests covering hover-on-not-selected, hover-AND-selected, pointerleave-preserves-when-selected, pointerleave-hides-when-not-selected, touch-fallback-via-selected); `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (3 new integration tests under new `describe("DragOverlay UUID leak class-fix")` block: Test A palette label preserved, Test B resize-handle suppressed, Test C whole-widget suppressed). All tests use the operator-observable assertion canon — assert against the rendered DOM at the specific `focus-builder-drag-overlay` testid + `focus-builder-resize-handle` testid presence/absence, NOT against wrapper attributes. **@dnd-kit aria-live announcer noted in test comments**: @dnd-kit emits a `DndLiveRegion-*` element that DOES carry the drag id ("Picked up draggable item …") for screen-reader a11y. That element is positioned-fixed + clipped to 1px (NOT operator-visible). Tests target the operator-visible DragOverlay testid, NOT the screen-reader region — initial test assertions used `queryByText(/-handle-/)` which incorrectly matched the live region; tightened to `queryByTestId("focus-builder-drag-overlay")`. **Operator-observable canon honored**: every assertion targets the specific rendered element via testid; no wrapper-attribute assertions. **Gate cascade**: 350/350 focus-builder vitest tests green (29 test files); `npx tsc -b` clean; `npm run lint` unchanged at 584 errors (all pre-existing per pre-fix diff confirmation — no new lint regressions introduced by my files); `npm run build` clean in 5.10s. **Bundle delta**: pre-arc `6,122.99 kB` → post-arc `6,123.23 kB`. Absolute delta **+0.24 kB**; percentage delta **+0.0039%**. Cost-of-fix is essentially free (one new boolean state + 54-line helper file). **Migration head unchanged**: `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **LOC delta** (focus-builder only): +475 source/test modifications + 117 new file lines = ~592 LOC. Within combined-arc estimate (140-270 LOC source + tests; combined is higher because the actual cost includes the `isDragInProgress` discovery + extensive hover-state test coverage + DragOverlay class-fix integration test scaffolding). **Q-10 refinement canon entry filing**: deferred per investigation §4 — file AFTER this fix arc commits. Q-10's investigation-time lock ("8 resize handles on-selection-only") refined by this fix arc to "hover OR selection OR isDragging." Canon-update arc considers a `DECISIONS.md` entry covering both (a) the Q-10 refinement itself and (b) the discovered process canon (investigation-time UX locks may need operator-experience refinement; investigation-time source-candidate locks may miss secondary load-bearing usages of the same state). The activeDragLabel dual-purpose discovery is itself a process-canon candidate. **Files modified**: `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/focus-builder/FocusBuilderPage.tsx` (37 LOC delta — import + 2 new lines in handleDragStart + 1 new line in handleDragEnd + 1 new line in handleDragCancel + isDragInProgress useState + 1-line guard change at line 721 + deps array change), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` (43 LOC delta — import-type → import + useState + 2 useCallback handlers + 2 new wrapper props + render-condition expansion + comment updates), `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (+239 LOC — describe block with 3 integration tests), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` (+167 LOC — 5 hover-state tests + existing test rename to clarify "AND not hovered"), `resolveDragLabel.ts` (new, 54 LOC), `resolveDragLabel.test.ts` (new, 63 LOC). **Files NOT touched per scope discipline**: `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx` (confirmed innocent during investigation), `FocusBuilderPalette.tsx::paletteItemIdToSlug` (not refactored — `resolveDragLabel` is independent), the 2 investigation docs (read-only reference), CLAUDE.md / PLATFORM_ARCHITECTURE.md / DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md / DECISIONS.md / BRIDGEABLE_MASTER.md / FUNERAL_HOME_VERTICAL.md / VISION.md (canon docs — Q-10 canon refinement filing deferred to post-deploy verification arc per investigation §4). **Active arc** → resize-handle-ux-fixes (this arc; uncommitted). **Filed for next arc** → Q-10 canon refinement entry in DECISIONS.md + investigation-arc-to-fix-arc process-canon entry capturing the `activeDragLabel` dual-purpose discovery. Canon entry count unchanged at 22 pending the Q-10 follow-up arc.

- **2026-05-20 (evening) — Read-only investigation arc produced: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-handle-ux-refinements.md` filed (uncommitted); locks two FF-4 operator-experience refinements; fix arc pending dispatch.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `9e47a3e` per process canon (focus-template free-form migration arc). Investigation triggered by two operator concerns surfaced during FF-series staging verification: (1) handles should appear on hover (current Q-10 lock: selection-only) — operator feedback verbatim "I would like it to work on hover without clicking the widget if that is possible"; (2) visible UUID text adjacent to widgets during active resize drag matching `<placement-uuid>-handle-<position>`. **Finding 1 locked at option (a) — hover OR selection.** Reasoning: discoverability via hover preserves the Figma / Sketch precedent operator behavior; selection-based persistence preserves the active-manipulation case where pointer drifts off mid-resize; touch / pointer-coarse devices degrade naturally via tap-to-select. LOC est ~30-60 (local useState + pointer-enter / pointer-leave on existing draggable wrapper at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:170-206`; condition change at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:225`). **Finding 2 locked at root cause: DragOverlay rendering `activeDragLabel` (= raw drag id) for non-palette drag-id shapes.** File:line evidence: `FocusBuilderPage.tsx:792` (`setActiveDragLabel(slug ?? id)` — explicit fallback to raw id when `paletteItemIdToSlug` returns null) + `FocusBuilderPage.tsx:1312` (`{activeDragLabel}` rendered as visible text content inside the DragOverlay child at lines 1302-1315). The text appears "outside the widget's right edge" because @dnd-kit's DragOverlay follows the cursor — during resize-SE-handle drag, cursor is at bottom-right corner of widget, overlay renders adjacent. ResizeHandleOverlay confirmed innocent — every line read at `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx:160-188`, handle divs render NO text content; data-attributes only. Same bug class affects whole-widget drag id (`free-form-placed-widget:<uuid>`) but operator hadn't reported it because the prefix made the leak look like a label rather than a raw UUID. **Fix shape**: new pure helper `resolveDragLabel(id: string): string | null` that returns slug for `palette-widget:` prefix; null for `free-form-placed-widget:` prefix; null for `<uuid>-handle-<position>` shape; null for unrecognized ids (safe default — no UUID leak by accident). DragOverlay child guard at line 1303 already handles null correctly. LOC est ~40-80 (helper + handler change + 6-10 unit tests + 1 integration test). **Combined fix arc shape recommendation: single dispatch** — both findings touch the same FF-4 substrate; ~140-270 LOC total; no architectural dependency between them. **Q-10 refinement note flagged**: substrate now carries operator-experience-derived knowledge that the Q-10 investigation-time lock (selection-only) needs refinement to hover-OR-selection. Canon-update arc should file AFTER the fix arc commits, recording both the new behavior and the investigation-time → operator-time refinement chain. **Architectural surprises**: (a) the same bug class affects ALL non-palette drag-id shapes, not just resize handles; (b) `paletteItemIdToSlug` was never designed as a universal label resolver and the `slug ?? id` fallback was a load-bearing safety net that started leaking when FF-4 introduced the resize-handle id shape; (c) ResizeHandleOverlay is genuinely innocent; (d) Q-10 predates operator hands; (e) DragOverlay is net-positive for one drag-id shape (palette) and net-negative for two (whole-widget, resize-handle) — suppressing via null return for the latter two preserves the overlay component for any future drag shapes that need a floating label. **Step 4 evidence conclusive** — no live-DOM DevTools diagnostic step required for the fix arc; dispatch directly against locked source candidate. **Files modified**: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-handle-ux-refinements.md` (new, ~2,400 words / ~280 lines markdown), `STATE.md` (this entry). **No code touched. No tests. No canon doc edits.** Active arc → none; investigation produced. Filed for next arc → **`resize-handle-ux-fixes`** (combined fix for Findings 1 + 2; depends on locks above). After fix arc lands, canon-update arc considers a `DECISIONS.md` entry for the Q-10 refinement + the discovered process canon (investigation-time UX locks refined by operator experience). Canon entry count unchanged at 22.

- **2026-05-20 — Focus template free-form migration arc shipped (uncommitted) — Standalone data-migration arc; reverses investigation Q-24 as product decision.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `14844c6` (FF-7). Standalone scope: NO substrate changes, NO frontend code changes, NO new canon entries. Single Alembic data migration `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform` (~315 LOC including pure helpers + 36-test coverage file at `backend/tests/test_focus_template_freeform_migration.py` — ~480 LOC, all green). Converts all grid-shape Focus templates in the `focus_templates` table to free-form-shape placements matching the Decide canvas substrate shipped in FF-1 through FF-7. **Q-24 reversal rationale**: at investigation time, decoupling substrate landing from migration risk was correct. Now that substrate has landed, the product decision is clear — Focus templates ARE Decide canvas substrate; existing grid-shape templates should match. **Per-placement translation rules**: widget placements get `x = starting_column * (canvas_width / 12)`, `width = column_span * (canvas_width / 12)`, `y = row_index * 200`, `height = 200` (universal fallback — widget registry's `defaultDimensions` lives frontend-side per F-3 substrate; backend has no access at Alembic time + no need; operators adjust heights post-migration via FF-4's resize gesture), `z_index = 0`. Inherited core placements (`is_core: true`) use the Q-20 canonical formula: `core_width = canvas_width * (clamped_column_span / 12)`, `core_x = (canvas_width - core_width) / 2`, `core_y = 40`, `core_height = canvas_height - 40`. The migration reads `default_column_span` from the placement's stored `column_span` (not from the live `focus_cores` row) because the F-series validator already enforces that `is_core` placements match the inherited core's component identity, and authors typically set `column_span == default_column_span` — self-contained migration discipline beats cross-table joins for no behavioral difference. **Canvas dimensions stamped per FF-1 pattern**: templates without `canvas_config.width` / `.height` get the FF-1 defaults (1200×800). Pre-existing canvas_config keys (gap_size, background_treatment, padding, etc.) are preserved verbatim — partial canvas_config blobs survive the stamp. **Grid fields cleared post-migration**: each placement loses `starting_column` + `column_span`; rows lose `column_count`. **Idempotent both directions**: upgrade detects already-free-form templates via field-presence check on any of x/y/width/height (matches backend `_placement_shape` semantics) and skips with explanatory log line; downgrade detects already-grid templates via the inverse check + skips. **Reversible**: down migration restores grid shape with `column_count: 12` per row + derived `starting_column` / `column_span` via rounding `x / (canvas_width / 12)` and `width / (canvas_width / 12)`. Provided for emergency rollback only; never expected to fire. **Investigation findings surfaced during pre-flight**: (1) The only currently seeded template `scheduling-fh` (vertical=manufacturing) ships with `rows: []` — accessories are populated via Tier 3 (`focus_compositions`) sub-arc C, not via Tier 2 placements. Migration on the dev DB found 0 templates (empty `focus_templates` table verified via psql); migration on staging will see 1 active row with empty rows and trivially skip-or-no-op (no placements to convert). **Operator-authored templates** are the real migration target — any operator who used the F-3 builder to author grid-shape templates before this arc shipped gets their data lifted to the canvas substrate without manual re-authoring. (2) `is_core: bool` is an EXPLICIT discriminator on placements per the `FocusTemplate` model docstring at `backend/app/models/focus_template.py:34`. Service-layer validator enforces exactly-one `is_core: true` placement per template + identity match against the inherited core. No fallback needed; explicit field carries the signal. (3) `column_count` lives on the ROW envelope (1..12) — rows can have arbitrary column counts in F-series, NOT always 12. The migration uses canvas-relative arithmetic (`canvas_width / 12`) regardless of `column_count` because the FF canvas substrate is canvas-relative, not row-relative; this is a deliberate semantic shift documented in FF-1's `_freeform_row` test fixture comment ("column_count is irrelevant for free-form placements but the row-level validator still requires it"). (4) Backend has NO widget-registry access at Alembic time — registry is frontend-only per F-3 substrate. Universal 200px height fallback is the only sensible value at migration time. Operators adjust via FF-4's resize gesture post-deploy. (5) JSONB read/write at Alembic time goes through `op.get_bind()` + `sa.text("CAST(:rows AS jsonb)")` with `json.dumps` parameter values — matches the pattern in adjacent migrations for raw JSONB UPDATE. Reads handled via `_coerce_jsonb` helper that defensively handles dict/list/string driver variations. **Test coverage** (36 tests, 1.35s wall, all green): shape detection × 6 (free-form-via-x, grid-via-starting_column, empty rows, empty placements, free-form-via-width, defensive non-dict row); free-form migration × 9 (widget translation basic + offset + row_index, clears-grid-fields, row loses column_count, core uses Q-20 full-width-centered + narrower-centered, preserves prop_overrides + display_config + placement_id, mixed widget+core in two rows); canvas stamping × 5 (empty, None, partial preserves keys, explicit dimensions preserved, only-width stamps height); to-grid downgrade × 4 (widget reverse, row regains column_count, round-trip restores grid, clamps overflow when x+width round to span > 12); idempotency × 4 (upgrade skips already-freeform, upgrade twice no-op, downgrade skips already-grid, downgrade skips empty); defensive × 3 (non-dict row passes through, non-dict placement passes through, missing starting_column defaults to 0); JSONB coercion × 4 (dict, list, string, None); end-to-end DB × 1 (seed a FocusCore + grid-shape FocusTemplate via service layer, run migration pure-function path against the live row via connection bind, verify post-row carries free-form shape + Q-20 core + canvas stamped + column_count stripped + gap_size preserved). **Gate cascade**: 36/36 migration-specific tests green; 110/110 across `test_focus_template_inheritance_service.py` + `test_focus_template_freeform_validation.py` + `test_focus_compositions.py` + new migration test file (no regression in adjacent F-series tests); `alembic upgrade head` clean (migration applied: `migrated=0 skipped=0 total=0` on empty dev DB); `alembic downgrade -1` clean (`reverted=0 skipped=0 total=0`); re-`upgrade head` clean (full cycle idempotency confirmed); `npx tsc -b` clean (no frontend changes). **Migration head advances**: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session` → `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **Frontend code unchanged.** **Architectural surprises during build, in order of significance:** (1) **`column_count` per-row vs canvas-relative ambiguity** — the F-series schema permits arbitrary `column_count` 1..12 per row, but the FF canvas substrate is canvas-relative (always /12 against canvas_width). The migration deliberately treats all grid-shape templates as if column_count=12 for x/width arithmetic, because (a) the seeded scheduling-fh template uses column_count=12 throughout, (b) the inherited core's `default_column_span` validator caps at 12, (c) any operator-authored template with column_count<12 would still convert sensibly (the placement just won't span the full canvas width post-migration, matching its grid-shape proportional position). Documented inline in the migration helper. (2) **Self-contained migration discipline beat cross-table joins** — the inherited core's `default_column_span` lives on `focus_cores` (Tier 1), but the migration reads from the placement's stored `column_span` instead. Rationale: F-series authors set `column_span == default_column_span` by convention (validator enforces identity match on `is_core: true`); avoiding the join means the migration is self-contained + easier to reason about + has no risk of an out-of-band `focus_cores` change mid-deploy invalidating in-progress migrations. (3) **JSONB driver variance forced a `_coerce_jsonb` helper** — depending on psycopg2 version + connection state, JSONB columns may come back as native Python dict/list OR as string. The helper normalizes; tested explicitly with 4 cases. (4) **Test discovery via importlib bypassed Alembic's import mechanism** — Alembic migration files aren't importable via dotted-path because `backend/alembic/versions/` lacks `__init__.py`. Tests load the migration module via `importlib.util.spec_from_file_location` against the absolute path. Pattern is reusable for any future migration tests that need to exercise pure-function helpers. **Manual verification deferred to post-deploy on staging**: load `scheduling-fh` template in admin; confirm canvas renders via WidgetFreeFormLayer (per FF-2 canvas substrate mode detection); FF-3 drag, FF-4 resize, FF-5 z-index, FF-6 inspector positioning, FF-7 snap/marquee/align gestures all work against the migrated data. Local dev DB has 0 focus_templates rows (verified via psql query) — staging is the first surface where real seeded data flows through the migration. **Future arcs**: if operator-authored Tier 2 templates accumulate in production AND a column_count<12 row shape appears, audit migration output for those edge cases. Pure-helper test fixtures cover column_count=12 only; staging deploy is the first real-data verification.

- **2026-05-20 — Sub-arc FF-7 shipped (uncommitted) — FF-series ARC FINALE — Snap-to-alignment + keyboard nudge + multi-select on canvas + Playwright pointer-event gate.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `065b59e` (FF-6). FF-7 closes the FF-series investigation (Q-1–Q-37 LOCKED) and mitigates the three pinned risks (Q-38 deploy-race, Q-39 canvas-dimension overflow, Q-40 JSDOM-vs-pointer-events gap). The free-form Focus canvas substrate is now FEATURE-COMPLETE; future Focus authoring work moves into vertical-specific arcs (real widget functionality, generation Focus templates per BRIDGEABLE_MASTER §3.26.11.12). **Four concerns shipped in one arc, each ringfenced to a self-contained subsystem:** (1) **Snap-to-alignment helpers** per Q-11 (b): new pure helper `computeSnapAdjustment` (261 LOC + 213 LOC test) computes proximity-to-6px against other placements' left/right/center edges + canvas centerlines; Alt-key disables; multi-axis snap allowed; SnapLine emit. New `SnapLineOverlay` component (72 LOC + 81 LOC test) renders 1px brass-accent overlay lines spanning the canvas with `pointer-events: none`. Page-level `handleDragMove` (DragMoveEvent from @dnd-kit) wires live snap during drag; `handleDragEnd` applies snap AFTER canvas-bounds clamp, then RE-clamps so a snap target near the edge that would push outside defers to the bound. Document-level keydown/keyup track alt-key state in `altKeyHeldRef` (ref-as-dominant-defense per the 2026-05-19 canon — @dnd-kit's DragMoveEvent does not expose activator modifiers mid-gesture). Snap lines cleared at drag-end + drag-cancel. (2) **Keyboard nudge** per Q-12: window-level keydown handler in FocusBuilderPage. Arrow keys nudge selected widget(s) by 1px; Shift+arrow nudges by 10px; `]` / `[` move z-order forward/backward; Shift+`]` / Shift+`[` move to front/back. Z-order shortcuts SINGLE-SELECT only per investigation (multi-select z-order behavior undefined; deferred). Defensive guards: ignores typing in INPUT / TEXTAREA / contenteditable / BUTTON (covers ScrubbableButton's own arrow-driven scrub UX) AND ignores when `activeDragLabel !== null` (a drag is in flight; @dnd-kit's KeyboardSensor owns arrow keys). Both guards were verify-against-pre-fix-required — the F-3.1b / F-3.1c chrome-scrub regression tests + FF-4 resize tests failed when my window listener hijacked their ArrowRight events; adding the BUTTON + activeDragLabel guards restored every previously-green test. (3) **Multi-select on canvas** per Q-16 (a) + Q-17 (b) + Q-18 (a): `FocusBuilderSelectionContext` extended additively with `widgets-multi` discriminator + five helpers (`addToSelection` / `removeFromSelection` / `clearSelection` / `setMultiSelection` / `isInSelection`). Single-select model UNCHANGED. PlacedWidgetCore extended with optional `onShiftSelect` prop — when present, shift+click routes through it (calls `addToSelection` or `removeFromSelection` depending on `isInSelection`); regular click still calls `onSelect` (preserves F-3.1c behavior). New `MarqueeOverlay` (57 LOC + 75 LOC test): absolutely-positioned rubber-band rectangle with 1px brass-accent border + ~15% alpha brass-subtle fill; 3×3 px threshold before rendering. WidgetFreeFormLayer accepts `onLayerPointerDown` / `Move` / `Up` props + carries `data-canvas-background="true"` on the layer element — page-level marquee dispatcher discriminates pointer-down by `target.getAttribute("data-canvas-background")` so a pointer-down on the canvas background starts marquee, but pointer-down on a widget starts widget-drag (gestures route to different state machines via target attribute, not via stopPropagation arms-race). On pointer-up, marquee state computes AABB intersection of every free-form placement vs the marquee rect; `setMultiSelection(intersectingIds)` commits the selection. Marquee below the 3px threshold collapses to `clearSelection` (background-click semantics preserved). **Critical fix during build: the pre-FF-7 hook `updateWidget` read `rowsRef.current` synchronously BEFORE calling `setRowsDraft(next)`; rowsRef is updated by a useEffect that runs AFTER render, so two synchronous `updateWidget` calls (e.g., multi-select arrow nudge moving widgets A + B) raced — the second call read the OLD rowsRef value and silently OVERWROTE the first call's setRowsDraft. The fix: convert to functional `setRowsDraft((current) => ...)` so React's batched-state-update pipeline supplies each call with the latest state. queueSave fires unconditionally on every call (debounced save coalesces; saving unchanged state is harmless at the boundary). Six existing F-3 / FF-3 / FF-4 / FF-5 / FF-6 hook regression tests stay green with the functional updater (verified). This is the most architecturally interesting change in FF-7 because it surfaces a latent race in updateWidget that was undetectable before multi-select made sequential same-tick mutations a load-bearing path.** New `computeAlignTargets` pure helper (79 LOC + 89 LOC test): six align actions (left / right / center-horizontal / top / bottom / center-vertical) over the selection bounding box (NOT canvas — operator intent is "align THESE widgets to each other"). New `AlignInspectorSection` (107 LOC + 81 LOC test): 2×3 button grid in the inspector, brass-accent hover, lucide AlignStartVertical / AlignCenterVertical / etc. icons; disabled when `selectedPlacements.length < 2`; multi-select count caption underneath. **CanvasContextMenu extended with `actionSet` prop** (default "z-order" preserves FF-5; new "align" branch renders the 6 align icons with `context-menu-action-align-${action}` test-ids); page-level dispatcher passes `actionSet={selection.kind === "widgets-multi" ? "align" : "z-order"}` and unified `handleContextMenuActionUnified` routes the action vocabulary by selection.kind. FocusBuilderInspector branches on `selection.kind === "widgets-multi"` BEFORE the single-select widget branch: hides Configuration / Placement / Chrome / Position / Layer / Remove; shows ONLY AlignInspectorSection per Q-18 (a). Cleanly composed onto existing F-2 inspector. (4) **Playwright pointer-event verification gate** per Q-40: new spec file `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts` (207 LOC) with 5 chromium scenarios covering pointer drag, pointer resize SE handle, focus-preservation-during-canvas-drag (FF-6 load-bearing UX correctness), snap visual feedback, marquee selection. Spec body fully written; scenarios marked `.skip` pending two staging-side seed gaps (a free-form-template fixture + a canonical URL path opening the Focus Builder against it). Spec infrastructure ships NOW so future fill-in is the smallest possible delta. **15 new files** (computeSnapAdjustment.ts + .test.ts, SnapLineOverlay.tsx + .test.tsx, MarqueeOverlay.tsx + .test.tsx, computeAlignTargets.ts + .test.ts, AlignInspectorSection.tsx + .test.tsx, FocusBuilderSelectionContext.test.tsx, focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts = 12 source + 3 retest-tests on previously-existing files via .test.tsx additions); **13 modified files** (FocusBuilderSelectionContext.tsx +102 LOC, PlacedWidgetCore.tsx + .test.tsx +16/56, FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx +16, WidgetFreeFormLayer.tsx +66, FocusBuilderCanvas.tsx +35, FocusBuilderInspector.tsx + .test.tsx +48/131, FocusBuilderPage.tsx +530, FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx +321, CanvasContextMenu.tsx + .test.tsx +139/71, useFocusTemplateDraft.ts +51). **LOC delta: ~2,912 inserts / 90 deletes = +2,822 net** — at the upper edge of the 1,500-2,400 midpoint range, within the 2,800 worst-case ceiling. Total touched: ~2,912 LOC. **Tests shipped Phase FF-7**: 333/333 focus-builder + hook tests passing (+57 vs FF-6: +12 computeSnapAdjustment + 5 SnapLineOverlay + 9 computeAlignTargets + 4 AlignInspectorSection + 5 MarqueeOverlay + 9 FocusBuilderSelectionContext + 3 PlacedWidgetCore shift-click + 3 CanvasContextMenu actionSet + 3 FocusBuilderInspector multi-select + 4 FocusBuilderPage integration). **Playwright spec: 5 scenarios registered, 5 skipped pending staging seed; spec body complete and exercises real chromium pointer pipeline once activated.** **tsc clean.** **eslint clean for FF-7 net change** — 584 / 473 errors / 111 warnings post-FF-7 EXACTLY matches the pre-FF-7 (FF-6) baseline; no new warnings or errors introduced. The pre-existing react-refresh/only-export-components warnings on FocusBuilderCanvas / FreeFormPlacedWidget / PlacedWidgetCore / FocusBuilderSelectionContext are inherited patterns, not FF-7-introduced. **vite build clean** (5.43s); bundle **6,122.99 kB** vs FF-6 baseline **6,107.89 kB** = **+15.10 kB absolute / +0.247% percentage** (separately reported per F-3.1c precedent; well within ±0.5% tolerance). Backend pytest unchanged — FF-7 touches zero backend files. **Architectural surprises during build, in order of significance:** (1) **The hook updateWidget race surfaced ONLY when multi-select made sequential same-tick mutations load-bearing** — the latent bug had existed since F-3 (or earlier) but was always masked because F-3's single-widget mutations or FF-3's single-drag commits never queued two `updateWidget` calls in the same JS tick. Converting to functional setState was a 30-line surgical fix preserving all existing behavior. The pattern's discovery itself is the most architecturally interesting moment of FF-7 — the multi-select feature literally exposed pre-FF-7 latent timing fragility, and the fix is now load-bearing for ANY future arc that calls updateWidget multiple times synchronously. (2) **Keyboard-nudge listener hijack of ScrubbableButton + @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor** — first runs of FF-7 broke 5 pre-existing tests (F-3.1b chrome scrub × 2, FF-4 resize × 3) because my window-keydown listener processed arrow keys before the inner consumer-component handlers. Fix: add `tag === "BUTTON"` short-circuit (covers ScrubbableButton + LayerInspectorSection buttons + AlignInspectorSection buttons + tab buttons) + `activeDragLabel !== null` short-circuit (covers active @dnd-kit gestures). Both guards are minimal AND test-validated; the regression test set caught both issues immediately. (3) **Marquee pointer-up captured stale React synthetic-event reference** — initial implementation called `(e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).getBoundingClientRect()` INSIDE the `setMarquee((prev) => ...)` updater body; React pools synthetic events, so by the time the updater function runs, `e.currentTarget` is null. Fix: capture rect + coords OUTSIDE the updater (before the call), close over the captured values inside. (4) **The selection.kind="widgets-multi" inspector branch sits BEFORE the single-select widget branch** in FocusBuilderInspector — the order matters because both branches handle `mode === "template"`; multi-select must short-circuit before the single-widget findPlacementById path runs. Documented in the inspector source comment block. (5) **Drag-of-non-selected-widget UX decision: deferred — only-this-widget moves on multi-select-active state** — the FF-7 prompt acknowledged the ambiguity; I chose Figma precedent (a drag of a widget NOT in the multi-selection moves only that widget; selection persists). Documented in the FreeFormPlacedWidget drag flow + future-polish flags below. **Build-report item answers** (per FF-7 prompt's 13-item gate): (1) Snap composed cleanly with FF-3 drag substrate; snap fires AFTER canvas-bounds clamp; snap result re-clamped so a snap target near the edge defers to the bound. (2) Keyboard nudge correctly preventsDefault on arrows + bails on BUTTON activeElement + bails when activeDragLabel != null; ScrubbableButton + @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor regression tests stay green. (3) Multi-select state extension composed cleanly with single-select; addToSelection idempotent across single / multi / none cases; isInSelection works across single + multi. (4) Marquee AABB intersection handles fully-inside, partial overlap, and below-threshold + click-without-drag-clears-selection cases (verified via integration test). (5) AlignInspectorSection's selection-bounding-box align computation matches operator intent — align-left targets `min(x)`, right targets `max(x+width)-width`, center-horizontal targets bbox-center. Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied at integration level on Test A (multi-select via shift+click + align). (6) CanvasContextMenu's `actionSet` prop composed cleanly with FF-5 single-select action set; the actionSet="align" branch renders the 6 lucide AlignXXX icons via the same MenuItem array pattern; data-action-set attribute exposes the active vocabulary for assertion targeting. (7) Playwright config + spec consumed the EXISTING `frontend/playwright.config.ts` infrastructure (testDir `tests/e2e/`, chromium project). Spec file lives at `tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts` OUTSIDE the runtime-editor subdir; CI integration deferred — the existing `.github/workflows/playwright-staging.yml` runs only `tests/e2e/runtime-editor/` and adding the focus-builder spec requires a workflow-extension follow-up. (8) All 5 Playwright scenarios marked `.skip` pending the staging-side seed gap (free-form Focus template fixture + reachable URL). Scenarios are fully implemented and ready to activate via a one-line per-scenario edit when the seed lands. (9) All FF-1 through FF-6 behaviors continue working — full 333-test regression green; the only test fragility surfaced was a PRE-EXISTING Tier2TemplatesEditor flake (`preview-card chrome preset updates live` — fails 2-3/3 runs of the full parallel vitest suite both PRE-FF-7 and POST-FF-7; verified by stashing FF-7 changes and running pre-baseline x3 — flake exists at the baseline; NOT a FF-7 regression). (10) Operator-observable canon honored: every FF-7 integration assertion targets DOM-level state (inline `left` / `top` style on draggable wrapper, AlignInspectorSection data-testid presence/absence, MarqueeOverlay data-testid presence, snap-line data-testid presence, multi-select count caption text) AND save-side PUT body shape where applicable (Test A). NOT internal wrapper attributes. (11) Bundle delta +15.10 kB absolute / +0.247% percentage (separately reported). (12) Five architectural surprises documented above (hook race, keyboard hijack, synthetic-event pooling, inspector branch ordering, drag-of-non-selected UX deferred). (13) **FF-series COMPLETION DECLARATION**: investigation questions Q-1 through Q-37 LOCKED across the seven sub-arcs (FF-1 backend; FF-2 canvas substrate; FF-3 drag-to-move; FF-4 resize; FF-5 z-index; FF-6 inspector positioning; FF-7 polish + verification). Risks Q-38 (deploy race) mitigated by FF-1-before-FF-2 sequential dispatch (shipped). Q-39 (canvas-dimension overflow) mitigated by per-template `canvas_config.width`/`.height` with defensive fallback (shipped). Q-40 (JSDOM-vs-pointer-events) mitigated by KeyboardSensor + direct-hook-invocation patterns in vitest + Playwright pointer-event coverage gate (shipped, .skip pending seed). The free-form Focus canvas substrate is feature-complete; future Focus authoring work moves into vertical-specific arcs (real widget functionality, generation Focus templates). **Future polish flags surfaced but not addressed in FF-7** (deferred per Q-32/33/34/35/36 + FF-7 scope discipline): distribute affordance (Q-17 (c) variant — even-spacing), layout templates (Q-32 save-as-reusable-layout), mobile/touch interactions (Q-33), collaborative cursors (Q-34), smart positioning engine (Q-35), tidy-up auto-arrangement (Q-36 — conflicts with operator-flexibility canon), multi-select z-order behavior (currently undefined; FF-7 z-order shortcuts are single-select only), drag-of-non-selected-widget UX (currently Figma-precedent: moves only that widget + preserves multi-selection; revisit if operator demand surfaces), CI workflow integration of focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts, staging seed of a free-form template fixture for Playwright activation. - **2026-05-20 — Sub-arc FF-6 shipped (uncommitted) — Inspector positioning fields (X / Y / Width / Height) with uncontrolled-with-sync focus-preservation pattern (fourth operator-interactive FF sub-arc; closes Q-30 (c)).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `be46182` (FF-5). After FF-6 ships, operators get pixel-precision positioning via four numeric inputs in a new "Position" section in the widget inspector, alongside the canvas drag (FF-3) + resize (FF-4) + Layer (FF-5) gestures they already have. Both interaction paths — canvas manipulation AND inspector-driven precision editing — update the same hook state and surface bidirectionally. Architecture: new component `PositionInspectorSection` (`frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/focus-builder/PositionInspectorSection.tsx`, 279 LOC) mounts inside `WidgetInspectorSection` between the existing Chrome and Layer sections, per the F-2 inspector composition canon (sections inline at the same composition layer). Renders a 2×2 grid of `PositionInput` controls (inline sub-component within the same file per the FF-6 prompt's item-9 latitude — file remains under ~280 LOC; extraction adds an indirection without clarity benefit). **Uncontrolled-with-sync pattern locked**: each PositionInput maintains local string state for in-progress edits; commits to placement via `onUpdate(field, clampedValue)` on blur OR Enter (NOT on each keystroke — avoids save-pulse storms during typing per the prompt's explicit gate). The load-bearing focus-preservation contract: a `useEffect([placementValue])` syncs local state from placement ONLY when the input is NOT focused (`document.activeElement !== inputRef.current`). When the input has focus, the operator's local string state dominates; canvas drag/resize/sibling-input updates do NOT clobber the mid-edit value. **Section ordering reorganized**: pre-FF-6 layout was Configuration / Placement / Layer / Chrome / Remove. Post-FF-6 layout matches the FF-6 prompt's spec: Configuration / Placement / Chrome / **Position** (NEW) / Layer (moved after Chrome) / Remove. Reordering required because Position semantically belongs adjacent to Layer (both control visual-layout dimensions); Chrome stays as the prominent middle section. **Free-form-shape detection at WidgetInspectorSection**: Position section renders ONLY when the placement carries any of x/y/width/height (mirrors the placement adapter's `isFreeFormShape` predicate). Grid placements (column_start + column_span only) skip the section entirely per the substrate-prevents-action canon: their positioning model is column-based and the existing Placement section covers it via `column_span`. The F-3 Placement section stays visible-but-empty for free-form placements per build-prompt instruction (future polish flag, NOT FF-6 scope). **Clamp semantics locked at PositionInspectorSection**: per-field clamp closures over canvas dimensions + min dimensions + sibling-field values matching Q-13 / Q-14 + FF-4 precedent (X: [0, canvas.width - widget.width]; Y: [0, canvas.height - widget.height]; Width: [min.width, canvas.width - widget.x]; Height: [min.height, canvas.height - widget.y]). Clamp math inlined at the input layer (rule-of-three — extracting a shared clamp helper waits for a 3rd consumer; FF-2 drop + FF-4 resize each have their own helpers, both consuming the same canvas + min substrate). Reuses `getFreeFormMinDimensions(widget_slug)` from FF-2's introspection helpers; 80×40 platform fallback. Canvas dimensions sourced from `templateHook.template?.canvas_config` with defensive 1200×800 fallback (matches FF-2 / FF-4 substrate). **Silent revert on invalid input** (Figma/Sketch precedent — NaN parse resets the display to current placement value; no error toast). Commit threshold: clamped !== placementValue (skips PUT for identity edits; pure cosmetic for the operator). Each PositionInput exposes `data-testid="position-input-{x|y|width|height}"` for integration-test targeting + `aria-label="X position"` etc. for a11y. Disabled state: when placement is null OR isCore is true (mirrors FF-5's LayerInspectorSection disabled semantics). **Canvas dimensions threaded through FocusBuilderInspector → WidgetInspectorSection → PositionInspectorSection**: 3-layer prop plumbing per FF-5's precedent. FocusBuilderInspector reads `templateHook.template?.canvas_config.width / .height` with defensive defaults at the source (one place to centralize the fallback). 2 new files (`PositionInspectorSection.tsx` 279 LOC, `PositionInspectorSection.test.tsx` 277 LOC = **556 new LOC**). 3 modified files (`WidgetInspectorSection.tsx` +66 LOC = isFreeForm detection + PositionInspectorSection mount + canvasDimensions prop + reorder Layer to after Chrome; `FocusBuilderInspector.tsx` +13 LOC = canvas-dimensions source from templateHook.template?.canvas_config with defensive default; `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` +329 LOC = 4 FF-6 integration tests). **Total LOC delta: ~953 LOC** — within the FF-6 budget midpoint (600-900) at the upper edge, well under worst-case (1,000-1,200). **`PositionInspectorSection.test.tsx` covers 13 cases**: 4-input render with labels, value reflection, onChange-does-not-commit, blur-commits, Enter-triggers-blur-commit, invalid-input-reverts-silently, disabled-when-null, disabled-when-core, X-clamp-to-canvas-bound, Width-clamp-to-min, X-clamp-to-0-on-negative, **focus-preservation when placement changes during focused edit (load-bearing UX correctness)**, sync-when-not-focused. **`FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` extended with 4 FF-6 integration tests** following the operator-observable cross-side canon (2026-05-20 late evening): (a) **Test A — inspector X input commit moves widget on canvas + persists via PUT**: select widget → find `position-input-x` → change value to "200" → blur → after 500ms debounce assert PUT body has `placement.x === 200` AND y/width/height unchanged AND inline `left: 200px` on the rendered draggable wrapper AND `top: 100px` unchanged.  via inspector buttons AND right-click context menu (third operator-interactive FF sub-arc; first right-click context menu in Focus Builder).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `c5d71c7` (FF-4). After FF-5 ships, operators control widget layering via four actions (Bring to front / Bring forward / Send backward / Send to back) accessible from two surfaces per Q-31 (c): (a) `LayerInspectorSection` — a new 2x2 button grid mounted inside `WidgetInspectorSection` between the Placement and Chrome sections; (b) `CanvasContextMenu` — the first right-click context menu in Focus Builder, portal-rendered into `document.body` with `position: fixed` at the cursor coordinates. Both surfaces dispatch through the new `templateHook.setWidgetZIndex(placementId, action)` helper which routes through the existing FF-1 `updateWidget` mutator (the `z_index` field was already in the positioning-keys split, so no positioning-pipeline changes were required). Z-order math lives in the new pure helper `computeZIndexCommit({currentPlacement, allPlacements, action})` — fourth pure-helper in the FF series after `computeFreeFormDropPosition` (FF-2), `computeDragMoveCommit` (FF-3), and `computeResizeCommit` (FF-4), all four sharing the same shape: immutable input → next-state output, no React, no DOM, no @dnd-kit. Semantics: front = `max(others.z_index) + 1` (or `1` if no others); back = `min(others.z_index) - 1` (or `-1` if no others); forward = `current + 1`; backward = `current - 1`. Undefined z_index treated as 0. The helper filters `currentPlacement` out of `allPlacements` by id before computing max/min so a target at z=5 doesn't compute max against itself. **Inherited-core exclusion happens at the caller level** (hook helper `setWidgetZIndex`), NOT in the pure function — keeps the helper agnostic to "what is a widget vs. what is core" (that's policy). Inspection of `rowsDraft` confirms the core is rendered externally by `WidgetFreeFormLayer` and is NEVER present in `rowsDraft.placements`, so the hook helper simply uses every flattened placement as `allPlacements` — no explicit filter needed. Q-22 + structural-immutability canon honored: core is not a z-order target. **Right-click on core no-ops correctly** — the canonical core is rendered by `WidgetFreeFormLayer`'s anchored core card (a separate `<div data-testid="focus-builder-core-placement">`), not via `FreeFormPlacedWidget`; the `onContextMenu` handler only attaches to free-form widget wrappers, so right-clicking the core surfaces the browser's native context menu rather than ours. Selection-model preservation (Q-7-adjacent): right-click does NOT change the operator's current selection — the `handleContextMenu` handler calls `preventDefault()` + `stopPropagation()` + forwards to the parent, but does NOT call `onSelect`. Left-click selection model continues to own selection state; right-click acts on the right-clicked target regardless. Mirrors Figma / Sketch precedent. Verified via dedicated unit test on `FreeFormPlacedWidget`. **F-3 drag + F-4 resize + F-3.1c chrome editing all continue working unchanged** — context-menu `onContextMenu` handler is declared AFTER the `{...attributes}` spread per the FF-4 plumbing-surprise canon (May 2026: @dnd-kit's spread can overwrite explicit props if they come before), so it can't be overwritten by dnd-kit's attribute set; drag listeners + a11y keyboard bindings retain their full surface area. **CanvasContextMenu's plumbing surprises**: 1 minor — `createPortal` into `document.body` was the cleanest way to escape any overflow:hidden canvas clipping; `position: fixed` + cursor coordinates renders the menu reliably at the viewport coord pair the operator clicked. Document-level `mousedown` + `keydown` listeners attach only while `isOpen` is true (the effect's `if (!isOpen) return` short-circuit means the verify-against-pre-fix discipline could detect listener-leakage if it surfaced — covered by a unit test). Click-inside-menu does NOT call onClose via the outside-mousedown handler (the handler checks `menuRef.current.contains(target)`); option-click DOES call onClose via the option's own onClick handler (the menu closes on action click — explicit). 6 new files (`computeZIndexCommit.ts` 99 LOC, `computeZIndexCommit.test.ts` 218 LOC, `LayerInspectorSection.tsx` 120 LOC, `LayerInspectorSection.test.tsx` 64 LOC, `CanvasContextMenu.tsx` 176 LOC, `CanvasContextMenu.test.tsx` 152 LOC = **829 new LOC**). 11 modified files (`useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` +55 LOC = `setWidgetZIndex` helper + interface extension + 2-line type re-export; `useFocusTemplateDraft.test.tsx` +171 LOC = 6 FF-5 tests in a dedicated describe block; `WidgetInspectorSection.tsx` +21 LOC = LayerInspectorSection mount + import + prop; `FocusBuilderInspector.tsx` +3 LOC = wire `onSetWidgetZIndex` from hook; `FocusBuilderInspector.test.tsx` +1 LOC = stub `setWidgetZIndex: vi.fn()` on the mock; `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` +36 LOC = `onContextMenuRequest` prop + `handleContextMenu` + React import + comment block; `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` +90 LOC = 3 new context-menu tests; `WidgetFreeFormLayer.tsx` +11 LOC = thread `onContextMenuRequest` through; `FocusBuilderCanvas.tsx` +16 LOC = thread `onWidgetContextMenuRequest` through; `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` +62 LOC = context-menu state + handler trio + CanvasContextMenu render + close-on-subject-change effect; `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` +310 LOC = 4 FF-5 integration tests = **+773 / -3 LOC**). Total touched: **~1,602 LOC** — slightly over the 800-1,500 estimate's worst case due to comprehensive test coverage (39 new tests across the 6 surfaces) and clean prop plumbing through three layers (page → canvas → free-form-layer → free-form-widget). **`computeZIndexCommit.test.ts` covers 18 cases**: front (4 — multi, single, no-others, target-already-at-max), back (3 — multi, single, negative-others), forward (3 — positive/zero/negative), backward (2 — positive/zero), undefined-z (4 — front/back/forward/backward all coercing to 0), filter-current-from-others (2 — front + back ignore target's own z_index). **`LayerInspectorSection.test.tsx` 4 cases**: 4-button render, action dispatch per button, disabled-on-null, disabled-on-isCore. **`CanvasContextMenu.test.tsx` 8 cases**: hidden when isOpen=false, all four options render when open, each option fires onAction + onClose, Escape closes, click-outside closes, click-inside does NOT trigger outside-handler onClose, position prop maps to inline style, listeners NOT attached when isOpen=false. **Hook `setWidgetZIndex` tests (6 cases)**: front updates target to max+1, back updates to min-1, forward increments, backward decrements, non-existent-id is no-op, debounced-save PUT body carries updated z_index. **`FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` extended with 3 FF-5 tests**: right-click fires `onContextMenuRequest` with placement id + viewport cursor coords, right-click does NOT change selection (selection-model preservation), no callback prop = no-throw + native menu defaults. **`FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` extended with 4 FF-5 integration tests** following the Q-40 operator-observable cross-side canon: (a) inspector "Bring to front" button — left-click widget A's inner core to select → click `layer-action-front` → after 500ms debounce assert PUT body has widget A z_index=1 and widget B z_index=0 AND inline `z-index: 1` on the rendered draggable wrapper of widget A AND `z-index: 0` on widget B; (c) click-outside closes menu — `fireEvent.contextMenu` opens, `fireEvent.mouseDown(document.body)` closes, no PUT fires; (d) Escape closes menu — opens via right-click, `fireEvent.keyDown(document, {key: 'Escape'})` closes, no PUT fires. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied per the 2026-05-20 late-evening canon refinement**: pass 1 — reverting `setWidgetZIndex` to a `return` no-op causes integration tests (a) inspector and (b) context menu to FAIL on both render-side (`z-index: 1` regex doesn't match) AND save-side (`update` not called); (b) The `LayerInspectorSection` initially imported `* as React` to use the namespace, which violated `noUnusedLocals` since I switched the implementation to only consume lucide icons + the bare types; dropped the import, kept the named lucide imports. **Right-click context menu substrate composed cleanly as precedent for FF-7 multi-select align** — the `CanvasContextMenu` component's API surface (`isOpen` + `position` + `onClose` + `onAction`) generalizes naturally: future multi-select align would dispatch a different action vocabulary (left / center / right / top / middle / bottom) into the same surface, OR a separate menu instance can mount alongside following the same portal + position-fixed pattern. - **2026-05-20 — Sub-arc FF-4 shipped (uncommitted) — Resize-to-resize via 8 handles + selection-conditional overlay + per-handle clamped commit (second operator-interactive FF sub-arc).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `63ecd7b` (FF-3). After FF-4 ships, operators can resize free-form widgets via 8 handles (4 corners + 4 edges) that appear when the widget is selected; resize commits debounced-save through FF-1's positioning-field-routing path on `updateWidget`. Architecture follows the canonical "core-plus-accessories" Figma/Sketch precedent: `ResizeHandleOverlay` is a SIBLING of `PlacedWidgetCore` inside the FF-3 draggable wrapper, NOT a child of the core. Sibling layering keeps drag-whole-widget vs. manipulate-specific-edge as event-target-separate gestures. Each of the 8 handles is its own `useDraggable` with id `<placementId>-handle-<position>` (positions: nw / n / ne / w / e / sw / s / se). `FocusBuilderPage.handleDragEnd` extended with an FF-4 branch checked BEFORE the FF-3 move branch (handle ids share the placement id prefix): `parseResizeHandleId(active.id)` → lookup placement via `flattenFreeFormPlacements(rowsDraft)` → resolve registry min via `getFreeFormMinDimensions(widget_slug)` (Q-13 80×40 platform fallback) → resolve canvas via `canvas_config` with 1200×800 fallback → call new pure helper `computeResizeCommit(...)` → fire `templateHook.updateWidget(id, { x, y, width, height })`. Per-handle math: e/s expand the right/bottom edge (x or y unchanged); w/n anchor the opposite edge (x or y adjusts inversely so the right/bottom edge stays put); nw/ne/sw/se compose corner cases. Clamping order locked at `computeResizeCommit.ts`: (1) per-handle delta application, (2) min-dimension clamp with opposite-edge anchoring for w/n/nw/sw/ne, (3) canvas-bounds clamp — when crossing the bound on a left/top-moving handle, x/y snap to 0 and width/height widen to anchor the original right/bottom edge (faithful to Figma; verified via integration test with widget at x=0). Aspect-ratio preservation NOT implemented in FF-4 (deferred to FF-7 polish per locked decisions). Visual treatment: 8×8 px white squares with 1px accent border, positioned with `-4px` offset so they center on the parent FreeFormPlacedWidget's edges/corners; per-position cursor (`nw-resize` / `n-resize` / etc.) signals motion axis. Each handle is `pointer-events: auto` so it receives events through the `pointer-events: none` overlay parent (CSS pointer-events non-inheritance contract); also keyboard-focusable (`tabIndex=0`) per Q-40 KeyboardSensor mitigation. `aria-label="Resize <position>"` for a11y. Selection-conditional render: `{selected ? <ResizeHandleOverlay placementId={placement.id} /> : null}` in `FreeFormPlacedWidget` — handles ONLY render when selected (canonical Figma/Sketch UX; matches Q-10 lock). 2 new pure helpers + 2 new components + 2 unit-test files + 2 edited integration tests. `computeResizeCommit.test.ts` covers **32 cases** organized as 8 per-handle describes + 6 min-dimension clamp cases + 6 canvas-bounds clamp cases + 8 zero-delta no-ops + nw corner double-anchor + se corner double-clamp. `ResizeHandleOverlay.test.tsx` (10 cases) verifies 8-handle render + position attrs + per-handle cursor at the operator-observable element + aria-labels + tabIndex + pointer-events:auto + corner positioning + id roundtrip helpers + non-handle id rejection + dash-containing placement ids. `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` extended with 2 conditional-render assertions: 8 handles when selected, zero handles when not selected. `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` extended with **4 FF-4 integration tests** driving the @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor path per Q-40 (JSDOM mitigation reuses FF-3's exact pattern: focus the handle, fire Space on the activator, advance fake timers ~10ms, dispatch arrows on document, advance, Space to commit on document, advance debounce 500ms, assert PUT body + render-side inline style): (a) e handle widens width via render + PUT (asserts `placement.width > 240` AND inline `width: <N>px` where N > 240 AND x/y unchanged); (b) w handle adjusts x as width grows with right edge anchored (asserts `placement.x + placement.width === 640` — original right edge preserved); (c) w handle at x=0 clamps to 0 and widens to original right edge per Q-14 (asserts `placement.x === 0 && placement.width === 240`); (d) e handle shrinking past today-pin-widget's declared min 120×64 clamps at 120 per Q-13. Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied: forcing the FF-4 dispatch to no-op (`if (handleParsed) return` early-out before commit) fails ALL 4 integration tests (save side: `update` not called past the FF-3 debounce; render side: inline `width` unchanged from 240) — restored → all 4 pass. Operator-observable canon honored on every integration assertion — assertions target `placement.width / .height / .x / .y` in the PUT body AND the wrapper's inline style at the rendered `focus-builder-freeform-placed-widget-draggable` (not a wrapper-internal attribute) per the 2026-05-20 late-evening canon refinement. Cross-side data↔render integration canon honored: the e-handle integration test asserts both the save-side PUT body AND the render-side inline `width` value advanced past 240. Registry min lookup discovered already-shipped at `getFreeFormMinDimensions(slug)` in FF-2's introspection helpers — no registry extension needed; today-pin-widget already declares `freeFormMinDimensions: { width: 120, height: 64 }`. `auto-register` registry import added to `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` so widget-slug lookups resolve in the JSDOM context (FF-3's selection-test-only path didn't need this; FF-4's min-clamp assertion does). - **2026-05-20 — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed architectural canon distinguishing Monitor canvas (grid model, F-series canonical) from Decide canvas (free-form model, FF-series upcoming)** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. One entry appended to `DECISIONS.md`. The three-primitive decomposition (Spaces=Monitor, Command Bar=Act, Focus=Decide) translates into distinct canvas substrates. Monitor canvas (Pulse/dashboards/anomaly surfaces) uses grid model (12-column row-based placement) — F-series established this canonically; structured composability across high variability is the load-bearing constraint enabling dashboard patterns to transfer across tenants. Decide canvas (Focus instances) uses free-form model (per-placement x/y/width/height + z-index) — operator-driven flexibility within decision scope is the load-bearing constraint enabling per-decision workspace manipulation. F-series's canonical decisions (placement structural immutability, unified-placement model, ≥3 configurableProps registry contract) remain valid for Monitor canvas; widget placements on Decide canvas adopt their own positioning shape. Cores remain anchored at canonical positions on both canvas types; free-form positioning applies to widgets only. Per-Focus free-form doesn't break cross-tenant coherence because it's bounded by the operator's decision scope, not a shared dashboard pattern. Next arc: investigation locking free-form substrate's architectural questions (positioning units, canvas dimensions, z-index model, snap behavior, resize constraints, persistence shape, adapter extension, inherited-core anchoring, multi-select). - **2026-05-19 (late evening / F-4.1) — Sub-arc F-4.1 shipped (uncommitted): typography preset chip clicks visibly re-render** — Tight fix arc closing F-4's typography render bug. F-4 shipped the theme picker; substrate chip clicks visibly updated the canvas (via substrate-resolver's `if (view.preset === "morning-warm")` branch coincidentally producing structurally different CSS); typography chip clicks saved correctly to backend but produced no visible render change because `typography-resolver.ts:expandTypographyPreset` only applies preset defaults when specific fields (heading_weight, body_weight, color tokens) are null. F-4's chip onClick fired only `{ preset: <slug> }` — pre-existing scrubbed specifics stayed at their values; resolver's specifics-win path returned unchanged output. Bug only surfaces when specifics have been authored (non-null); from an empty template all specifics are null so the chip click coincidentally works — which is why F-4's existing render-side assertion (canvas inline-style attribute string change) passed false-positive: typography updates surface as CSS custom properties on the canvas wrapper that change with state regardless of resolver output. **Fix shape**: chip onClick fires preset + nullified specifics. **F-2 inspector audit outcome**: C-1 SubstratePresetPicker + TypographyPresetPicker primitives are "dumb" (emit `slug | null` via onChange); bug lives at the consumer's onChange handler. F-2 inspector has the same bug pattern at `FocusBuilderInspector.tsx:407-409` (substrate) and `:491-493` (typography). Per canon — "chip click is operator-intent 'apply preset wholesale'" — fix applies symmetrically to BOTH theme picker (F-4) AND F-2 inspector. Specific-field scrubbing via ScrubbableButton / TokenSwatchPicker below the chip continues to take priority (resolver's specifics-win path is correct for fine-grained scrubbing). - **2026-05-19 (late evening) — F-3.1c shipped (uncommitted): widget canvas wrapper applies chrome via resolver** — Closes the render-side gap in F-3 + F-3.1b. - **2026-05-19 (PM) — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed six architectural canon entries from F-3.1a + F-3.1a.2** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. (3) "Ordinary template updates version-bump by default; session-aware mutate-in-place is the exception" — `update_template` has two paths (default version-bump deactivates prior + creates new row + new id; session-aware fast path mutates in place when token + window match); template_ids are inherently unstable across version-bumps. (4) "URL stability for versioned entities requires slug-based addressing as long-term canonical pattern" — F-3.1a.2 symptom fix (URL recovery on 410-retry) is current handling; slug-based addressing (`(template_slug, scope, vertical)` tuple) is the structural answer for Page/Document/Workflow Builders. (5) "GET-on-inactive 200 + version-bump-on-every-save = silent staleness without URL discipline" — interaction-canon entry; neither backend policy is wrong alone, but their combination requires frontend URL discipline as the integration layer. (6) "Callback-ref pattern extends multi-hook-mount canon to consumer callbacks" — F-3.1a.2's `onActiveTemplateIdChangeRef` pattern; ref-as-dominant-defense discipline (C-2.1.4 + C-2.2b) generalizes from internal state to consumer-supplied callbacks. Active arc → no active arc, canon update only. **Files modified**: `DECISIONS.md` (+~155 lines, format matches existing F-series canon entries verbatim — prose-paragraph, date-prefixed with `(PM)` disambiguator, inline `code`, `---` separator, "Implication for future arcs" section per entry), `STATE.md` (this entry).
