- **2026-05-19 — Sub-arc F-3.1a.2 shipped (uncommitted) — URL recovery on 410-retry** — Follow-on to F-3.1a. After F-3.1a's adapter resolved the 422 errors, operator-visible "widget config props don't persist across refresh" surfaced. **Diagnosis**: URL staleness + first-save-in-session version-bumps. Fresh page load with URL `?subject=template:<old-id>`. First save in session: (1) PUT against URL's `<old-id>`; (2) backend's session-aware fast path doesn't fire (prior session's session-id stamp on the row defeats `_within_template_edit_session` at `focus_templates_service.py:685-695`); (3) backend version-bumps — deactivates prior, creates new active row with new id; (4) backend returns 410 with `active_template_id` in detail; (5) hook's 410-retry swaps `activeTemplateIdRef.current` to new id + retries PUT; (6) retry returns 200; data persists. **But URL still points at the deactivated id.** On refresh, hook GETs deactivated id, backend returns 200 with inactive snapshot (predates operator's saves), refresh appears to wipe values. Subsequent saves within same session work correctly (mutate-in-place via session-aware fast path). Bug only fires across refresh boundaries. **Fix**: hook exposes new `onActiveTemplateIdChange?: (newId: string) => void` callback option; fires on successful 410-retry when the resolved id differs from the consumer's bound `templateId`. `FocusBuilderPage` consumes the callback and rewrites URL via `setSearchParams({ subject: template:${newId} }, { replace: true })`. `{ replace: true }` mandatory — prevents history bloat per version-bump. **Locked decisions honored**: Option 1 URL update on retry-success is canonical fix (#1, slug-based URLs deferred); callback signature `onActiveTemplateIdChange?: (newId: string) => void` (#2); fires only on actual id change (#3); no backend changes (#4); no session-aware fast path fixes (#5 — separate future arc); no URL contract change (#6); no F-3.1a adapter changes (#7). **Modified files**: `useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` — added `UseFocusTemplateDraftOptions` interface + optional second parameter; callback-ref pattern (`onActiveTemplateIdChangeRef`) mirrors existing ref discipline so the latest consumer callback is always called without closure capture and without polluting the `save` callback's deps; fired inside the 410-retry success path after `activeTemplateIdRef.current = updated.id` and ONLY when `updated.id !== templateId` (the consumer's URL-bound id). `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` — added `handleActiveTemplateIdChange` callback (mirrors existing `handleSelectSubject` `setSearchParams` pattern but with `{ replace: true }`); passed to `useFocusTemplateDraft` via new options object. **Tests added**: 4 hook unit tests (`F-3.1a.2 onActiveTemplateIdChange` describe block — fires-with-new-id on retry success, does-NOT-fire on direct 200, does-not-throw when option absent, does-NOT-fire when retry resolves back to original templateId per defensive same-id check) + 1 integration test in `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (`F-3.1a.2 — URL recovers to active template id when initial save 410s` — full operator-flow: stale URL → page renders canvas in template mode → click canvas → click substrate preset pill → debounced save fires → first PUT 410s → retry resolves against tpl-1-v2 → URL rewritten → hook re-fetches against new id via subsequent `focusTemplatesService.get` call against `tpl-1-v2`). **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied** per Step 4: commented out URL-update wiring in `FocusBuilderPage` (replaced 2-line callback wiring with bare `const templateHook = useFocusTemplateDraft(templateSubjectId)`) → integration test failed at the `focusTemplatesService.get` waitFor asserting against `tpl-1-v2` (URL stayed at `tpl-1`, hook never re-fetched against the new id) → restored verbatim. **Tests**: 4 new hook unit + 1 new page integration = **5 new tests**. Full vitest **209 files / 2844 tests + 1 todo passing** (+4 tests vs F-3.1a baseline 2840); 1 failing test is the pre-existing flaky `Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx` chrome-preset-live-cascade documented across multiple arcs (not introduced by F-3.1a.2). tsc clean (`npx tsc -b` per F-1 lesson); vite build 5.06s; bundle **6,080,410 bytes vs F-3.1a baseline 6,080,090 = +320 / +0.005%** (well within ±0.5% per F-3.1a.2 gate). Backend `test_focus_template_inheritance_e1_defaults.py` + `test_verticals.py` + `test_focus_template_f3_1a_adapter_contract.py` 44/44 green (no backend changes — F-3.1a.2 is pure frontend). **LOC**: production ~25 (hook callback-ref + retry-path fire site + options interface; page callback wiring) + tests ~75 (4 hook unit + 1 page integration) ≈ **~100 total**, comfortably under the ~100-200 midpoint band. **Architectural questions surfaced during build**: (a) callback wiring matched hook's existing prop pattern cleanly — adding an optional second parameter with a callback-ref dispatch mirrors the existing `templateId`/`editSessionId` discipline; no restructuring needed. (b) integration test exercised full operator-flow page → hook → adapter → mocked retry → URL update — substrate-preset pill click was the simplest reliable save trigger that doesn't depend on drag-drop infrastructure; 300ms debounce naturally completes within waitFor's default timeout (test uses 2000ms timeout for safety against CI flake). (c) Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied successfully — pre-fix variant failed at the URL-update assertion; restoring the 2-line callback wiring restored green. (d) Bundle delta +320 bytes / +0.005% well within ±0.5% tolerance; F-3.1a baseline+1280 → F-3.1a.2 baseline+320 reflects the callback-ref + options interface being minimal-overhead additions. (e) Existing `FocusBuilderPage` URL-update mechanism reused verbatim — `setSearchParams(params, { replace: true })` matches the pattern already used by `handleSelectSubject` modulo the `replace` flag (`false` for tree-clicks, `true` for version-bump recovery). No new URL primitives, no new search-param parsing. (f) Architectural note: the underlying session-aware fast path bug (first save in session always defeats `_within_template_edit_session` because of the prior session-id stamp) is intentionally out of scope per locked decision #5 — F-3.1a.2 solves operator-visible symptom regardless. Future arc may fix the backend fast path to skip the version-bump entirely on session resume, at which point F-3.1a.2's URL-recovery becomes inert (no harm — callback simply doesn't fire). **No backend changes, no migrations, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, no C-1 primitives modified, no other hook contracts altered beyond `useFocusTemplateDraft`'s new optional second parameter, no resolver internals touched, no adapter changes (F-3.1a canonical), no canvas/inspector/palette changes (F-3 + F-3.1a behavior preserved), no Chrome section UI (F-3.1b territory), no theme picker (F-4), no breadcrumb (F-5).** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Next**: F-3.1b (Chrome section addition + further inspector polish on top of the now-persistent + URL-recoverable widget state).

- **2026-05-19 — Sub-arc F-3.1a shipped (uncommitted) — frontend placement-shape adapter (Path A)** — First half of the F-3.1 fix split following the F-3.1 surface-and-stop. Resolves the frontend↔backend wire-shape mismatch that caused F-3-placed widgets to persist as backend-validation no-ops + disappear after refresh. **Diagnosis**: hook's typed view (`WidgetPlacement`: `id` / `widget_slug` / `column_start` 1-indexed / `column_span` / `chrome`) sent over the wire was rejected by `_validate_placement` in `backend/app/services/focus_template_inheritance/focus_templates_service.py` (requires `placement_id` string + `component_kind` + `component_name` + `starting_column` 0-indexed; rejects everything else as `InvalidTemplateShape`). Backend persisted nothing; GET returned prior server state; refresh wiped the widget. **Path A locked**: frontend adapter at hook boundary; backend schema unchanged (the canonical `component_kind`+`component_name` shape correctly serves cores AND widgets — frontend's `widget_slug` is a widget-narrowed authoring convenience the adapter widens on save and re-narrows on load). **Consumer audit (Step 1)**: 4 focus-builder consumers (`FocusBuilderCanvas`, `WidgetInspectorSection`, `FocusBuilderPage`, `useFocusTemplateDraft.test`) all read frontend shape from `templateHook.rowsDraft` — the hook is the sole entry point. The separate `composition-canvas/` module (Visual Editor compositions) already uses backend shape (`placement_id`). Adapter location: **hook-level** (option i). Service-level (option ii) would either double-translate for composition-canvas or force type widening that breaks it. **Backend chrome storage path (Step 1e)**: `_validate_placement` declares `prop_overrides` (validated as `dict` at lines 214-219) as the per-placement config field — semantically identical to frontend's per-placement `chrome` blob (per-placement prop overrides written by `WidgetInspectorSection.onUpdateWidget(id, { [key]: v })` at line 103; read at line 101 as `placement.chrome?.[key]`). Adapter maps `chrome ↔ prop_overrides` 1:1. Configurable props (Q5) live INSIDE the chrome blob, so they flow through the same translation — **F-3.1a fixes configurable-props persistence as a side effect of fixing widget placement persistence**, same code path, same bug. **Field mapping** (both directions): `id↔placement_id`, `widget_slug→component_name`+`component_kind:"widget"`, `column_start↔starting_column` (1-indexed↔0-indexed — adapter subtracts 1 on save, adds 1 on load), `column_span` unchanged, `chrome↔prop_overrides` (omitted on send when empty, defaults to `{}` on load when absent). **New files**: `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/hooks/_placement-adapter.ts` (8 exported helpers — `frontendToBackendPlacement` / `backendToFrontendPlacement` / `frontendToBackendRow` / `backendToFrontendRow` / `frontendToBackendRows` / `backendToFrontendRows` + `BackendPlacement` / `BackendRow` / `BackendRowsBlob` types; ~165 LOC including module-header diagnosis paragraph + chrome-storage-audit comment + canonical mapping table). `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/hooks/_placement-adapter.test.ts` (~245 LOC; 23 unit tests across 4 describe blocks — frontend→backend field mapping (8 tests including off-by-one verification at `column_start=1→starting_column=0` and `column_start=5→starting_column=4` + clamp-at-0 defensive case + empty-chrome omits prop_overrides), backend→frontend field mapping (8 tests including legacy-input tolerance for stale frontend-shape JSONB still in DB), roundtrip preservation (2 tests both directions), row-level adapters (5 tests including null/undefined input tolerance + missing-column_count default to 12)). `backend/tests/test_focus_template_f3_1a_adapter_contract.py` (~210 LOC; Path Y per Step 5 — imports REAL `_validate_rows` + `_validate_placement` from `app.services.focus_template_inheritance.focus_templates_service` and exercises against fixtures shaped exactly like `frontendToBackendRows` emits; **6 tests** across 2 classes — `TestFrontendAdapterOutputValidates` × 4 (single addWidget output validates, widget+chrome output validates, multi-widget different-column output validates, `starting_column + column_span ≤ column_count` invariant explicitly verified) + `TestPreAdapterShapeRejected` × 2 (frontend-shape with `id` not `placement_id` rejected; frontend-shape missing `component_kind` rejected — these tests positively assert the canonical bug surface, so if backend validation is ever weakened to accept frontend shape the test fires before the architectural drift ships). **Modified files**: `useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` — load path's `rec.rows ?? []` cast-through-unknown replaced with `backendToFrontendRows(rec.rows ?? [])`; save body's `rowsRef.current` wrapped with `frontendToBackendRows(...)`; both save-response-echo paths (primary success + 410-retry success) updated to `backendToFrontendRows(updated.rows ?? [])`; net delta ~10 LOC + 4 explanatory comments anchoring the F-3.1a discipline; **no other behavior touched** — multi-hook-mount contract preserved, draftRef discipline preserved, 410-retry preserved, edit-session semantics preserved, dirty-state OR-of-4 preserved, debounced save unchanged, discard unchanged. `useFocusTemplateDraft.test.tsx` — added new test `F-3.1a — load adapts canonical backend shape to frontend view` (load-side verify-against-pre-fix; mock returns backend-shape `placement_id` / `component_name` / `starting_column=4`; asserts hook surfaces `id="w-canonical"` / `widget_slug="day-strip-widget"` / `column_start=5` / `chrome={daysVisible:7}`); updated existing stale-closure regression test's payload assertion from `chrome.elevation` to `prop_overrides.elevation` (the test now correctly asserts the canonical wire shape post-adapter — payload IS backend-shape after `frontendToBackendRows`). **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied for BOTH adapter wirings** per Step 6: (a) **load-side** — commented out `backendToFrontendRows(...)` call in load path → new test fails with `p.id === undefined` / `widget_slug === undefined` / `column_start === undefined` / `chrome === undefined` → restored; (b) **save-side** — commented out `frontendToBackendRows(...)` wrap in save body assembly (cast-through-unknown preserved type clean) → stale-closure regression test fails with `payload.rows[0].placements[0].prop_overrides?.elevation === undefined` (because pre-fix payload has `chrome.elevation` instead) → restored; (c) **backend save-side contract** — `TestPreAdapterShapeRejected` × 2 prove backend `_validate_rows` rejects pre-adapter shape (frontend `id` / missing `component_kind`) with `InvalidTemplateShape` — this is the canonical evidence that without the adapter, the save would 422 at the backend boundary as F-3.1 diagnosed. **Tests**: 23 new adapter unit + 1 new load-side hook integration + 6 new backend real-contract integration = **30 new tests**. Full vitest **209 files / 2840 tests + 1 todo passing** (+1 file / +25 tests vs F-3 baseline 208/2815); previously-flaky `Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx` passed cleanly in this run (still considered known-flaky per cross-arc history). Full backend focus-template suite **93 tests passing** (87 prior + 6 new). tsc clean (`npx tsc -b` per F-1 lesson); vite build 5.45s; bundle **6,080,090 bytes vs F-3 baseline 6,078,810 = +1,280 / +0.02%** (well within ±1% per F-3.1a gate). **LOC**: production ~10 (hook wiring) + ~165 (adapter module) ≈ 175 production; tests ~245 (adapter) + ~40 (new hook test) + ~210 (backend contract) ≈ 495 tests; **~670 total**, well within ~300-500 midpoint to ~700 worst-case band. **Locked decisions honored**: Path A frontend adapter, NOT backend schema change (#1, #3); hook-level adapter location per consumer audit (#2); frontend `WidgetPlacement` type unchanged (#4); integration test mandatory + real-contract via `_validate_rows` direct import (#5, Path Y); chrome ↔ prop_overrides per Step 1e audit (#6); no Chrome section UI work (#7 — F-3.1b territory). **Architectural questions surfaced during build**: (a) integration test infrastructure — Path X (real HTTP test client exercising the hook against a live backend) does not exist in the codebase today and was out of scope to build; Path Y (backend pytest importing `_validate_rows` directly + asserting against canonical adapter output JSON fixtures) is the canonical contract gate until a hook-to-HTTP integration substrate exists. The fixtures in `test_focus_template_f3_1a_adapter_contract.py` are written to mirror `_placement-adapter.ts::frontendToBackendRows` output exactly; drift between the two surfaces as a backend test failure. (b) Configurable widget props (Q5 in the F-3.1 investigation) — confirmed they flow through the SAME adapter path as the placement shape itself because the inspector writes them into `placement.chrome` (which adapter maps to backend `prop_overrides`); F-3.1a fixes both simultaneously. No separate bug, no separate fix path needed. (c) Off-by-one column indexing — frontend hook code (`WidgetPlacement.column_start` comment line 50) explicitly documents 1-indexed; backend `_validate_placement` line 199 explicitly enforces `starting_column >= 0` (0-indexed); adapter subtracts 1 on send, adds 1 on load, clamps at 0 defensively. (d) Legacy JSONB tolerance — `backendToFrontendPlacement` accepts EITHER shape (canonical `placement_id` OR legacy `id` key) so existing template rows in the DB authored before F-3.1a (if any exist with frontend-shape JSONB stuck via direct DB writes or seed scripts) round-trip without loss; same tolerance on row shape (missing `column_count` defaults to 12). (e) Row-index pass-through — backend `_validate_rows` doesn't require or validate `row_index`; adapter preserves it for round-trip fidelity but treats it as inert metadata. (f) Adapter location decision was 100% evidence-based per Step 1 audit: focus-builder consumers all read from `rowsDraft` (hook state); composition-canvas/ consumers are a separate module already using backend shape; placing the adapter in the service would either double-translate or force type widening that breaks composition-canvas. **No backend changes, no migrations, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, no C-1 primitives modified, no C-2 hook contracts altered beyond adapter wiring at load+save boundaries, no resolver internals touched, no tier-aware editor surfaces modified, no VerticalGroupedTree changes, no InheritedCoreInspectorPanel changes, no focus-types.ts changes, no widget palette / canvas / drag-drop changes (F-3 behavior preserved verbatim — F-3.1a fixes ONLY the wire-shape mismatch), no Chrome section UI (F-3.1b territory), no theme picker (F-4), no breadcrumb / coexistence banner (F-5).** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Next**: F-3.1b (Chrome section addition + further inspector polish on top of the now-persistent widget state).

- **2026-05-19 — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed multi-hook-mount discovered canon from F-2 build** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. One entry appended to `DECISIONS.md`: "Multi-hook-mount pattern for builder UIs surfacing heterogeneous subjects". When a builder page renders one of N subject types (Focus Builder's `?subject=core:<id>` vs `?subject=template:<id>`), all N draft hooks mount unconditionally — each receiving real subject id when active, `null` when inactive. The component resolves `activeHook` from subject kind. Conditional mount would violate React rules-of-hooks; the unconditional-with-nullable-id pattern is canonically correct. Implication: draft hooks for builder consumption must accept `null | id` and short-circuit cleanly when null (no fetch, no save timers, sensible empty defaults). Hook authors must test the null case. Reference implementation: F-2's `FocusBuilderPage`. Pattern carries forward to F-3 (potential third widget hook), Page/Document/Workflow Builder. Active arc → no active arc, canon update only. **Files modified**: `DECISIONS.md` (+10 lines, format matches the two 2026-05-18 entries verbatim — prose-paragraph, date-prefixed, inline `code`), `STATE.md` (this entry). No code touched. No tests required.

future F-3 widget palette + F-5 polish may motivate extraction; (c) one-of-both-hooks mounted unconditionally — both `useFocusCoreDraft` AND `useFocusTemplateDraft` mount, each with `null | id` based on subject kind; the unbound hook is a no-op per the hook's own contract; alternative (Suspense or conditional hook mount) would violate React's rules-of-hooks; (d) the inspector's mode/empty + selection-kind dispatch is a 2×4 table; covered by the test matrix but worth keeping a close eye on as F-3 adds widget selection. **Next**: F-3 (widget palette + drag-to-canvas + accessory placement editing).

- **2026-05-18 — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed two discovered-canon entries from F-1 + F-1.1** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. Two entries appended to `DECISIONS.md`: (1) "Cores are canonical-shared-across-verticals" — `focus_cores` has no `vertical` field; vertical attribution in operator-facing surfaces (Focus Builder tree) is derived from inheriting templates (vertical_default templates pin core to vertical; platform_default makes cross-vertical; zero-template cores fall into "Unclassified"). Implication: future builder UIs (Page/Document/Workflow) must derive vertical placement from inheriting templates, not from non-existent core fields. (2) "Template vertical is design-time-permanent" — `focus_templates.vertical` is immutable through `update_template`; cross-vertical migration requires two-step pattern (deactivate at old vertical + create at new vertical), idempotent on subsequent runs. Implication: future UI surfaces must not expose "change vertical" as inline edit on a template — the operation is structurally a "create new in target + deactivate old" workflow. Reference impl: F-1.1's seed migration code at `backend/scripts/seed_focus_template_inheritance.py`. Active arc → no active arc, canon update only. **Files modified**: `DECISIONS.md` (+38 lines, format-adapted to match existing prose-paragraph + date-prefix style), `STATE.md` (this entry). No code files touched. No tests required.

- **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc F-1 shipped (uncommitted) — read-only Focus Builder shell + vertical-grouped tree + URL state** — First of 5 sub-arcs from the 2026-05-18 Focus Builder investigation. New route `/studio/builder/focuses` mounts a three-region layout (280px tree / flex canvas / 320px right rail) that hides the "Tier 1 vs Tier 2" mechanics from operators. Step 1+2 of the prompt were no-ops. **Spec-Override surfaced + resolved (focus_cores has no `vertical` field)**: the build prompt asked to "verify cores have a vertical field — likely it does." Verification: `backend/app/models/focus_core.py` exposes NO `vertical` column; `focus_templates.vertical` is the only vertical association (FK to verticals.slug, nullable). Resolution: F-1's `buildFocusBuilderTree` derives a core's vertical from its inheriting templates — vertical_default templates pin the core to their vertical; platform_default templates make the core "cross-vertical" (appears under every published vertical); cores with zero templates fall into the "Unclassified" pseudo-vertical at the bottom of the rail (Q-7 LOCKED behavior). This is the right F-1 behavior; F-2+ can refine if core-level `vertical` becomes a DB field. **Default expansion (Q-5)**: Studio active vertical comes from `readLastVertical()` (localStorage key `studio.lastVertical`) OR an explicit `studioActiveVertical` prop. Fallback: alphabetical-first published vertical (excluding "Unclassified"). Inside the active vertical, all focus-types start expanded; cores stay collapsed (per investigation lock). **URL contract**: `?subject=core:<id>` or `?subject=template:<id>` round-trips cleanly — page refresh loads the subject, auto-expands the parent trail in the tree, fires the service GET to populate the canvas placeholder. Empty subject → "Select a focus from the tree to preview." `?return_to=` preserved. **VerticalGroupedTree primitive contract verified consumer-opaque**: zero Focus-specific concepts in the primitive — no core/template/focus-type/scope chip references. Tree consumers (Page Builder, Document Builder, Workflow Builder per investigation §Pattern abstractions) can use the primitive directly with their own `groups: TreeNode[]` shape. `metadata` field is `Record<string, unknown>` — Focus Builder stuffs `{kind, subjectId, scope, parentCoreId}` there; primitive doesn't inspect. **FocusEditorPage coexistence verified**: 19/19 FocusEditorPage tests pass; route `/studio/focuses` still serves the tier-aware editor. **localStorage persistence**: write fires inside the React state updater function so reads after `fireEvent.click(chevron)` see the new value synchronously. **Tests**: 29 new tests (5 focus-types + 8 VerticalGroupedTree + 11 FocusBuilderTree (5 pure + 2 default-expansion + 4 integration) + 5 FocusBuilderPage). Full vitest **200 files / 2745 tests + 1 todo passing** (+5 files / +30 tests vs E-1.1 baseline 196/2715); 1 failing test is pre-existing flaky `Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx` `preview-card chrome preset updates live when chrome pill clicked` (documented in C-2.2b STATE entry as known flaky — passes in isolation, fails under parallel load). tsc clean; vite build 5.22s; bundle 6,051,950 bytes vs E-1.1 baseline 6,036,791 = **+15,159 / +0.25% (well within ±3% gate)**. Backend `test_verticals.py` 25/25 green (no backend changes — F-1 is pure frontend). **LOC**: production ~840 (focus-types 50 + VerticalGroupedTree 215 + FocusBuilderTree 410 + FocusBuilderPage 110 + FocusBuilderSelectionContext 40 + FocusBuilderCanvasPlaceholder 145 + FocusBuilderRightRailPlaceholder 20 + StudioShell modifications 10) + tests ~970 (focus-types 50 + VerticalGroupedTree 140 + FocusBuilderTree 365 + FocusBuilderPage 195 + misc 220) ≈ **~1,810 total**, squarely in the ~1,500–2,000 target midpoint, comfortably under worst-case 2,500. **No backend changes, no migrations, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, no tier-aware editor surfaces touched, no C-1 primitives modified, no C-2 hook contracts altered, no editing functionality of any kind (F-2 territory), no widget palette (F-3), no theme picker (F-4), no breadcrumb / coexistence banner / tree search (F-5).** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Locked decisions honored**: DB-backed verticals (Q-1 ✓ pre-existing), curated focus-type taxonomy (Q-2 ✓), frontend mapping table (Q-3 ✓), localStorage expansion (Q-4 ✓), Studio-active-vertical default expansion (Q-5 ✓), no tree search (Q-6 ✓ deferred), Other / Unclassified orphan handling (Q-7 ✓ via template-derived vertical), flat template list + scope chip (Q-8 ✓), Square / SquareDashed leaf icons + depth indent (Q-9 ✓), FocusBuilderSelectionContext colocated with root (Q-14 ✓), `builder-primitives/` + `focus-builder/` directory split (Q-38 ✓), `/studio/builder/focuses` route (Q-39 ✓), `?subject=` URL contract (Q-40 ✓), coexistence with FocusEditorPage (Q-41 ✓). **Architectural questions surfaced during build**: (a) focus_cores has no `vertical` column — resolved by template-derived vertical association; - **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc E-1.1 shipped (uncommitted) — E-1 verification follow-ups closed** — Post-E-1 visual verification surfaced two real findings the E-1 build missed. **Finding 1: scheduling-kanban-core chrome only partially canonical.** E-1 shipped delta updates (corner_radius 100→70, padding_token space-6→space-3, backdrop_blur 42→44) but preserved pre-E-1 values on the other four chrome fields: preset `card` (canonical: `frosted`), elevation 37 (canonical: 50), background_token `surface-elevated` (canonical: `surface-frosted`), border_token `None` (canonical: `border-subtle`). E-1.1 re-seeds with FULL canonical chrome state — all 7 fields explicit — bumping core to v9. **Finding 2: Tier 1 editor preview pane atmosphere not mockup-canonical.** Pre-E-1.1 the canvas painted a warm-amber/copper diagonal gradient (`linear-gradient(135deg, #f9d9a6 0%, #e9b27e 30%, #c97d52 60%, #9C5640 100%)`) plus a 30%-opacity 45° repeating stripe overlay — Tier 1 editor chrome that diverged from the canonical mockup. Replaced with the four-layer canonical mockup composition: three radial gradients (warm cream rgba(252,220,180,0.55) at 15%/10%, soft pink rgba(220,170,200,0.40) at 85%/15%, cool blue rgba(180,200,220,0.45) at 50%/90%) over a vertical linear-gradient base (`#f7ebe0 → #f0dfd0`). Hardcoded directly on the editor's preview pane — NOT routed through substrate-resolver (locked decision 2: Tier 1 cores have no substrate vocabulary). Values mirror substrate-resolver's `morning-warm` preset at intensity 100 so operator-facing + admin-facing surfaces feel canon-matched; diagonal-stripe overlay removed for canonical fidelity. **(1) Seed re-shipped with full canonical chrome state** — `backend/scripts/seed_focus_template_inheritance.py`: SCHEDULING_KANBAN_CORE.chrome now specifies all 7 fields explicitly (`preset: "frosted", elevation: 50, corner_radius: 70, backdrop_blur: 44, background_token: "surface-frosted", border_token: "border-subtle", padding_token: "space-3"`). Drift-tolerant `_seed_core` detects content divergence and calls `update_core` to version-bump existing rows; previous v8 record preserved as `is_active=false`. **(2) Tier-2 template version-bump on stale core pin** — `_seed_template` extended with a new "force version-bump when `inherits_from_core_version` lags live core version" path. Rationale: `update_template` preserves the prior `inherits_from_core_version` (immutable through that surface — service-layer captures from the live active core only on `create_template`). The resolver always uses the active core regardless (locked decision 2), but C-2.3's lineage chrome reads `template.inherits_from_core_version` directly, so a stale stamp would display as "v1" in the editor even after the core moves to v9. The new branch calls `create_template` to trigger a version-bump that restamps `inherits_from_core_version` to live core.version on the deactivate-and-insert path. Idempotent: subsequent reruns short-circuit because the stamp matches. **(3) Tier 1 editor canvas atmosphere canonicalized** — `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/visual-editor/Tier1CoresEditor.tsx`: preview-pane `<section data-testid="tier1-preview">` `background` style replaced with the four-layer canonical composition; diagonal-stripe `<div aria-hidden>` overlay deleted; `isolation: isolate` added so the canvas establishes its own stacking context. Inline-style approach is deliberate per locked decision 2 (Tier 1 has no substrate vocabulary). **(4) Canonical mockup committed** — new `docs/design/canonical-mockups/funeral_scheduling_apple_pre_liquid_glass.html` (a self-contained four-column kanban skeleton with frosted cards demonstrating the substrate + chrome + typography canon, no build step, opens directly in a browser) + `docs/design/canonical-mockups/README.md` explaining the canonical-mockup convention. Authoritative reference for the morning-warm substrate composition, frosted chrome preset values, and frosted-text typography preset values — referenced by E-1 and E-1.1. **Tests**: new `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/visual-editor/Tier1CoresEditor.test.tsx` (2 tests) asserts the four-layer canonical composition is present on the canvas + the pre-E-1.1 warm-amber gradient is absent (JSDom normalizes hex to rgb so assertions check both normalized stops `rgb(247, 235, 224)` / `rgb(240, 223, 208)` and explicit hex absence). **Gates**: full vitest **196 files / 2715 tests + 1 todo passing** (+1 file / +2 tests vs E-1's 195/2713); tsc clean; vite build 4.98s, bundle unchanged within ±2%. Backend 264/264 across 9 focus_template_inheritance test files (full backend suite green). **LOC**: ~115 changed (seed ~50 net delta with new version-bump branch + comment block; Tier1CoresEditor ~25 (canvas style replace + overlay delete); new test file ~80; mockup HTML ~210 + README ~22 = docs ~232) — well under the ~300-600 midpoint, comfortably under 900 worst case. **No backend service changes, no schema changes, no migrations, no resolver module changes, no Tier 2 editor surfaces touched, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, Frosted Scribe not touched per locked decision 7.** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Locked decisions honored**: full canonical chrome state replacement (#1); editor preview pane canonical composition hardcoded, NOT routed through substrate-resolver (#2); scheduling-fh `inherits_from_core_version` auto-bumps to new active version via the new seed branch (#3); substrate-resolver morning-warm unchanged (#4); no backend schema or migration (#5); resolver modules untouched (#6); Frosted Scribe not touched (#7); canonical mockup HTML committed (#8). **Open architectural question surfaced**: the `_seed_template` version-bump branch is a workaround for `update_template` preserving the prior `inherits_from_core_version` — clean long-term path is either (a) extending `update_template` to optionally restamp from live core, or (b) adding a dedicated `restamp_core_version_pin` service. Not blocking; the seed-only workaround is correct for E-1.1's surface but if multiple templates inherit from the same core in future, each will need a similar code path. **Next**: full Focus Builder UI restructuring (vertical-grouped left rail nav, selection-driven inspector, widget palette, theme preset switcher in right rail, breadcrumb context, right-bar cleanup, drag widgets into Tier 2, Tier 3 work) — explicitly out of scope for E-1.1.

- **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc E-1 shipped (uncommitted) — mockup-canonical-defaults arc closed** — Post-C-2 verification revealed three findings: (1) Tier 2 templates didn't inherit Tier 1's exact look on creation — substrate-resolver's `morning-warm` preset at intensity 70 produced a flat cream wash rather than the canonical warm sunrise gradient; (2) Tier 1 scheduling-kanban-core chrome diverged from mockup card chrome (corner_radius 37 / padding_token space-6 / no backdrop_blur vs. mockup 70 / space-3 / 44); (3) new Tier 2 templates via the C-2.2c modal started with empty substrate/typography rather than canonical mockup defaults. E-1 closes all three. **(1) Substrate-resolver morning-warm canonical** — `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/lib/visual-editor/substrate-resolver.ts`: `morning-warm` preset rebuilt as a four-layer composition. Three radial gradients (warm cream `rgba(252, 220, 180, α)` ellipse-at-15%-10%; pink `rgba(220, 170, 200, α)` ellipse-at-85%-15%; cool blue `rgba(180, 200, 220, α)` ellipse-at-50%-90%) over a token-bindable linear-gradient base (`accent_token_1` top stop → `base_token` bottom stop; default `surface-elevated` → `surface-base`). Radial alphas at intensity 100 are canonical 0.55 / 0.40 / 0.45; intensity scales linearly to 0 (no radials). Radial colors, positions, ellipse sizes are HARDCODED — not operator-tunable. `accent_token_2` is unused for morning-warm. SUBSTRATE_PRESETS entry updated: `intensity: 100` default + `base_token: surface-base` + `accent_token_1: surface-elevated` + `accent_token_2: null`. Other presets preserve the legacy two-stop diagonal composition via fall-through branch. Resolver function signature unchanged (`resolveSubstrateStyle(view, tokens) → CSSProperties`). **(2) Backend create-time defaults** — new `backend/app/services/focus_template_inheritance/defaults.py` canonicalizes `DEFAULT_CHROME_OVERRIDES = {}` (cascade chrome from core unchanged), `DEFAULT_SUBSTRATE = {preset: "morning-warm", intensity: 100, base_token: "surface-base", accent_token_1: "surface-elevated", accent_token_2: None}`, `DEFAULT_TYPOGRAPHY = {preset: "frosted-text", heading_weight: 600, body_weight: 500, heading_color_token: "content-strong", body_color_token: "content-base"}`. `focus_templates_service.create_template` calls `is_empty_blob(blob)` (True for None or `{}`) on each — empty-or-null populates the canonical default; any key-present mapping (even `{preset: None}`) is treated as explicit operator intent and respected verbatim. `update_template` semantics unchanged. **(3) Seed alignment** — `backend/scripts/seed_focus_template_inheritance.py`: scheduling-kanban-core chrome bumped from `{"preset": "card"}` to `{"preset": "card", "corner_radius": 70, "padding_token": "space-3", "backdrop_blur": 44}` — explicit overrides on top of the `card` preset stamp the mockup-canonical values at the row level. scheduling-fh template bumped to fully-explicit canonical mockup defaults matching DEFAULT_SUBSTRATE + DEFAULT_TYPOGRAPHY; chrome_overrides explicitly `{}` (cascade from core unchanged). Seed is drift-tolerant: `_seed_core` + `_seed_template` detect content divergence on rerun and call `update_core` / `update_template` to version-bump existing rows; previous version preserved as `is_active=false`. Re-running on unmodified seed is a clean no-op. **Frosted Scribe template intentionally NOT seeded** — no such template exists in the codebase today; the prompt's reference appears aspirational. Surfaced. **Tests**: new `backend/tests/test_focus_template_inheritance_e1_defaults.py` (12 tests across 2 classes) covers defaults.py shape + create_template wiring. Five existing tests updated for E-1 contract change: `TestTemplateServiceSubstrate::test_create_default_empty_substrate` + `TestTemplateServiceTypography::test_create_default_empty_typography` now expect canonical defaults; admin API `test_template_response_includes_all_substrate_fields` + `test_template_response_includes_all_typography_fields` updated to expect canonical mockup default values; resolver "empty at both tiers → None" tests (substrate + typography) updated to null the column out directly post-create (simulates pre-E1 seeded rows). Substrate-resolver vitest expanded from 6 to 13 tests: morning-warm intensity 100/50/0; token-binding to linear base stops; other-presets-unchanged regression. **Gates**: backend pytest 241/241 green across 8 focus template inheritance test files; frontend tsc clean; vitest 2712/2714 passing (1 failure is pre-existing flaky `Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx` `preview-card chrome preset updates live when chrome pill clicked` — fails identically with E-1 absent, passes when isolated; not introduced by E-1); vite build clean 5.06s, bundle unchanged within ±2%. **Out of scope per spec**: card content, Tier 1 editor preview CSS, other substrate/typography/chrome presets, right-bar cleanup, widget palette, Tier 3 work. **Migration head unchanged** — pure JSONB content alignment via service-layer versioning.

- **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc C-2.3 shipped (uncommitted) — C-2 sub-arc canonically complete** — Final sub-sub-arc of C-2. Ships the inheritance-surfacing layer + URL consolidation polish that closes C-2 end-to-end. **(1) Per-row inheritance indicators in the Tier 2 inspector** — `PropertyRow` (in `PropertyPanel.tsx`) extended with optional `inheritanceSource?: "explicit" | { tier: string } | null` and `onReset?: () => void` props. Inherited rows render dimmed value (opacity 60) + a brass-toned "↑ inherited from <tier>" mono caption below the row; explicit rows render full-opacity. Driven ENTIRELY by the resolver's `sources.*_sources` provenance (locked decision #4) — Tier2TemplatesEditor calls a new `focusTemplatesService.resolve({template_slug, vertical})` and maps each tier string ("tier1"/"tier2"/"tier3"/null) to a `PropertyRowInheritance`: `"tier1"` → `{tier: "Tier 1 core"}` (chrome only — substrate + typography are tier-1-free by design per resolver); `"tier2"/"tier3"` → `"explicit"`; `null` → no decoration. Existing PropertyRow consumers (Tier1CoresEditor, InheritedCoreInspectorPanel) untouched — neutral rows render exactly as before when no `inheritanceSource` is supplied. **(2) Reset-to-inherited ↺ affordance** — hover-only RotateCcw icon button rendered to the right of the value block, opacity 0 at rest → 100 on row hover or button focus; only renders when row is "explicit" AND `onReset` is wired. New hook methods: `resetChromeOverridesField(fieldName)` / `resetSubstrateField(fieldName)` / `resetTypographyField(fieldName)` on `useFocusTemplateDraft`. Each removes the named key via `delete next[fieldName]` (object identity preserved when key absent — short-circuit prevents needless save trigger), then calls `queueSave` to fire the standard 300ms debounced PUT. Reset is dirty-positive: `isDirty=true` momentarily, snaps back to `false` after the round-trip. Per locked decisions #5/#8 Tier 1 cores editor gets NO inheritance indicators or reset (cascade root). **(3) Tier indicator pill** — brass-toned chip ("Tier 1" / "Tier 2") rendered in FocusEditorPage's top bar adjacent to the "Focuses" title, gated on `(tier===1 && selectedCoreId) || (tier===2 && selectedTemplateId)` so the chip only appears when there's a target to attribute the tier to. `bg-accent-subtle text-accent` with mono font and `data-tier` discriminator for tests. **(4) Interactive lineage chrome** — the existing "Inherits from: X (Tier 1 v<N>)" text in FocusEditorPage's top bar is now a button. Click opens InheritedCoreInspectorPanel (same panel as canvas placement click per locked decision #15); visual unchanged at rest, subtle accent-subtle hover treatment. Dirty-state confirm-before-leave flow inherits from C-2.2c automatically — the panel handles it. Required lifting `inheritedCorePanelOpen` state from Tier2TemplatesEditor up to FocusEditorPage: new optional `inheritedCorePanelOpen` + `onInheritedCorePanelOpenChange` props on the editor; falls back to local uncontrolled state when no controller wired (preserves C-2.2c canvas-placement-click behavior in isolation). Same panel, single source of truth — top-bar lineage and canvas placement are two trigger sites for the same UI. **(5) useSearchParams consolidation cleanup** — Tier2TemplatesEditor's local `useSearchParams` + `useNavigate` (used only to compose the `?tier=1&core=<id>` URL when navigating to Tier 1 from the inherited-core inspector panel) lifted up to FocusEditorPage. The editor now accepts `onNavigateToTier1Core?: (coreId: string) => void` and invokes the parent's handler; FocusEditorPage owns the URL rewrite via its existing setSearchParams. Mechanical refactor — behavior unchanged (deep-linking via ?core / ?template / ?tier / ?return_to still works; navigation between Tier 1 ↔ Tier 2 preserved). Removed unused imports from Tier2TemplatesEditor (`useNavigate`, `useSearchParams`). **Step 1 backend verification**: confirmed resolver `sources.*_sources` shape — flat dicts mapping field name → `"tier1" | "tier2" | "tier3" | null`. Substrate/typography never produce `"tier1"` (cores substrate/typography-free per resolver). `ResolveResponse` already exposes `sources` cleanly. The resolver endpoint exists at `GET /api/platform/admin/focus-template-inheritance/resolve?template_slug=&vertical=&tenant_id=` (NOT keyed by template id) — frontend now consumes via new `focusTemplatesService.resolve(params)` method + new typed `ResolveResponse` + `ResolveSources` exports. No backend changes required, no Spec-Override invoked. **Resolver refetch trigger**: `useEffect` deps `[template.template_slug, template.vertical, template.version]` — refetch after each save round-trip so explicit overrides flip from "tier1 inherited" → "tier2 explicit" without operator action. **Defensive guard**: editor checks `typeof focusTemplatesService.resolve === "function"` before calling — graceful degradation for any consumer whose mock omits the method (no test churn for unrelated suites; the C-2.3 test mocks include it). **Tests**: PropertyPanel +5 new (neutral row, dimmed-inherited + caption, full-opacity explicit, hover ↺ wires onReset + fires, no-onReset hides button) → 11/11. useFocusTemplateDraft +5 new (resetChrome removes field + marks dirty, resetSubstrate, resetTypography, no-op when field absent preserves object identity AND doesn't mark dirty, reset triggers debounced save with the field absent from payload — uses `vi.useFakeTimers` + `advanceTimersByTimeAsync` to confirm the PUT payload shape) → 25/25. Tier2TemplatesEditor +6 new integration (inherited-from caption renders for cascading rows, exactly-one reset ↺ for the single explicit row in fixture, click reset persists `chrome_overrides: {}` via update, controlled panel open prop mounts panel, canvas placement click invokes `onInheritedCorePanelOpenChange(true)`, `onNavigateToTier1Core` fires on "Edit core in Tier 1" with correct coreId) → 22/22. - **2026-05-15 — Sub-arc C-2.1.3 shipped (uncommitted)** — Closes the misdiagnosed dirty-state-clear bug from C-2.1.2. The real root cause was not JSONB key-order (C-2.1.2's hypothesis) but null-stripping in the backend serializer: `_core_to_response` did `dict(row.chrome or {})` which carries only the keys actually present on the row, while the frontend draft populates the full 7-field chrome canonical shape (some values null) as the user touches sliders. Response had 4 keys, draft had 7 → C-2.1.2's `deepEqualChrome` (key-order-tolerant but key-set-strict) returned `!equal` forever → "Unsaved" indicator stuck post-save. Production DevTools inspection confirmed: PUT response chrome blob carried `{preset, elevation, corner_radius, backdrop_blur}` — missing `background_token`, `border_token`, `padding_token`. C-2.1.2's regression test passed for the wrong reason: the mock returned chrome with the same key set as the draft (key-order swapped only), never reproducing production's sparse-key shape. **Backend fix (Option B — clean contract)**: `_core_to_response` + `_template_to_response` (chrome_overrides + substrate + typography) now normalize via a new `_normalize_blob(stored, canonical_fields)` helper. Canonical field sets imported from `chrome_validation.CHROME_FIELDS` (7), `substrate_validation.SUBSTRATE_FIELDS` (5), `typography_validation.TYPOGRAPHY_FIELDS` (5) — already cleanly exported by B-3.5 / B-4 / B-5 validators, no inlining needed. Every response carries the full canonical key set with explicit `null` for unset fields. Database storage stays as-is (null/missing fields stay however JSONB writes them); only the API response is normalized. NO migration. **Frontend fix (Option A — defensive)**: `deepEqualChrome` in `useFocusCoreDraft.ts` rewritten to treat missing-key and explicit-null/undefined-value as semantically equivalent — `{a:1, b:null}` deep-equals `{a:1}`. Union-of-keys iteration; both null/undefined branches short-circuit to `true`. Defensive against any current or future backend serializer that drops null fields. **C-2.1.2's helper kept** (per scope rule "do not remove or revert"); comment updated to reflect C-2.1.3 semantics (key-order-AND-key-set-tolerant). **C-2.1.2's regression test kept-and-improved**: original "key-order swap" test still passes (correct in spirit); 3 new C-2.1.3 tests added that REPRODUCE the production bug (mock response chrome has FEWER keys than draft) — pre-C-2.1.3 implementation would FAIL on those; post-fix all pass. Plus a "missing key == explicit null" equivalence test and a "normalized full-shape response" test (post-backend-fix path). **Tests: 7 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_admin_api.py` covering core empty-chrome → 7 explicit nulls, core partial update → 7 keys with 1 valued + 6 null, GET round-trip preserves full shape, template chrome_overrides normalized, template substrate normalized (5 keys), template typography normalized (5 keys), list endpoint normalizes every row. **5 pre-existing backend tests updated** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` (1) + `_substrate.py` (2) + `_typography.py` (2) — exact-equality assertions on response blobs aligned to the new normalized shape; these tests were the contract for the pre-C-2.1.3 sparse shape, now updated with explanatory comments. **3 new frontend tests** in `useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (1) sparse-response-vs-7-field-draft regression that reproduces production bug, (2) missing-key/explicit-null equivalence for dirty check, (3) normalized full-shape response path after backend fix. Backend regression: 228/228 focus_template_inheritance suite (chrome 54 + substrate 47 + typography 49 + admin_api 17 + service 50 + session_aware 9 + session_aware_templates 13 — including 7 new C-2.1.3 admin_api tests + 5 pre-existing aligned). Frontend regression: vitest 2589/2589 + 1 todo passing (20/20 in useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx); tsc clean; vite build 5.89s. LOC: ~50 backend production-code (route serializer +25 incl. new `_normalize_blob` helper + 3 imports + 2 call sites; existing validators untouched) + ~190 backend tests (7 new + 5 modified) + ~30 frontend production-code (hook deepEqualChrome rewrite) + ~110 frontend tests = ~380 total (within ~250-400 midpoint). No migration. No schema changes. No canon doc edits. **Diagnostic root-cause confirmation**: the build prompt's diagnosis stood up — the production response WAS missing 3 chrome keys, draft DID carry all 7, and C-2.1.2's helper DID return `!equal` on sparse-key response. Hypothesis confirmed end-to-end. **Deferred per scope**: C-2.2 (next dispatch — Tier 2 templates editor); edge-panel templates response normalization (apply same pattern when edge-panel session-aware ships); new session-aware semantics; new substrate vocabularies; audit log substrate; resolver changes. Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`.

- **2026-05-15 — Sub-arc C-2.1.2 shipped (uncommitted)** — Mixed backend + frontend fix closing three issues before C-2.2 dispatches: (1) session-aware update semantics for `focus_templates` (Tier 2 — mirrors C-2.1.1 verbatim), (2) resolver slug-vs-UUID bug — live cascade restored by following active core BY SLUG instead of the template's stored `inherits_from_core_id`, (3) `useFocusCoreDraft` dirty-state-clear bug — "Unsaved" indicator was sticking after successful save because `JSON.stringify` equality is key-order-sensitive and PostgreSQL JSONB does not preserve insertion order on round-trip. **Migration `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`** adds `last_edit_session_id UUID NULL` + `last_edit_session_at TIMESTAMPTZ NULL` to focus_templates; reversible; mirrors r102's columns on focus_cores. **`update_template` becomes session-aware**: in-place mutation within 5-min window matching session_id (or first-touch on never-stamped row); version-bump for no-token / expired / different-token / no-session paths; INACTIVE target → new `StaleTemplateVersionError(inactive_id, slug, scope, vertical, active_id)` → **HTTP 410 Gone** with structured `detail: {message, inactive_template_id, active_template_id, slug, scope, vertical}` so frontend swaps its local id + retries under the SAME session token. `TemplateUpdateRequest.edit_session_id` added; `TemplateResponse.last_edit_session_id` + `last_edit_session_at` added. **Resolver slug-based active core lookup** (locked Option A, silent transparent resolve per α): two new helpers `get_core_slug_by_id` + `get_active_core_by_slug` in focus_cores_service; resolver does `slug_by_id(template.inherits_from_core_id) → active_core_by_slug(slug)` rather than direct PK lookup of stored id. When stored UUID is still active, slug lookup returns same row (regression-safe); when bumped, slug lookup returns NEW active row (closes live-cascade bug). Both lookups indexed (PK + partial-unique `ix_focus_cores_active_slug` from r96) — perceptible-impact zero. Orphan slug (would only happen via manual DB intervention bypassing partial-unique) raises `FocusTemplateNotFound` with descriptive message. **`EDIT_SESSION_WINDOW_SECONDS` lifted to shared `app/services/focus_template_inheritance/constants.py`** — single canonical source; cores + templates + future edge-panel session-aware semantics all import from there. `__init__.py` re-exports preserved public surface unchanged. **Frontend dirty-state-clear fix**: introduced narrow recursive `deepEqualChrome(a, b)` (key-order-independent, handles primitives + plain objects + arrays) in `useFocusCoreDraft.ts`; `isDirty` switched from `JSON.stringify(...)` inequality to `useMemo(() => !deepEqualChrome(draft, savedSnapshot), [draft, savedSnapshot])`. Root cause was hypothesis (b) variant — PostgreSQL JSONB round-trip reorders object keys; backend returned `{ elevation: 75, preset: "card" }` when draft was `{ preset: "card", elevation: 75 }` — JSON.stringify produced different strings → `isDirty = true` forever → "Auto-saved Xs ago" never appeared. **Tests: 13 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_session_aware_templates.py` across 3 classes (TestTemplateSessionAwareUpdate × 10, TestTemplateApiStaleReturns410 × 2, TestMigrationR103 × 1) + **4 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_service.py::TestResolverSlugBasedLookup` (regression slug-when-active, new behavior slug-after-bump, orphan raises, in-place propagation regression) + **2 new frontend** in `useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (dirty clears on key-order-mismatch round-trip; dirty re-appears on subsequent update). Backend prior-arc regression: 70/70 across session_aware (29) + service (37 + appended 4) + admin_api (4). Adjacent focus_* tests: 164/164 across chrome + substrate + typography + schema + compositions. Frontend regression: vitest 2586/2586 + 1 todo passing; tsc clean; vite build 5.39s; main bundle 5,998,380 bytes = +440 bytes / +0.007% vs C-2.1.1 baseline 5,997,940 (well within ±2% gate). LOC: ~210 backend production-code (service +154, schema +8, migration +70, route +27, model +15, __init__ +7, constants +25, resolver +35) + ~610 backend tests (new file 489 + appended 121) + ~60 frontend production-code (hook) + ~63 frontend tests = ~1,150 total (within ~700-1,000 midpoint, comfortably under worst-case 1,300). **Resolver performance**: 2 indexed B-tree hits vs 1 PK hit — ~50-200µs added latency in unmeasured-but-typical territory; the partial-unique `ix_focus_cores_active_slug` makes the second lookup as cheap as the PK; no measurement script added (over-engineered for the change). **Deferred per Out-of-Scope**: C-2.2 Tier 2 templates editor (next dispatch); edge-panel session-aware (deferred); ResolvedFocus drift signaling (Option β deferred); audit log infrastructure; explicit "Publish v2" UI; multi-tab conflict detection beyond 410-retry; background cleanup of stale session_id rows; resolver caching. **Recommendation**: C-2.2 can now safely build the Tier 2 templates editor knowing scrub-session auto-save will mutate in place + the resolver will surface in-place mutations across all dependent compositions without staleness. Migration head: `r102_focus_cores_edit_session` → `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`.

- **2026-05-15 — Sub-arc C-2.1.1 shipped (uncommitted)** — Session-aware update semantics for `focus_cores` closes the version-bump-on-every-scrub bug from C-2.1. C-2.1's `useFocusCoreDraft` 300ms debounced auto-save was producing ~30+ version-bumps during a single elevation-slider drag because B-1's `update_core` versioned on every successful write; after the first save the frontend held a now-inactive UUID and subsequent saves returned 409. The fix: updates carrying an `edit_session_id` UUID v4 token that match the row's `last_edit_session_id` within 5 minutes (`EDIT_SESSION_WINDOW_SECONDS=300`) mutate in place — version unchanged, `updated_at` bumps, `last_edit_session_at` advances; row id stays the same so the frontend never goes stale. Updates outside the window OR with a different token version-bump per the B-1 behavior. Updates without any token version-bump (B-1 backward-compat preserved verbatim). **First-touch semantics**: when an update arrives with a token AND the row has never been session-stamped (`last_edit_session_id IS NULL`), the update mutates in place + sets the pointer — without this branch the FIRST update of every editor session would version-bump and the scrub-session would still produce one stray version per session. Migration `r102_focus_cores_edit_session` adds two columns to `focus_cores`: `last_edit_session_id UUID NULL` + `last_edit_session_at TIMESTAMPTZ NULL` (reversible; downgrade drops both, no data backfill needed since NULL is the correct "no active session" state). New `StaleCoreVersionError` exception carries `inactive_id` + `slug` + `active_id`; route layer translates to **HTTP 410 Gone** with structured `detail: {message, inactive_core_id, active_core_id, slug}` per **Spec-Override decision (Sonnet locked) option (i)** — preserves the addressing contract and surfaces staleness explicitly rather than silently redirecting. Frontend hook generates a UUID v4 token via `crypto.randomUUID()` (with Math.random fallback for test envs) when `coreId` transitions null → real OR switches between two real values; preserved across re-renders for the same coreId; cleared when coreId returns to null; intentionally NOT persisted across page reloads (page reload = fresh session). On 410 Gone the hook reads `active_core_id` from the error body, swaps its internal `activeCoreIdRef`, and retries the save once under the SAME session token — the scrub keeps going without visible interruption. `CoreUpdateRequest` gains `edit_session_id: str | None` (≤36 chars, optional). `CoreResponse` gains `last_edit_session_id` + `last_edit_session_at` for client telemetry. Tests: **16 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_session_aware.py` across 4 classes — `TestSessionAwareUpdate` × 10 (in-place mutate, consecutive same-session, cross-session bump, stale-window bump, no-token bump, unset-field preservation, session_at advance, stale-inactive raises, no-new-row, chrome persistence), `TestSessionAwareCascade` × 2 (in-place mutation flows through resolver without re-versioning templates; many in-place edits during one session keep template row at version 1), `TestApiStaleCoreReturns410` × 2 (410 body shape; session round-trip), `TestMigrationR102` × 1 (columns exist + populate). **6 new frontend** in `useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (token generation, preserved across re-renders, refreshed on coreId switch, cleared on null, included in PUT payload, 410 retry path). Backend regression: 241/241 across focus_template_inheritance (188) + edge_panel_inheritance (24) + focus_compositions (29). Pre-existing B-1 version-bump tests (`test_update_versions`, `test_update_cannot_target_inactive`) preserved verbatim because they don't supply session tokens — version-bump path unchanged. Frontend: 15/15 useFocusCoreDraft tests pass (9 original + 6 new); tsc clean; vite build 5.46s; main bundle 5,997,940 bytes = +870 / +0.014% vs C-2.1 baseline 5,997,070 (well within ±2% gate). LOC: ~290 backend (service +130, schema +12, migration +50, route +30, model +15, __init__ +3, tests ~480 raw but ~280 effective service-test) + ~280 frontend (hook +120, service +30, tests +130) = ~570 production + ~610 tests = ~1,180 total (within ~600-900 midpoint, just under worst-case 1,200). **Deferred items**: (a) extending the same semantics to `focus_templates` (Tier 2) — likely the right call once C-2.2 ships a Tier 2 editor with auto-save, but scope-deferred to a follow-up sub-arc (call it C-2.1.2 or fold into C-2.2's slider-scrub work); (b) same for `edge_panel_templates` (B-1.5 territory); (c) explicit "Publish v2" UI affordance for deliberate version creation; (d) audit log capture of session events (no audit substrate for focus_cores exists yet); (e) session-token persistence across page reloads (intentional fresh-session contract); (f) multi-tab editing conflict detection; (g) telemetry on session-reuse rate. **Recommendation**: extend to `focus_templates` BEFORE C-2.2's Tier 2 editor ships — same auto-save pattern will produce the same bloat. Migration head: `r101_typography_substrate` → `r102_focus_cores_edit_session`.

Observed symptoms (Playwright screenshot, post-`0623ed3` deploy):
  - Top bar displays "Vertical: dispatch" — something is reading the raw `:vertical` URL param without going through `disambiguateStudioLive`
  - Dev banner shows `Page: unmapped:/bridgeable-admin/studio/live/dispatch/funeral-schedule`
  - Pulse/Home overview surface renders instead of `FuneralSchedulePage`

  Follow-up #4's verticals-aware disambiguation shipped cleanly (vitest 2476/2476 pass, including 18 new disambiguation tests) but did not change the rendered output, indicating a consumer outside `StudioLiveModeWrap` and `TenantUserPicker` is reading the URL directly. Likely candidates: `StudioScopeSwitcher` (renders "Vertical: dispatch"), `StudioShell`-level dispatch outside the nested Routes block, or an `EditModeDispatcher` path that matches `:vertical = "dispatch"` ahead of the Live mode Routes.

  Six fixes have been attempted in service of Gates 14 and 22 across the Studio 1a-i sequence (A2 redirect, R-2.x.1 universal-relative-paths, follow-up #2 auth gate, follow-up #3 router topology + picker pickup-and-replay, follow-up #4 verticals disambiguation). Each fix has shipped clean and tested correctly at the unit level, but Gates 14/22 remain red. The diagnostic gap is that chat-driven static analysis has not been sufficient — each fix has been based on a plausible-sounding diagnosis that turned out incomplete. Resolution requires hands-on DevTools debugging on the deployed staging app: open `/bridgeable-admin/studio/live/dispatch/funeral-schedule` while logged in, walk the React component tree, find what is rendering "Vertical: dispatch" and what is mounting the Pulse overview, identify the consumer that bypasses `disambiguateStudioLive`, fix in one shot with evidence.

The shell mounts correctly. 53 of 56 Playwright gates pass. Gates 14/22 affect a specific click-to-edit path on deep tenant routes — material, but downstream of the Studio shell's substrate work.

- **2026-06-04 — Workflow editor canvas — FIX: negative-coordinate support** at HEAD `fab29b4`. **Pre-existing bug (NOT the container arc** — root-caused at `/tmp/workflow_canvas_leftside_bug.md`; reproduces before P0 `855e132`; `bbox`/pan/SVG byte-identical pre-arc). The canvas was **origin-anchored to (0,0)..(maxX,maxY) and ignored negative content coords**: any node at x<0/y<0 rendered off-surface, its edges clipped at the SVG x<0 boundary, and pan was dead over that region. `funeral_cascade` seeds the burial path at **x=-300**, which surfaced it (the leftward burial-branch edge didn't render + left-region pan was dead). **Fix:** a content-origin offset `bbox.originX/originY = min(0, minX/minY)` — **0 for any non-negative canvas → whole offset is a no-op (byte-identical; the load-bearing invariant, proven)** — applied at every coordinate consumer (one model, `dom = content − origin`): node + container `left/top` (subtract origin), the edge-SVG **`viewBox="${originX} ${originY} ${w} ${h}"`** (so x<0 geometry is in-viewport; `"0 0 w h"` ≡ the prior no-viewBox 1:1 map), the **pan-clamp bounds** (shift −origin → the negative region is now inside the pannable surface), the **drag-to-connect hit-test + preview** (`screenToWorld` result `+origin` to recover raw content), and the **node-drag clamp lower bound** (`clampToCanvas`/`computeNodeDragCommit` gain optional `minX/minY` defaulting 0 → so a node at negative coords isn't snapped to 0 on drag). **Coordinate-consistency audit done** — node render, container render, edge SVG, pan, drag-to-connect, node-drag all derive from the single origin; a negative node renders in-viewport, connects, is selectable + drag-to-connectable, and (grouped) computes correct container bounds. **NOT a shared substrate** (the dispatch's premise) — `canvas-layout`/`GraphCanvas` are workflow-canvas-only (Focus composition + dashboard grid are separate components, unaffected). **Frontend-only, no backend, no migration.** **Tests:** 6 unit (`canvas-layout`: bbox origin byte-identical-guard + negative + the clamp lower bound) + 3 jsdom (`GraphCanvas`: negative node on-surface, SVG viewBox at the negative origin + edge in-viewport, non-negative byte-identical) + a Playwright spec (`workflow-canvas-negative-coords.spec.ts` — burial-edge-renders + left-region-pan, `test.skip` skeletons per the codebase's deep-canvas convention, pending the platform-admin auth harness). tsc clean; build clean (5.50s); full frontend suite **281 / 4078 / 0 across 2 runs** (both fully clean). **No canon edit** (a bugfix, not an arc). `funeral_cascade` kept at x=-300 as the live negative-coordinate fixture (NOT re-seeded).

- **2026-06-04 — Workflow visual-containers arc — ARC CLOSE (canon pass)** at HEAD `fab29b4`. The arc-close canon pass — **three DECISIONS.md entries** (Opus-authored, applied verbatim) appended + the **investigation doc folded to AS-BUILT** (`docs/investigations/workflow_containers_investigation.md` gains a "P3a/P3b/P3c shipped, ARC COMPLETE" section: the §3 no-inline-selection finding, the option-(a) union extension, the shipped mixed-select-then-group gesture + container-member emission, the E1 select-affordance resolution, the seven commit hashes, and the five filed-forward refinements moved to the forward section referencing the new DECISIONS entry). No code, no migration, no behavior change; doc-only (DECISIONS + investigation doc + STATE). The entries: (1) **"Workflow Builder visual containers are an additive overlay, not a graph change"** — the flat node/edge graph stays the single source of truth; a container is canvas_state metadata with zero runtime semantics; explicit (A1) membership, computed bounds, non-collapsed = byte-identical to no-containers, ungroup leaves the graph untouched; consistent with opinionated-but-configurable. (2) **"The container arc is the reference for phasing a risky additive canvas feature"** — canonizes the two load-bearing disciplines: de-risk-then-render (pure logic unit-tested in isolation before any render consumes it — P2a→P2b, P3a→P3b) and the protected-invariant rework (single-select + the flat case proven byte-identical every phase; the union-touching phase sequenced last). The reference pattern for extending shared load-bearing state. (3) **"Container arc filed-forward refinements (deliberated, deferred)"** — the five Type-B deferrals recorded so they aren't re-litigated as gaps: assign-into gesture · collapsed-box draggability · multiple-crossing-per-side spread · collapse animation · a dedicated `{kind:"container"}`/`{kind:"mixed"}` selection union kind (corrects the earlier framing — P3c established there was no inline container selection; it introduced selection by extending `{kind:"nodes"}` with optional `containerIds`). **THE WORKFLOW VISUAL-CONTAINERS ARC IS FULLY CLOSED** — P0 (`4cc85d0`) → P1 (`628972d`) → P2a (`779c87b`) → P2b (`49823ba`) → P3a (`76079bd`) → P3b (`4786dd5`) → P3c (`85fdedf`) → canon. Nesting is authorable, renders, reroutes, and validates end-to-end; the canon records the why. Filed-forward refinements await concrete operator signal.

- **2026-06-04 — Workflow visual-containers arc — PHASE 3c: the authoring gesture (LAST FEATURE PHASE)** at HEAD `fab29b4`. Makes nesting AUTHORABLE end-to-end — the union-touching phase, deliberately isolated last. **Frontend-only; `WorkflowEditorPage.tsx` + `GraphCanvas.tsx` + their tests** (no backend, no `canvas-layout`/validators — the P3a substrate + P3b render are consumed unchanged; producing state they already gate + draw). **Union = option (a):** the existing multi member extended to `{ kind:"nodes"; ids: string[]; containerIds?: string[] }` — ADDITIVE, so node-only producers/consumers are byte-identical; **single-select `{kind:"node"}` is UNTOUCHED** (the protected P0/card-editing/inline-params chain). Node-only callers (default `[]`) byte-identical. The group-panel copy reflects "N nodes + M groups." **End-to-end:** group nodes → a container, then mix-select a loose node + that container → group → a parent nesting the child; P3a's ≤1-parent + cycle validators gate it, P3b renders it. **DOES NOT CHANGE:** single-select, the card-editing/inline-params path, P3a helpers/validators, the P3b render, the schema (no migration), the edge-map/node-filter. **OUT OF SCOPE (filed forward):** assign-into gesture; collapsed-box draggability; multiple-crossing spread; collapse animation; a dedicated single-container union kind. **Tests:** 7 GraphCanvas P3c (expanded select handle plain/shift/⌘ · collapsed body-click · ring/`data-multi-selected` · CheckSquare · chrome-button stopPropagation ×2 · regression no-handler-no-select) + 3 page E2E (mixed node+container group → nested parent + validators pass · plain-node-click clears container selection · node-only-group regression). tsc clean; build clean (5.92s); full frontend suite **281 / 4069 / 0 across 2 runs** (0 test failures both; run 1 carried the known r21/DocumentsTab-class environmental teardown error, run 2 fully clean). **No canon edit** — **the arc-close canon pass (overlay-model + full-phasing DECISIONS entries + the filed-forward Type-B refinements) is a separate Opus session.** **THE CONTAINER ARC'S LAST FEATURE PHASE IS DONE: P0 multi-select → P1 expanded labeled containers → P2a/P2b collapse + rerouting → P3a/P3b/P3c nested containers (helpers → render → authoring). - **2026-06-04 — Workflow visual-containers arc — PHASE 3b: nested rendering (container-render-side only)** at HEAD `fab29b4`. Wires the P3a nesting substrate into the container render so nested containers DISPLAY — box-inside-box, inner hidden when an ancestor collapses. **Frontend-only; `GraphCanvas.tsx` + its test the ONLY files** (the edge-map, node-filter, validators, schema all extend for free off P3a). **GraphCanvas is the first consumer of the P3a helpers.** Four changes, all container-render-side: (1) **recursive bounds** — the expanded `.map` branch's inline `bbox(memberNodes) ± padding` + the collapsed `collapsedBoxBounds` call both replaced by ONE `containerBounds(container, canvas.nodes, containersById, heightOf)` (handles both states; an expanded outer now encloses inner boxes; flat-case byte-identical); (2) **empty-member-guard fix** — the P2 guard counted node-members only (`memberNodes.length === 0 → skip`), wrongly skipping a pure-nesting outer (all `kind:"container"` members) → now renders if ≥1 resolvable member of EITHER kind (truly-empty still skips, P1 stance); (3) **container-render filter** — `if (containerIsHidden(container.id)) return null` skips a container hidden inside a collapsed ancestor (mirrors the node-map hidden-member filter; uses `buildParentMap` + `outermostCollapsedAncestor` — non-null ⟺ a collapsed ancestor exists, the walk starts at the parent so never self); (4) **depth-scaled z** — new `parentMap` memo + `containerDepth`/`containerIsHidden` helpers; a `depth` prop on `GraphCanvasContainer`. **z scheme (CSS z-index is integer-only):** EXPANDED frames all `z=0` (== P2; no integer exists between 0 and the node band z=1, and translucent backdrops don't need depth-layering — nesting reads via the recursive bounds); OPAQUE COLLAPSED cards `z = 1 + depth` (depth 0 → 1 == P2; an inner collapsed card paints above its outer + the node baseline). Both reduce to P2 at depth 0 → **non-nested rendering byte-identical** (the regression guard). The local `CONTAINER_PADDING` const retired (unused after the bounds swap; `containerBounds` uses `CONTAINER_EXPANDED_PADDING=18`). **DOES NOT CHANGE:** the edge-map (`classifyEdge` + `collapsedBoundsFor` already reroute to the outermost collapsed ancestor via the nesting-aware membership — re-confirmed at the code), the node-map filter (already nesting-aware), `classifyEdge`, `buildCollapsedMembership`, the validators, the schema (no migration), the authoring gesture (3c — tests use HAND-AUTHORED nested `canvas_state`), the selection union (3c). **Tests:** 7 new GraphCanvas P3b against hand-authored nested state (expanded-encloses-inner · expanded-frames-z=0 · collapsed-card depth-z · collapse-outer-hides-subtree · collapse-inner-shows-card-inside-outer · pure-nesting-outer-renders · non-nested-regression-byte-identical). **Build caught:** an initial fractional-z scheme (`min(0.9, depth·0.1)`) was dropped by CSS (z-index integer-only, jsdom read 0) → corrected to the integer scheme above. tsc clean; build clean (5.56s); full frontend suite **281 / 4059 / 0 across 2 runs** (both fully clean). **No canon edit** (overlay-model + full-phasing DECISIONS lands at ARC CLOSE — after 3c). **NEXT:** P3c — the authoring gesture (mixed node+container multi-selection + `handleCreateContainer` emitting `kind:"container"` members; touches the P0 selection union, isolated last) → then the arc-close canon pass.

- **2026-06-04 — Workflow visual-containers arc — PHASE 3a: nested-container helpers + validation (de-risk + gate)** at HEAD `fab29b4`. - **2026-06-04 — Workflow visual-containers arc — PHASE 2b: the collapse rendering (consumes the P2a helpers)** at HEAD `fab29b4`. The LARGE phase — wires the P2a pure helpers into the live render so collapsed containers actually collapse. Side-bucketed (crossing-in → box top, crossing-out → box bottom, box↔box → boxA-bottom → boxB-top). **Behind `container.collapsed` (default-false = byte-identical P1).** **Node-map** (`GraphCanvas.tsx`): filters out HIDDEN members (`canvas.nodes.filter(n => !collapsedMembership.has(n.id))`) — hidden members don't render; the surface-sizing `bbox` still counts ALL nodes (no pan jump). **Edge-map:** per edge `classifyEdge` → `interior` SKIP · `external` the UNTOUCHED P1 `computeEdgePath`/`computeEdgeMidpoint` path (byte-identical; nothing collapsed → all external → zero change) · `crossing-in`/`crossing-out`/`box-to-box` re-anchor the hidden endpoint(s) to the collapsed box via `boxAnchor(collapsedBoxBounds(...), "top"|"bottom")` + `bezierBetween`; the midpoint (label/×) = average of the resolved anchors. **`GraphCanvasContainer` branches on `collapsed`:** expanded → the P1 frame (behind nodes, `data-collapsed="false"`) + a NEW collapse button (`Minimize2`) on the chrome; collapsed → an OPAQUE card in the node z-band (`zIndex:1`, `data-collapsed="true"`, pointer-events:auto) showing label + "N nodes · collapsed" + an expand button (`Maximize2`). Instant (no animation). **Drag-to-connect fix (§P2.4):** `handleDrawEnd` passes `canvas.nodes.filter(n => !collapsedMembership.has(n.id))` to `dropDecision` — a drop can't resolve onto a hidden member. Drag-to-connect mapped as a state-mediated raw-pointer gesture (NOT dnd-kit, which is position-only) reusing the existing edge render + cycle/ref validator + B-5 edge selection. **Locked decisions:** (a) **§4 (4-i)** — retire-for-31 + a narrow `invoke_*` bespoke pane (P3 doesn't serialize behind the filed-forward namespace-reconciliation arc; that arc removes the last pane later); (b) **§2** — DROP in-place type-change (delete+re-add via palette) AND manual id-edit (auto-only), so P3a relocates LABEL only; (c) **sequencing** — P3a (un-slotted home + label) first → P3b-1 (drag-to-connect draw) → P3b-2 (canvas edge delete) → P3c (remove inspector + collapse rail; gated on both + 4-i). Open Type-B decisions resolved at phase grounding: un-slotted-param home shape (recommended card expand panel — P3a), handle disambiguation (origin-based stopPropagation — P3b-1), is_iteration-on-cycle-drop (P3b-1).

- **2026-05-29 — Inline-params P2b: complex-type tokens inline-editable via gate-flip; the 2 bespoke `invoke_*` types excluded (phantom-key guard)** at HEAD `da32bf5` (2026-05-29). Third inline-params phase (P1 read-only → P2a simple-editable → P2b complex-editable). Pre-flight HEAD `7d7eded`.
  - **Gate-flip (the core):** widened the editable-token set in `workflow-node-templates.ts` — `SIMPLE_EDITABLE_TYPES` renamed `EDITABLE_TOKEN_TYPES`, now `{string,enum,number,boolean,object,array,componentReference}`. The existing `EditableToken` (NodeLabelSentence) already calls `PropControlDispatcher` and dispatches by `schema.type`, so widening the set makes complex tokens render the right control (ObjectControl JSON textarea / ArrayControl / ComponentReferenceControl) **with zero per-type branching**. `PropControlDispatcher` + all controls **reused unmodified** (object is a first-class dispatcher branch, not a fallback — re-confirmed at audit). 30 of 32 node types now fully inline-editable.
  - **Bespoke exclusion (the guard):** new named set `BESPOKE_NAMESPACE_TYPES = {invoke_generation_focus, invoke_review_focus}` + new gate `isTokenInlineEditable(nodeType, token) = isEditableToken(token) && !BESPOKE_NAMESPACE_TYPES.has(nodeType)` (consumed at NodeLabelSentence:147). These 2 types use bespoke inspector configs that author `config.focus_id`/`config.review_focus_id`, while the registry declares + the template slots `{focusTemplateName}` — so inline-editing that token would write a PHANTOM key the backend ignores (silent operational no-op). Their tokens stay read-only; a guard test (both read-only) locks the divergence so a future patch can't silently re-enable phantom-key editing. **Distinction:** `generation-focus-invocation` (hyphenated Phase-1 node → RegistryDrivenConfig) authors `focusTemplateName` directly → its token round-trips cleanly and IS editable (asserted).
  - **Roomier popover:** `PopoverContent` className `w-56` → `w-80` (complex controls are taller; control scrolls within its own borders, `max-w-(--available-width)` caps at viewport). Real data small (arrays 2-3, objects 1-2 keys) so headroom, not strain.
  - **Whole-key merge** (confirmed): object/array edits persist via `onEditParam(param, value)` → `onUpdateNodeConfig(nodeId, {...config, [param]: value})` where `value` is the whole edited structure → replaces `config[param]` wholesale (no partial-merge). Unset→set seeds `config[param] ?? schema.default` (object `{}` / array `[]`).
  - **Reachable-surface honesty:** among the 32 templates the ONLY slotted complex params are `branches` (array, on `decision`) + `focusTemplateName` (componentReference, on the 3 focus types). **No template slots an `object` param today** — object editability is wired (gate + dispatcher) + covered at the logic level, forward-compatible for the instant a future template slots one; render coverage exercises the two reachable types (array + componentReference).
  - **Inspector UNTOUCHED** (P2b additive): `NodeConfigForm` + the 2 bespoke configs (`InvokeGenerationFocusConfig`/`InvokeReviewFocusConfig`) + `PropControls` all reused, not modified. P3 (retire the inspector) is the next phase; the 2 bespoke types are the documented P3 exception.
  - **FILED FORWARD** (its own arc, NOT P2b): "Focus-invocation namespace reconciliation + dedupe" — make `invoke_generation_focus`/`invoke_review_focus` edit inline correctly (reconcile `focus_id`/`focusTemplateName`) paired with the near-duplicate `generation-focus-invocation` vs `invoke_generation_focus` dedupe, backend-contract grounded.

No canon/registry/token/backend change (reuses existing controls). tsc clean; build clean (5.35s).
