1. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc FF-2 — canvas substrate replacement (free-form rendering ships visibly)** (uncommitted, 2026-05-20). First FF-series sub-arc producing operator-visible change. Canvas substrate now detects template shape per `detectTemplateShape(rowsDraft)` and routes to one of two layers: `WidgetFreeFormLayer` (absolute-positioned, FF-2 new) or `WidgetRowsLayer` (CSS-grid, F-3 preserved). `PlacedWidgetCore` extracted as shared inner wrapper per Q-29 — owns chrome resolution (DEFAULT_WIDGET_CHROME ← placement.chrome via `chrome-resolver` pipeline), selection chrome (brass outline on selected), click + keyboard handlers, widget component render via registry. Both positioning shells (`PlacedWidget` for grid, `FreeFormPlacedWidget` for free-form) are thin layout-only adapters consuming the shared core. Outer `data-testid="focus-builder-placed-widget"` preserved on the wrapper (F-3.1c selector continuity); new `data-testid="focus-builder-placed-widget-core"` added at the inner div as the FF-2 operator-observable assertion anchor per the 2026-05-20 late-evening canon. Inherited core renders at Q-20 canonical position inside `WidgetFreeFormLayer`: `core_width = canvas_width * (default_column_span/12)`, `core_x = (canvas_width - core_width)/2`, `core_y = 40`. Drop coordinate translation in `handleDragEnd`: pulls cursor from dnd-kit's `activatorEvent.clientX/Y + delta` minus layer-rect offset, computes pixel position via new pure helper `computeFreeFormDropPosition({cursorX, cursorY, width, height, canvasWidth, canvasHeight})` applying Q-4 centering (`x = cursorX - width/2`, `y = cursorY - height/2`) + Q-14 canvas-bounded clamp; resolves per-widget default size via new `getFreeFormDefaultDimensions(slug)` (registry lookup with `FREE_FORM_DEFAULT_DIMENSIONS` 320×180 platform fallback). Empty templates default to free-form per Q-27 — every new Focus template authored after FF-2 ships is free-form. `RegistrationMetadata.canvasMetadata` extended with optional `freeFormDefaultDimensions` + `freeFormMinDimensions` (pixels) alongside existing grid-cell `defaultDimensions` + `minDimensions`. Day Strip + Today Pin + Map widget seeds backfilled: 240×120 / 240×120 / 400×400 free-form defaults. Defensive `canvas_config` fallback to 1200×800 honored throughout (Q-2 refinement from FF-1) — partial canvas_configs carrying only `{gap_size: 4}` render correctly. Selection model carries over unchanged from F-2: `{kind: "widget", id}` discriminator works for both grid and free-form placements. Tests shipped: PlacedWidgetCore (9 unit), PlacedWidget regression (5 unit), FreeFormPlacedWidget (7 unit), WidgetFreeFormLayer (9 unit), FocusBuilderCanvas FF-2 extension (10 unit covering detectTemplateShape + flattenFreeFormPlacements + computeFreeFormDropPosition + free-form layer render + grid regression + defensive fallback), FocusBuilderPage FF-2 integration (3 page-level cross-side tests covering free-form render through full mount + grid regression + selection wiring). Operator-observable canon honored: every integration assertion targets inline style values at rendered elements (e.g., `expect(styleAttr).toMatch(/position:\s*absolute/i)` + `/left:\s*100px/i`); pure-function unit tests cover Q-4 + Q-14 drop logic so JSDOM weakness on dnd-kit pointer gestures per Q-40 doesn't block FF-2 — full drag-end Playwright coverage defers to FF-7. **Full frontend regression: 2965 vitest tests + 1 todo across 217 test files passing.** tsc clean. vite build clean (bundle 6,095 kB, within ±0.5% tolerance). Phase 1–FF-1 regression unaffected. FF-1 substrate (validator, adapter, hook helpers, WidgetPlacement interface) untouched per FF-2 scope. **Architectural surprises: zero** — PlacedWidgetCore extraction was mechanical Q-29 (c) decomposition; the cleanest seam was passing `outerStyle: React.CSSProperties` from positioning shells to the shared core so the chrome+selection+click layer stays byte-equivalent with F-3.1c's inline implementation while positioning becomes shape-aware. HEAD pre-flight verified `10321ed`. Foundation is in place for FF-3 drag-to-move via @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor.

1. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc FF-1 — free-form canvas foundation (validator + adapter extension)** (uncommitted, 2026-05-20). Foundation sub-arc of the FF-series (locked decisions Q-1 through Q-5 / Q-23 / Q-24 / Q-25 / Q-27 from `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-free-form-focus-canvas.md`). Backend `_validate_placement` now dispatches on placement-shape detection (field presence of `x` / `y` / `width` / `height` → free-form; otherwise grid). Free-form validation: positive numbers, bounds against `canvas_config.width` / `.height` (default 1200×800 — `DEFAULT_CANVAS_WIDTH` / `DEFAULT_CANVAS_HEIGHT` constants). Optional `z_index` integer; min width/height = 1 px (per-widget min/max is FF-4's resize-gesture concern). `is_core` discriminator works for both shapes; same component_kind+name match check as grid. Template-level shape consistency check fires AFTER per-placement validation — mixed-shape templates rejected with 422 + clear message. `create_template` stamps default canvas_config ONLY when caller passes empty/null config (E-1 empty-blob discipline preserved — explicit keys round-trip verbatim, so F-series test fixtures passing `{gap_size: 4}` aren't infill-stamped). `update_template` reorders canvas_config computation BEFORE row validation so free-form bounds check against operator's intent on THIS save. Frontend `WidgetPlacement` interface extended: `column_start` / `column_span` now optional; additive `x` / `y` / `width` / `height` / `z_index`. `_placement-adapter.ts` detects shape by field presence; free-form coords pass 1:1 (Q-25 — no off-by-one for pixels); grid retains 1↔0-indexed column translation. Hook `addWidget(slug, position?)` accepts BOTH field families and emits the matching placement shape (free-form when any positioning field supplied; otherwise grid F-3 default). `updateWidget(id, partial)` routes positioning-field keys (x/y/width/height/z_index/column_start/column_span) to top-level placement fields and remaining keys to chrome merge — single mutator handles future drag/resize commits (FF-3/4) AND existing F-3 chrome merges through one code path. **ZERO Alembic migrations** (Q-23 pure-JSONB extension; migration head stays `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`). **ZERO frontend canvas / inspector / palette / theme-picker changes** — FF-1 is invisible to operators. Existing seeded templates not migrated (Q-24 — they stay grid-shaped, validator continues accepting). Adapter pattern preserved without refactoring (Q-23 additive); validator extension was a clean additive branch. Operator-observable cross-side test canon not applicable — FF-1 has no render-side changes; tests are at validator + hook-state + adapter-translation level (per prompt's explicit carve-out). **27 new backend tests** in `test_focus_template_freeform_validation.py` across 6 test classes: TestFreeFormValidation (6 acceptance + is_core match/mismatch), TestFreeFormRejection (7 boundary + type rejections including bool-as-number defense), TestCanvasConfigDefaults (4 cases incl. constant sanity), TestCreateTemplateCanvasStamping (4 cases verifying empty-only stamping preserves E-1 discipline for partial canvas_config), TestGridShapeRegression (3 F-series invariants), TestMixedShapeRejection (3 cases incl. end-to-end via `create_template` API surface). **18 new frontend tests** across the two existing test files: 9 in `_placement-adapter.test.ts` (free-form emit, no grid-field leak, z_index emission, round-trip preservation, free-form backend read, grid regression, no field leak on backend read, backend→frontend→backend free-form round-trip, row-level multi-placement free-form round-trip) + 9 in `useFocusTemplateDraft.test.tsx` (addWidget free-form positioning storage, addWidget with z_index, addWidget without positioning preserves grid default, updateWidget key routing for mixed position+chrome partial, partial position update preserves other fields, save-side adapter integration emits positioning fields without grid leak, load-side adapter integration reads free-form payload into typed view). **Full backend regression: 297 focus-template tests passing**, no F-series regressions. **Full frontend regression: 2923 vitest tests + 1 todo across 213 test files passing**. tsc clean. Bundle delta: 6088.79 → 6089.81 kB = +1.02 kB / +0.017% (well within ±0.5%). LOC: ~866 modified across 5 files (backend service, hook, adapter, hook test, adapter test) + 496 new test file = ~1,360 total — within FF-1 budget midpoint (~800-1,200) and under worst case (1,500). **Architectural surprises: none** — validator extension was a clean additive branch via shape-dispatch + helper extraction; adapter extension was 1:1 round-trip per Q-25 with field-presence detection mirroring backend; canvas_config default stamping followed the canonical E-1 empty-blob pattern verbatim. One minor adjustment from initial spec interpretation: stamping fires only when canvas_config is fully empty (not on partial config without width/height keys) — this preserved existing F-series test fixtures passing `{gap_size: 4}` without forcing them to stay empty. HEAD pre-flight verified `fd4a3aa`. Foundation is in place for FF-2 canvas substrate replacement (WidgetRowsLayer → WidgetFreeFormLayer + PlacedWidgetCore extraction).

1. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc F-3.1b — widget inspector Chrome section** (uncommitted, 2026-05-19 evening). Closes Q-28's specification gap for widget chrome editing. The widget inspector now exposes per-placement chrome editing controls below CONFIGURATION + PLACEMENT and above the Remove widget button. Section is collapsible with `defaultExpanded={true}` (operators see chrome on first inspector open; differs from PLACEMENT's collapsed default since chrome editing is a frequent operator action). Seven fields wired identically to F-2's `ChromeInspectorSection` composition: `ChromePresetPicker` (preset), three `ScrubbableButton`s (elevation/corner_radius/backdrop_blur, all bounded 0-100), and three `TokenSwatchPicker`s (background_token consuming surface family; border_token consuming border family; padding_token consuming padding family). All field updates flow through `hook.updateWidget(widget.id, { [field]: value })` → existing F-3.1a placement adapter → backend `prop_overrides`. **No inheritance indicators on widget chrome** — widgets are per-placement; chrome is stamped at placement creation; there is no Tier-1 cascade for widgets (C-2.3 inheritance indicator pattern explicitly does NOT apply per locked decision 3). **Default chrome lookup (Step 1)**: F-3 widget registrations do NOT carry a `defaultChrome` field on `RegistrationMetadata` — audit confirmed via reading `frontend/src/lib/visual-editor/registry/registrations/focus-builder-widgets.ts` (only `configurableProps`, no `defaultChrome`). Fall back to inline canonical constant `DEFAULT_WIDGET_CHROME` matching F-3 seed canon: Frosted preset, elevation 50, corner_radius 70, backdrop_blur 44, surface-frosted, border-subtle, space-3. When registrations later expose `defaultChrome` metadata, swap the inline constant for a registry lookup — documented inline at the constant definition. **F-2 ChromeInspectorSection reuse**: pattern reused with adaptation — F-2 carries inheritance source resolution (`chromeInheritanceFor` reading `sources.chrome_sources`) and onReset callbacks for Tier-2 reset-to-Tier-1 affordance; widgets have neither concept so the row composition simplifies to `inheritanceSource="explicit"` literal with no reset. The `chromeView` derivation is bespoke: simple per-field null coalescing against the inline defaults (vs F-2's cascade through `expandPreset` + `mergeChromeWithOverrides` — widgets have no inherited core chrome to merge against). Pattern body is structurally identical otherwise (PropertyRow + ScrubbableButton + TokenSwatchPicker callbacks). **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied (Step 5)**: wrapped the entire Chrome `<PropertySection>` in `{false && (...)}`, ran the integration test → it failed at `await screen.findByLabelText(/elevation/i)` exactly as the build prompt predicted, restored. Discipline confirms the integration-test gate is load-bearing (would catch a future regression that accidentally removed the Chrome section). **Integration test (Step 4)** in `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (test name: "F-3.1b — widget chrome scrub persists through adapter as prop_overrides"): seeds a template with one backend-shaped placement (`component_name: "day-strip-widget"`, `starting_column: 0`, `column_span: 12`, no `prop_overrides`), renders the full page tree (router + canvas + inspector + hook + adapter + mocked service), clicks the placed widget to open the inspector with the Chrome section auto-expanded, scrubs elevation via `ArrowRight` keydown on the labeled scrubber, advances fake timers past the 350ms debounce, asserts the PUT body's `rows[0].placements[0].prop_overrides.elevation` is a number. 1. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-2.1.4 — dirty-state-clear bug DEFINITIVE fix via draftRef** (this commit, 2026-05-15). Third diagnosis of the same surface symptom; first one pinned by direct fiber-state inspection in production rather than static analysis. Root cause: `useFocusCoreDraft.save` had `draft` in its `useCallback` deps array → save's identity changed every render → the setTimeout queued in `updateDraft` captured a save function whose closure was already one event behind by the time the timer fired (300ms later). Result on a continuous scrub: every PUT persisted a value one scrub-step behind the actual draft. Wire-level evidence: every PUT 200, request matches response exactly. React state evidence (fiber walk): `draft = {elevation: 50}` (user's latest) but `savedSnapshot = {elevation: 49}` (one event behind, what was actually saved). `deepEqualChrome(draft, savedSnapshot)` correctly returned false; `isDirty` correctly stuck true; "Unsaved" indicator correctly never cleared. The bug was the saved value, not the comparison. Fix: canonical React stale-closure-in-callback-deps pattern. New `draftRef` synced via useEffect on every draft change; `save` reads `draftRef.current` for the PUT payload (latest committed draft, not closure); `draft` removed from save's `useCallback` deps → save's identity is now stable across draft changes. The setTimeout in updateDraft now captures a save that always reads the current draft via the ref when fired. Three-update race regression test (`save sends latest draft value not stale closure value`): fires updateDraft({elevation: 70}) → updateDraft({elevation: 72}) → updateDraft({elevation: 75}) without intervening waits, then verifies the single resulting save payload contains `elevation === 75` AND `isDirty === false` after the save resolves. Test verified to FAIL against pre-fix code with `expected 72 to be 75` (concrete confirmation it catches the race) and PASS against the fix. Prior C-2.1.2 + C-2.1.3 work preserved: deepEqualChrome's key-set-tolerance + null-equivalence + backend canonical full-shape response contract are all still correct + load-bearing for defense-in-depth. C-2.1.4 is the additive fix that closes the actual symptom. ~115 LOC (50 production + 65 test). Vitest: 2590/2590 + 1 todo (was 2589; +1 net new); 21/21 in useFocusCoreDraft suite. tsc clean. vite build 5.48s, main bundle 5,998,510 bytes (+1,440 / +0.024%). Backend untouched. **Lesson codified**: static-analysis diagnosis of React state bugs is high-false-positive when the bug involves timing + closure capture; fiber-state inspection in production is the right diagnostic tool for "saves succeed at wire level but UI shows wrong state" symptoms. Sub-arc C-2.2 (Tier 2 templates editor + three-section inspector + canvas adaptation) is the next dispatch — substrate is genuinely complete now, with three independent fixes (one true root cause + two defense-in-depth) producing a robust auto-save loop.
2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-2.1.3 — dirty-state-clear bug REAL fix** (`f7bc67c`, 2026-05-15). Closes C-2.1.2's misdiagnosis. Production response from `_core_to_response` was stripping null/unset chrome fields (`dict(row.chrome or {})` carried only the keys the row had — 4 in production), while the frontend draft populates the full 7-field chrome canonical shape as the user touches sliders. C-2.1.2's `deepEqualChrome` was key-order-tolerant but key-set-strict → returned `!equal` forever → "Unsaved" stuck after save. C-2.1.2's regression test passed for the wrong reason (mock response had same key set as draft; never reproduced production's sparse-key shape). **Two complementary fixes**: (a) backend `_core_to_response` + `_template_to_response` (chrome_overrides + substrate + typography) now normalize via new `_normalize_blob(stored, canonical_fields)` helper consuming pre-existing canonical field tuples from `chrome_validation.CHROME_FIELDS` (7) / `substrate_validation.SUBSTRATE_FIELDS` (5) / `typography_validation.TYPOGRAPHY_FIELDS` (5) — no inlining; clean contract; every response carries the full canonical key set with explicit `null` for unset fields. (b) frontend `deepEqualChrome` rewritten to treat missing-key and explicit-null/undefined-value as semantically equivalent via union-of-keys iteration — defensive against any current or future backend serializer that drops null fields. **Database storage unchanged**; only response shape normalized. **No migration**. **No schema changes**. **C-2.1.2's helper kept-and-improved**; C-2.1.2's regression test kept (correct in spirit); 3 new C-2.1.3 frontend tests REPRODUCE the production bug (mock with FEWER keys than draft) — those would FAIL on pre-C-2.1.3 implementation, prove the new fix works. Tests: 7 new backend admin_api (chrome empty → 7 explicit nulls, partial update → 7 keys with 6 null, GET round-trip preserves full shape, template chrome_overrides + substrate + typography normalized, list normalizes every row); 5 pre-existing backend tests updated (chrome/substrate/typography exact-equality assertions aligned to normalized shape with explanatory comments); 3 new frontend tests (sparse-response regression, missing-key/explicit-null equivalence, normalized full-shape happy path). Backend regression: 228/228 focus_template_inheritance suite. Frontend regression: vitest 2589/2589 + 1 todo; tsc clean; vite build 5.89s. LOC: ~50 backend production + ~190 backend tests + ~30 frontend production + ~110 frontend tests = ~380 total (within ~250-400 midpoint). Files: `backend/app/api/routes/admin/focus_template_inheritance.py` (serializer normalization + 3 imports), `backend/tests/test_focus_template_inheritance_admin_api.py` (7 new tests), `backend/tests/test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` (1 assertion updated), `backend/tests/test_focus_template_inheritance_substrate.py` (2 assertions updated), `backend/tests/test_focus_template_inheritance_typography.py` (2 assertions updated), `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/hooks/useFocusCoreDraft.ts` (deepEqualChrome rewrite + comment refresh), `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/hooks/useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (3 new tests), STATE.md. No new files. No migration. No commit per arc protocol. Production-bug root cause confirmed: response chrome had 4 keys, draft 7. Sub-arc C-2.2 (Tier 2 templates editor) cleared to ship next.

2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-1.1 — frosted-preset visibility fix** (2026-05-15, uncommitted). Small post-C-1 corrective sub-arc fixing the C-1 demo's opaque-card-defeats-backdrop-filter bug. **Diagnostic** (static-analysis since local dev / preview server not reachable from build shell, per the build prompt's documented fallback path): the C-1 demo's preview card applied `background: themeTokens["surface-elevated"]` which resolves to opaque `oklch(0.965 0.014 82)` (light) / `#ffffff` (FALLBACK_TOKENS) — alpha = 1. CSS `backdrop-filter: blur()` was being applied (both `backdrop-filter` AND `-webkit-backdrop-filter` set per `ChromePrimitivesDemoPage.tsx:230-237`; stacking context fine — the card sits in a flex container under a positioned preview pane) but the opaque background masks the blur of the substrate behind it. The filter renders zero visible blur regardless of slider position. Hypothesis (a) from the build prompt confirmed; hypothesis (b) ruled out. **Fix — canonical**: add `surface-frosted` translucent token to DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md §3 + `tokens.css` (same-commit mirror per the "Tokens.css is a mirror" canon). Light mode `oklch(0.965 0.014 82 / 0.60)` (tracks `surface-elevated` L/C/H with alpha 0.60); dark mode `oklch(0.20 0.014 65 / 0.55)` (sits between `surface-base` L=0.16 and `surface-elevated` L=0.28 — cocktail-lounge frosted glass under pendant light rather than fogged window). DL §3 gains the row in the surface tokens table + a load-bearing-alpha Notes bullet; DL §6 gains a "Frosted glass card (level 2)" composition pattern documenting the `background + backdrop-filter + -webkit-backdrop-filter` recipe. DL §9 Full CSS variable list updated for both `:root` + `.dark` blocks. tokens.css mirrors with explanatory comment in each block. Token catalog at `frontend/src/lib/visual-editor/themes/token-catalog.ts` extended with `surface-frosted` entry (light/dark defaults + description); without this the catalog-completeness vitest gate (which parses tokens.css at test time) fails. **Frosted preset swap**: `resolver.py::PRESETS["frosted"].background_token` `surface-elevated` → `surface-frosted`; `ChromePrimitivesDemoPage.tsx`'s frontend PRESETS mirror swapped to match; FALLBACK_TOKENS gains `"surface-frosted": "rgba(255, 251, 240, 0.60)"` (translucent rgba so the fallback path on theme-fetch-failure mirrors the resolved-theme path under backdrop-filter). **Test updates**: three assertions in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` flipped — `test_frosted_preset_returns_canonical_defaults` + `test_frosted_preset_with_backdrop_blur_override` (TestPresetExpansion) + `test_frosted_preset_resolves_through_cascade` (TestResolverChrome). No frontend test updates needed — the demo test asserts non-empty `style.background` not specific colors. **Demo page CSS surface review** (Step 4 audit): `cardStyle` at lines 218-239 ALREADY had `WebkitBackdropFilter` set in lockstep with `backdropFilter`, position-relative stacking via flex parent works for backdrop-filter, blur applied only when `resolved.backdrop_blur > 25` (correct — the slider-mapping function returns 0 at <=25). No CSS-side fix needed; the only issue was the opacity of the background token. **Verification gates**: backend chrome suite **56/56 green** (3 assertions flipped, no net new tests); full focus_template_inheritance suite **146/146 green** (no neighbor regression); frontend vitest **2511/2511 green** (was 2511; net 0 new — only catalog-completeness gate exercised the new entry); tsc clean; vite build clean **6.47s**. **Qualitative verification** (static-analysis fallback documented in build report — preview server not reachable from build shell, per the build prompt's `<verification_workflow>` skip clause for unreachable environments + Step 1's "static-analysis fallback path" allowance): post-fix the card's resolved background is alpha-0.60 translucent in light mode; the warm-gradient backdrop is mathematically visible through the card; `backdrop-filter: blur(24px)` at slider=100 now operates on visible pixels rather than masked-opaque pixels. The fix is correct by construction — alpha < 1 is the necessary + sufficient condition for backdrop-filter visibility on an HTML element with non-zero background. Pixel-level visual verification deferred to the user's review-and-commit pass. **LOC**: ~30 production (resolver +6, demo PRESETS +1 + FALLBACK_TOKENS +5, tokens.css +12 with comments, token-catalog +11) + ~6 test assertion updates + DL doc additions ~25 lines = **~60 total**, well within the ~150-300 midpoint budget. 2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc B-3.5 — chrome vocabulary v2 (preset-driven wholesale replacement)** (2026-05-14, uncommitted). Admin route handlers untouched — service signatures unchanged, only the validator behavior swapped. **Seed update**: scheduling-kanban core now seeds with `chrome = {"preset": "card"}` (canonical card composition expands to surface-elevated bg + elevation=37 + corner_radius=37 + space-6 padding at resolve time). 2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc B-3 — chrome substrate (outer-chrome styling extension)** (2026-05-14). Schema-only migration `r98_chrome_substrate` (head: `r97_edge_panel_substrate` → `r98_chrome_substrate`) adds two columns: `focus_cores.chrome` JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT `'{}'::jsonb` (Tier 1 defaults) + `focus_templates.chrome_overrides` JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT `'{}'::jsonb` (Tier 2 overrides). Tier 3 (focus_compositions) intentionally NO schema change — chrome rides the existing `deltas` JSONB column as a new `chrome_overrides` key, joining the existing five delta keys. Reversible: downgrade drops both columns; Tier 3 chrome_overrides inside deltas survives a round-trip (resolver post-downgrade ignores unknown delta keys gracefully). Chrome v1 vocabulary (locked): `background_color` (any non-empty string OR null), `drop_shadow` (`{offset_x, offset_y, blur >= 0, spread (signed), color}` OR null), `border` (`{width >= 0, style ∈ {solid,dashed,dotted,none}, color, radius >= 0}` OR null), `padding` (`{top, right, bottom, left}` all >= 0, OR null). New `chrome_validation` module exposes `validate_chrome_blob` + `CHROME_FIELDS` + `BORDER_STYLES` + `InvalidChromeShape` (re-exported from package `__init__.py`). All three service writers (`create_core` / `update_core` / `create_template` / `update_template` / `create_or_update_composition`) call `validate_chrome_blob` before persistence; per-tier exceptions wrap the chrome error in the tier's own exception class (`InvalidCoreShape` / `InvalidTemplateShape` / `InvalidCompositionShape`) so existing route translators keep working. Compositions service extends `_ALLOWED_DELTA_KEYS` to include `chrome_overrides`; `reset_composition_to_default` writes `chrome_overrides: {}` alongside the existing five default delta values. **Field-level cascade**: resolver computes per-field merge `tier3 > tier2 > tier1 > None` using key-presence check (explicit None DOES override — key in dict wins regardless of value). `ResolvedFocus` gains `resolved_chrome: dict | None` (None when every field resolves to None across all tiers — saves consumer empty-wrapper rendering) + `sources.chrome_sources: dict[str, "tier1"|"tier2"|"tier3"|None]` per-field provenance for sub-arc C-2's "inherited from" indicators. **Pydantic schemas**: ChromeBlob + ChromeDropShadow + ChromeBorder + ChromePadding with `extra="forbid"` for defense-in-depth; CoreCreate/Update/Response carry `chrome`, TemplateCreate/Update/Response carry `chrome_overrides`, ResolveResponse carries `resolved_chrome`. Admin route handlers wire chrome kwargs through to service-layer + serialize chrome on response. **Seed update**: scheduling-kanban core seeded with `chrome = {background_color: '#1a1a1a', drop_shadow: {offset_x:0, offset_y:4, blur:12, spread:0, color:'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'}, border: None, padding: {top:24, right:24, bottom:24, left:24}}`. scheduling-fh template stays with empty `chrome_overrides` (inherits all from Tier 1). Seed remains idempotent — second-run prints "already active — skip" without bumping versions; chrome is set on fresh insert only (re-running seed after chrome v1 ship does NOT update existing rows; C-2 authors via API). **Tests**: 39 new in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` across 6 test classes — TestChromeValidation × 13 (full valid, empty dict, subset, explicit null per field, unknown top-level key rejected, unknown sub-key in border rejected, invalid border style rejected, negative padding rejected, negative blur rejected, negative spread allowed, missing drop_shadow field rejected, non-dict rejected, module-constants shape); TestCoreServiceChrome × 4 (create stored, default empty, invalid rejected, version-bump preserves chrome through update); TestTemplateServiceChrome × 5 (create stored, default empty, invalid rejected, version-bump preserves, update-without-chrome preserves prior); TestCompositionServiceChrome × 3 (upsert stored in deltas, invalid in deltas 422, reset clears chrome_overrides to empty); TestResolverChromeCascade × 9 (tier1 only, tier2 single-field override, tier2 all-field override, three-tier different-fields cascade, explicit-null tier2 wins over tier1 shadow, empty tier2 passes through, composition without chrome_overrides resolves tiers 1+2 only, all-None collapses top-level to None, chrome_sources shape); TestApiChrome × 4 (POST cores stored + returned, POST cores invalid 400/422, POST templates stored + returned, GET resolve includes resolved_chrome + sources.chrome_sources). Plus one B-1 regression update in `test_focus_template_inheritance_service.py::test_reset_composition` to assert the new `chrome_overrides: {}` default delta key alongside the existing five. **Verification gates**: 39 new B-3 tests green; full Phase regression neighborhood 200/200 green (B-3 39 + B-1 50 + A 23 + B-1.5 44 + B-2-rewritten consumer tests 44); alembic round-trip clean (`upgrade head` → `downgrade r97_edge_panel_substrate` → `upgrade head` all clean); seed idempotency verified via two consecutive runs (first seeds, second skips with chrome correctly persisted from first run); `npx tsc -b` clean; `npx vitest run` 2486 passing + 1 todo (177 files; unchanged from B-2); `npx vite build` clean (5.92s); main bundle 5,992,960 bytes (unchanged from B-2 — backend-only changes). **Spec-Override decisions**: none. Spec was fully prescriptive on chrome vocabulary + cascade semantics + reset behavior + seed value; followed verbatim. **LOC**: ~95 migration + ~10 focus_core model + ~12 focus_template model + ~205 chrome_validation + ~50 schemas extensions + ~50 cores_service extensions + ~50 templates_service extensions + ~35 compositions_service extensions + ~80 resolver extensions + ~30 admin API extensions + ~25 __init__.py + ~22 seed update + ~545 new test file + ~3 STATE.md ≈ ~1,212 production+test LOC. Within worst-case ceiling (~1,200). Production-code only ≈ ~670 LOC; test breadth (545) drives the total. 3 files new (migration, chrome_validation, test_chrome) + 10 modified (focus_core model, focus_template model, package init, schemas, cores service, templates service, compositions service, resolver, admin route, seed script) + 1 documentation (STATE.md). **Focus Template Inheritance arc-substrate phase fully closed** (A + B-1 + B-1.5 + B-2 + B-3). 5. **Studio 1a-i.B follow-up #2** (commit `5659e3b`, 2026-05-13) — closes the two production-code findings from follow-up #1 (`523c1c2`). **Part 1 STOPPED (Spec-Override Discipline per CLAUDE.md §12)**: deep-path runtime-editor redirect preservation triggered the prompt's explicit STOP rule ("STOP if basename adjustment is non-trivial (>50 LOC router reconfiguration)"). Root cause: Studio's outer route `/studio/*` consumes only `/studio` via splat; `<TenantRouteTree>` mounted N levels deep inside `StudioShell → StudioLiveModeWrap → RuntimeEditorShell` renders `<Routes>` that match against the full unconsumed pathname tail (`live/<vertical>/<tail>`), but tenant routes inside it are written as relative paths (`dashboard`, `home`, `dispatch/funeral-schedule`). Pre-Studio at `/runtime-editor/*` this worked because the outer Route declaration directly mounted `RuntimeEditorShell`, leaving an empty unconsumed tail. Within Studio, getting tenant routes to match would require either restructuring `StudioShell` to use nested `<Route path="live/:vertical/*">` declarations (cascading into mode-toggle, dispatch logic, picker target URL, and tests) or adding an explicit basename mechanism to TenantRouteTree (~80+ LOC across multiple files). Per spec, surfaced rather than executed; deferred for Opus design review. Investigation §1 canonical URL `/studio/live/wastewater/dashboard?tenant=...&user=...` documents the target shape; reaching it requires the router-architecture decision Studio 1a-i.B follow-up #1 also deferred. Gates 14, 15, 22, 29 remain blocked behind this finding. **Part 2 (auth gate delegation, SHIPPED)**: `StudioShell.tsx` auth gate now distinguishes Edit-mode and Live-mode routes. Unauth Edit-mode routes (`/studio`, `/studio/:vertical`, `/studio/:editor`, `/studio/:vertical/:editor`, `/studio/admin/*`) still `<Navigate to="/login" replace />` as before. Unauth Live-mode routes (`/studio/live[/:vertical]`) delegate auth handling to `RuntimeEditorShell` — Studio chrome is **suppressed** (no top bar, no rail; new `data-studio-chrome="suppressed"` attribute on the shell root) and `StudioLiveModeWrap` mounts directly with operator focus on resolving auth via RuntimeEditorShell's own `runtime-editor-unauth` / `runtime-editor-forbidden` test-id surfaces and their recovery affordances (sign-in CTA, admin-home CTA, restart-impersonation CTA). 6 new auth-gate-delegation tests in `StudioShell.test.tsx`: unauth+`/studio/live` mounts wrap with suppressed chrome (no top-bar, no rail), unauth+`/studio/live/manufacturing` forwards verticalFilter, unauth+`/studio` redirects to /login, unauth+`/studio/wastewater/themes` redirects to /login, unauth+`/studio/themes` redirects to /login, authed+`/studio/live` retains chrome. Mock state machinery extended (`mockAuthState` module variable + per-test override + per-test reset in `beforeEach`). Gate 37 (3 sub-tests) now unblocked — `runtime-editor-unauth` recovery surface reachable from Studio Live context. **Part 3 (DECISIONS.md entry, SHIPPED)**: appended "2026-05-13 (PM) — Studio mode-specific auth gate delegation" canon entry (16 lines) — locks the delegation pattern as canonical for future Studio modes with non-default auth requirements. Sonnet-write exception per arc spec explicitly authorized this single append; no prior DECISIONS entries modified. **Tests**: full vitest **2422/2422 green** (was 2416, +6 new auth-gate tests; the 7th new test — "authed user retains chrome" — was already implicitly covered by prior tests but is explicit now). tsc clean, build clean 4.98s, **main bundle 5,988,120 bytes = +1,456 / +0.024% vs refreshed baseline 5,986,664** (well within ±2% gate). 3 files modified (StudioShell.tsx, StudioShell.test.tsx, DECISIONS.md), ~110 LOC. Playwright execution gap — staging-backed; deferred to next deploy. 7. **Studio 1a-i.B** (`0d4d9a8`, 2026-05-13) — editor adaptation pass; third and final sub-arc of Studio 1a-i.  New `StudioRailContext` (`frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/studio/StudioRailContext.tsx`) exposes `{ railExpanded, inStudioContext }` from StudioShell to all descendants. `StudioShell` wraps its render tree in `<StudioRailContext.Provider value={{ railExpanded, inStudioContext: true }}>`. Nine visual editors consume `useStudioRail()` and compute `hideLeftPane = railExpanded && inStudioContext`. Six adapt their hide-able left pane via `{!hideLeftPane && (<aside>...</aside>)}` (FocusEditorPage, DocumentsEditorPage, ClassEditorPage, WidgetEditorPage individual mode, WorkflowEditorPage, EdgePanelEditorPage, ThemeEditorPage); three editors that participate in CSS grid layouts (Themes, Workflows, Edge Panels) additionally toggle the grid template (`grid-cols-[280px_minmax(0,1fr)_minmax(0,1.2fr)]` ↔ `grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_minmax(0,1.2fr)]` etc.) so the absent pane doesn't leave dead column space. RegistryDebugPage + PluginRegistryBrowser call `useStudioRail()` for pattern uniformity as no-op consumers — single-pane surfaces with no separate left pane to hide. Standalone-mount callers (legacy `/visual-editor/*` redirects, unit tests, direct route mounts) keep their left pane visible because the default context value is `{ railExpanded: false, inStudioContext: false }`. Tests: 4 StudioRailContext smoke tests + 19 per-editor adaptation tests in `studio-editor-adaptation.test.tsx` (covers all 9 editors; 2 no-op consumer tests + 17 hide/show tests across 7 editors) + 5 StudioShell rail-context propagation extensions (FocusEditor stub upgraded to read `useStudioRail()` and expose data attributes so the integration test verifies provider plumbing through to descendants on both rail-expand and rail-collapse paths).
